## JMP-01 观星者们 / The Stargazers

**？？？**：……关于类星体，我们有以下假设……\
**???**: Hypotheses have been made regarding the quasars as follows ...

会场内座无虚席。\
The hall was packed with audience members.

呼——\
*exhales*

讲台下方的黑暗翻涌着。那些质询的，审视的，或许在镜片后的目光滑出了黑暗。\
The darkness below the podium is boiling. The eyes with questions and inspection, some behind glasses, are cast out of the darkness.

仿佛我们曾在塔顶观测到的，那些几光年外的讯号。\
Just like the signals beamed from several light years away and received at the top of the observatory.

**？？？**：……很好。\
**???**: Good.

**？？？**：根据光谱红移，施密特博士初步推算它的退行速度可达到光速的六分之一……\
**???**: Based on the data of its redshift, Dr. Schmidt deduced that it is moving away from us at a recessional velocity of 1/6 of light speed.

第三页……第三页我记得我放在……\
Page 3, mmm, I did put it in ...

**？？？**：……通常，我们认为恒星黑洞是恒星坍塌后的遗骸。\
**???**: In most cases, we would consider a stellar black hole as what is left from the gravitational collapse of a star.

红色的粉笔在黑板上的圆圈周边留下了一圈嶙峋的痕迹。\
The red chalk left a jaggy circle in one stroke on the blackboard.

**？？？**：它们相互斗争、吸引、融合，最终成为超大质量黑洞——也是其周围星系内恒星的最后归宿……\
**???**: They fight, attract each other, and merge into a supermassive black hole to which the stars in the nearby galaxies will be eventually pulled by gravity ...

啊，第三页在这儿。是库玛尔给我调整的位置吗？\
Page 3, oh, here it is. Did Kumar put it here for me?

“于那时日，混沌中空无一物。存在者与非存在者皆无，无至上之域，无大气，无天穹。”\
"Then there was neither existence nor non-existence; there was neither the realm of space nor the sky beyond."

**？？？**：“无死无生，无昼无夜。”\
**???**: "Then there was neither death nor immortality; there was neither day nor night."

**？？？**：类星体之中……正发生着一场近似于超新星爆发的剧烈活动。\
**???**: Inside the quasars, there is a violent activity occurring that is close to a supernova.

**？？？**：它吞噬恒星……\
**???**: It devours stars ...

**？？？**：其生成的气体云在引力作用下又将重新耦合——\
**???**: And the gas cloud turns into stars out of gravitational driving.

**？？？**：诞生出新的恒星。\
**???**: Thus, a new star is born.

**？？？**：它是由恒星的尸骸融成的墓茔。\
**???**: It is a graveyard filled with corpses.

**？？？**：——却亦是恒星诞生的摇篮。\
**???**: As well as a cradle for new stars.

风，草地，新鲜的空气，这里是个并不隐秘的好去处。\
The evening breeze, the meadow, and the fresh air. Despite its lack of privacy, this was as good a place to chill as it could be.

今日的夜空格外的晴朗，群星闪烁，清晰可辨。\
It was a clear night. Stars twinkled in the sky like golden sprinkles on a dark cloth.

**？？？**：成功的演讲，伽菈波那。\
**???**: That was a successful lecture, Kaalaa Baunaa.

熟悉的声音与步伐节奏，无需回头，脑海便能浮现出那抹身影。\
Kaalaa Baunaa heard a familiar voice and recognized the footsteps. Without looking back, she already knew who was behind her.

**伽菈波那**：感谢你难得的夸奖。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Thanks for your rare compliment.

她伸出手去，仿佛能碰到繁星。\
She extended her arm, reaching out for the stars.

**伽菈波那**：没想到你离开这么长的时间，回来第一件事就是亲自来看我出糗……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I can't believe the first thing you do after the long absence is listening to my embarrassing speech.

**伽菈波那**：你知道，我并不擅长这些……我现在仍认为自己在第三部分的一处用词不够精准。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: You see, this is not my thing. I'm still struggling with a word I should use in Part 3.

**？？？**：哦，但你也知道，我无法抗拒这样美妙的观众席——\
**???**: Oh, but you know I won't pass up a good chance to sit in the audience ...

身侧草丛窸窣作响——有人并排躺了下来。\
The grass rustled. She lay down next to Kaalaa Baunaa.

**？？？**：既能与讲台上的瞩目者心照不宣，又能清晰地感受周围的窃窃私语……\
**???**: ... to be someone who can smile knowingly at the argument made by the lecturer, knowing full well the thinking process behind, while staying close to other whispering opinions.

**？？？**：置身事内的绝佳观景位，正如同我们在这个星球上去观测宇宙里的一切！\
**???**: This is the perfect spot for observations, like a perfect observatory from which we witness the events in the universe!

**伽菈波那**：唉。比起评判你的个人趣味……库玛尔，我认为之后的观测仍需要做一些细节上的调整——\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I'd rather not give a comment on your personal taste. Kumar, I think we should make some adjustments to the details of the following observation.

**库玛尔**：我有个建议——这会儿放下工作如何？就好好儿地、单纯地看看这些星星……往那边躺躺，这草怎么像松针似的扎人……\
**Kumar**: Here's an idea. How about we put away the work for the moment? Forget those things. Just look at the stars. Simply fix your eyes on them. Ah, move over. The grass beneath me feels like pine needles.

**伽菈波那**：……在你离开的这几个月里，研究所的达恩曾来过。看他的态度，似乎已经对我的人类身份起了疑心。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: When you were away, Daane from the institution had paid a visit here. Based on his attitude, I may tell he was doubting my identity as a human.

**库玛尔**：……\
**Kumar**: ...

**伽菈波那**：这样下去我们很有可能被踢出这个原本属于我们自己的项目……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: If it goes on like this, we are likely to be kicked out of our own project.

**伽菈波那**：关于那个特殊天体的观测资料我已经全部销毁了……至少这样可以暂时确保观测方式只有咱们两人掌握。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I've destroyed all the observation data of that special celestial body. At least through this, we can keep the observation method between you and me.

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

长久的沉默。伽菈波那微微侧头望向身侧。\
Her words were only met with a lasting silence. Kaalaa Baunaa turned to the person next to her.

**伽菈波那**：看你的表情……我做错了什么吗？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: You seem ... Have I done anything wrong?

**库玛尔**：不，以研究项目的角度来说，你做得很好——不过我对此早有预料。\
**Kumar**: No. As a research student, you did an excellent job, though no more than I'd expect from a student of mine.

她的声音出奇地平静。\
Her voice was incredibly calm.

**库玛尔**：我们不总是这样？偷偷摸摸、躲躲藏藏，做一些——完全与世无争的研究。\
**Kumar**: That's just what we've been doing, isn't it? Hiding in the corners, doing research that completely has nothing to do with others.

**库玛尔**：……你知道吗？我真的有些厌烦了，厌烦这些“星际尘土”之间的无聊斗争，明明死了之后都会变为这个偌大宇宙的一部分……\
**Kumar**: You know what? I'm a bit tired, seriously, tired of the pointless power struggles between these specks of "stardust." We all know none of us could avoid the fate of being restored to the basic elements of the universe after we die.

她深深叹了口气。\
She sighed deeply at the thought.

**库玛尔**：……算了，这又不是第一次。反正我无论在哪边都不受欢迎。\
**Kumar**: Never mind. It's not the first time it's happened. I've never been welcomed on either side.

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

**库玛尔**：嘁，说起这个……\
**Kumar**: Ah, speaking of which ...

她显然因为这个话题被勾起了更不好的回忆。\
Hooked by the conversation, unpleasant memories swam up again.

**库玛尔**：我那对父母——我和你说过的，那对因为我见鬼的薄弱神秘学家血统而抛弃我的父母……\
**Kumar**: My parents, yeah, I told you about them. They abandoned me because I had little so-called talent for arcanum.

**库玛尔**：如今……他们竟然感到对不起我！\
**Kumar**: And now, they are showing remorse for what they have done!

**库玛尔**：更离谱的是——我那个傻弟弟竟然一无所知……甚至没认出我是他姐姐！\
**Kumar**: There's more—my stupid younger brother knew nothing about what happened to me. He didn't even recognize me, his own sister!

**伽菈波那**：……你这次回乡见到他们了？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: You paid them a visit this time back in your hometown?

**库玛尔**：见？不，亲爱的，我是去——反正不是为了听人忏悔去的！我没在乎过那些。\
**Kumar**: Visit them? No, sweetheart, I went home to ... to do many things except to hear some old people's apology! I've never cared about those things.

**库玛尔**：我只是去处理些小事……而且很顺利。\
**Kumar**: I went there to deal with a little business, and it was done smoothly.

她似乎感到了安心。\
She seemed to be in a state of ease.

**库玛尔**：顺利到……我把我能做到的，都做到了。\
**Kumar**: So smoothly that I've taken care of everything there is to be done.

**伽菈波那**：……？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...?

**库玛尔**：伽菈波那，如果……\
**Kumar**: Kaalaa Baunaa, if ...

一阵风吹过草地。纤维细碎的摩擦音清晰地传入耳中。\
A gust of wind blew by the meadow. The subtle sound of plant fibers rubbing against each other could be heard clearly.

**库玛尔**：如果有一天，我们能亲眼看到那个天体，能触碰到它的话……我一定——\
**Kumar**: If one day, we can see that celestial body with our own eyes, or even touch it with our own hands, I will definitely ...

**伽菈波那**：库玛尔？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Kumar?

**伽菈波那**：你在说什……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: What are you talking ab- ...

女孩倏地支起身子，试图看清身旁的人。\
Kaalaa Baunaa propped herself up on both of her elbows, trying to see the one beside her clearly.

可对方的面容就像是隐藏在黑色的浓雾之后，令人无法辨认。\
But that person's face was indistinguishable, as if hidden in a thick black fog.

**库玛尔**：把他们*……&%……都*&*——！\
**Kumar**: I WILL DEFINITELY ...!

**伽菈波那**：库玛尔！\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: KUMAR!

**伽菈波那**：……！\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...!

## JMP-02 黄水晶灵摆 / Yellow Crystal Pendulum

**玛蒂尔达**：让我——\
**Matilda**: Excuse me.

**玛蒂尔达**：过——去——！\
**Matilda**: Let me get through!

**玛蒂尔达**：哦……让让，都给我让开……看在勒诺曼的面子上！\
**Matilda**: Ah! Will you move, please? For the sake of Marie Anne Lenormand!

站台上熙熙攘攘的人流像是忙碌的彩色沙丁鱼群，相互拥挤着，以极快的速度涌向各自的方向。\
The crowds on the platform are like schools of colorful sardines, pushing each other toward their destinations at an incredible speed.

**玛蒂尔达**：总算——痛痛，挤火车挤得脖子好痛啊。\
**Matilda**: Oh, finally! Ah-ah, ouch, this train ride gave me a real pain in the neck!

女孩卸了浑身的力气，瘫倒在车站为数不多的空座椅上。\
She finally gets to relax in one of the few empty seats in the station.

**玛蒂尔达**：这样凉爽的天气，如果能在我的小床上睡上一觉……或者干脆和妈妈一起留在德里，卖完那些黄水晶也好啊！\
**Matilda**: How nice it'd be if I were to sleep on my bed in such cool and comfortable weather! Or I may as well just stay in Delhi with Mom to sell those topazes!

**玛蒂尔达**：唉……\
**Matilda**: *sighs*

手掌不自觉地收紧，小小的动作让手中的资料发出了轻微的响动。\
Her fist tightens, though she doesn't consciously want to. The documents rattle in her hand.

她低下头去，看向手中的一叠纸张。\
She looks down at the documents.

**玛蒂尔达**：……\
**Matilda**: ...

**玛蒂尔达**：不行，玛蒂尔达绝对不会放弃！\
**Matilda**: No! Matilda will not just give up here!

**玛蒂尔达**：谁知道下次外出审批等到什么时候？\
**Matilda**: Who knows when they will approve my leave next time?

**玛蒂尔达**：难得观测到这么充沛的天体能量——距离这样近、这样刚好，简直是为我这样的占卜天才特意准备的……笨蛋才会让好机会溜走！\
**Matilda**: These days, the celestial energy appears to be ideally strong, and the best observation area happens to be close to Delhi. What a heaven-sent opportunity for this genius of divination! Only the fools will take no action!

**玛蒂尔达**：等着吧，等我找到那个冥想点修习了之后——\
**Matilda**: Wait and see. When I find the right place to meditate ...

女孩轻轻挥舞着拳头，像是下了什么了不起的决心一般。\
She slightly shakes her fist. It seems she has made up her mind very seriously.

**玛蒂尔达**：哼哼，第一的宝座早晚会回到我手里！\
**Matilda**: Hum-humph, sooner or later, I will take my ride back to the top!

她手上翻动着，凑近查看那些印刷模糊的文字。\
She rummages through the documents and moves close enough to read the poorly printed text.

**玛蒂尔达**：唔，让我看看，他们究竟发的是什么的宣传海报……烛星节？\
**Matilda**: Emm, let me see what this poster is about. Emm, Dīpa Festival?

手中的海报被翻了个面。\
She turns over the poster.

**玛蒂尔达**：“……而摩卢旁卡将每年的流星雨期定为烛星节，以祈求毗因陀神的护佑……”\
**Matilda**: "People in Mor Pankh hold the Dīpa Festival during the meteor shower period every year to seek the blessings of Vindre."

**玛蒂尔达**：哦，原来是与当地的流星周期相关！毗因陀……我记得我查到的资料里提到过这个名字……\
**Matilda**: Oh, so it's based on the meteor shower here! Vindre ... I think I have seen this name in the materials.

**玛蒂尔达**：我现在在……昌迪加尔东面……这里的景点标识也太少了吧？\
**Matilda**: Now I'm in the east of Chandigarh. Can there be fewer signs here?

**玛蒂尔达**：啊哈！地图背面有英语版！很好，如果有法语版的就更有品位了。\
**Matilda**: Ah-ha! This map has English on its back! Very nice. Would be more classy if they put French here instead.

**玛蒂尔达**：之前占卜出来的地方是——摩，摩卢……旁卡……是个神庙！是它的……北窟？\
**Matilda**: The place I found through divination is called Mor Pankh. It's a shrine! I need to go to its north cave?

**玛蒂尔达**：神庙……那或许与我调查到的那个彗星神话有些关系，最近这里是不是也要有流星雨来着？\
**Matilda**: Good. So, a shrine. Perhaps it has something to do with that comet myth I read about earlier. Isn't this also one of the places to see the upcoming meteor shower?

**玛蒂尔达**：好！目的地确定了。我的笔呢……在这里！很好，让我先标记一下……\
**Matilda**: Great! This is where I am going, then. Where's my pen? Ah, here! Very good, let me put it down.

女孩躬起身子，努力地在纸上标记着什么。\
She hunches over and writes down something carefully.

**玛蒂尔达**：呼！大功告成！新城真是方便多了……\
**Matilda**: Phew! Nicely done! Everything is a lot more convenient in the new town.

仰头望去，车站的天花板看起来像是才搭建了不久，光洁如新。\
The ceiling looks new. This train station seems to have been built not too long ago.

**玛蒂尔达**：德里的看上去甚至比这里还旧些。也不知爸爸妈妈在那边还顺利吗……那个印度大叔讲起价来语速真夸张……\
**Matilda**: Looks a lot better than the ceiling in Delhi's train station. I wonder how Mom and Dad are doing now. That Indian man can speak really fast when he's bargaining.

**玛蒂尔达**：唔……\
**Matilda**: Emm.

松懈下来的神经令疲惫缓缓攀上躯体。\
As she slackens off, tiredness catches up with her.

**玛蒂尔达**：唔……就休息一下……就一下……\
**Matilda**: Emm. Just one quick nap, very brief ...

**玛蒂尔达**：……Zzz……\
**Matilda**: ... Zzz ...

**？？？**：哇，真不错，够胆大的……\
**???**: Wow, cool! What a bold girl!

**？？？**：嘻嘻……\
**???**: Hee hee ...

**？？？**：大伙儿，看到了没？那个敢在火车站睡觉的家伙……\
**???**: Guys, you see that? The girl brave enough to sleep in the train station.

**阿贾尔**：呃……看不到哇，坎吉拉大姐！像你这样的好眼神能有几个——呃，好吧，谢谢你的望远镜……\
**Ajar**: Err, I see nothing, Boss! Not everyone has the great eyesight as yours. Oh, thank you. Nice monocular.

**阿贾尔**：哦哦，亮晶晶的宝石和钱包……\
**Ajar**: Oh, shiny jewels and wallet.

**阿贾尔**：可她怎么睡着了还能把手里那堆纸攥得那样紧？我记得车站门口的地图是免费的……\
**Ajar**: But what is the thing she is holding so tightly, even when she's asleep? Isn't that the map they give away at the train station for free?

**坎吉拉**：唔，没准儿是什么值钱的东西？像是那些书中插画里的藏宝图！要是能凑近一些……\
**Kanjira**: Hmm, something valuable, I guess? Like the treasure map pictures in the books! If I can take a closer look ...

**坎吉拉**：算了，那个对你来说难度有点大……阿贾尔，你从左边过去，就按我教你的那样去做，得手了就打这个手势……\
**Kanjira**: Well, that's too hard for you. Ajar, you go from left, just as I taught you. Give me this gesture after you get it.

**阿贾尔**：嘿嘿……没问题！\
**Ajar**: Heh-heh, no problem!

**坎吉拉**：好好干，小子！这单成功了，你就能顺利踏出第一步了！噢，记得，别告诉夏尔贾我教了你这些！\
**Kanjira**: Do it well, boy! If you make it, that would be your first step to victory! Oh, remember, don't tell Ms. Sherjah I taught you these!

**坎吉拉**：去吧，快去。别让其他的家伙抢了生意……\
**Kanjira**: Go, go! Don't let other people get it before you do.

**玛蒂尔达**：呃……嗯？\
**Matilda**: Umm ...?

**玛蒂尔达**：什么……晃来晃去的……？\
**Matilda**: What is it? Something swaying?

女孩儿迷迷糊糊地睁开眼，正看到一个鬼鬼祟祟，转身欲走的小小身影。\
Sleepily, Matilda struggles to open her eyes and sees a little figure prowling away.

**阿贾尔**：呃，咳咳……小姐，这是你的东西吗？\
**Ajar**: Emm, ahem! Is this yours, Miss?

**玛蒂尔达**：嗯？嘿，这是我妈妈给我的灵摆！你是……\
**Matilda**: Emm? Hey, that's the pendulum Mom gave me! Who are you?

**阿贾尔**：多亏我给你拾起来啦！喏，拿好了～\
**Ajar**: It fell on the floor. I was just picking it up for you! There, don't lose it again.

**玛蒂尔达**：哦！真是谢——\
**Matilda**: Oh! Thank you ...

玛蒂尔达伸出手，想要接过男孩掌心的灵摆。\
Matilda reaches for the pendulum.

**？？？**：可惜，谢得有点早啦，小姑娘。\
**???**: Nuh-uh. It's yet too early to say thanks, girl.

**玛蒂尔达**：嗯？\
**Matilda**: Hmm?

**鬃毛沙砾**：不知从哪里冒出来的巨大身影笼罩住了他们。\
**Shamane**: They find themselves in the shadow of a tall man.

**鬃毛沙砾**：男人看上去风尘仆仆，却没见他带着什么行李。\
**Shamane**: The man seems travel-worn, but he's carrying just a little luggage.

**？？？**：三分钟前？五分钟前？这小子在你身边儿打转的样子就像只鼬獾——总之相信我，这可不是什么友好的巧合。\
**???**: About three minutes ago? Or, five minutes ago? This fellow was wandering around you like a sneaky ferret-badger. Trust me. This is no friendly encounter.

他抬起左手，义肢看似僵硬的手指灵巧地夹着一枚精致的皮夹。\
He raises his left hand, more specifically, his prosthesis, to show the delicate wallet between those seemingly stiff fingers.

**玛蒂尔达**：嗯？这是我的——你这家伙，竟然偷了我钱夹？！\
**Matilda**: Umm? That's mine. You! You stole my wallet?!

**阿贾尔**：什……我明明放在裤子——\
**Ajar**: Wha, what? I've put it in my pocket.

**？？？**：看起来你的技术不太过关，小子。\
**???**: Someone needs to work on his techniques, right, boy?

这次是那只正常的手，他轻巧地向上一提，男孩便像个小鸡一般被男人拎在了手里。\
The man catches Ajar's clothes—this time with his real hand—and easily picks him up.

他抓得极有技巧，领子丝毫没碰到男孩脖子上的肌肤。\
Ajar is lifted in the air, but he isn't strangled with his collar, for the man has skillfully avoided the area of his neck.

**阿贾尔**：放手，别抓我衣服！可恶，怎么遇上个多管闲事的……\
**Ajar**: Let go! Let go of me! D**n it! Go mind your own business!

**？？？**：很不巧，多管闲事目前是我的主营业务。看样子你身上还有其他东西——走吧，有什么话到该说的地方去说。\
**???**: Unfortunate for you, my business these days is to mind others' business. Seems like there are more things in that pocket of yours. Come on, you know where we are going.

**阿贾尔**：讨厌！啊呜——\
**Ajar**: Ah! Urrrh!

男孩呲着两排牙齿，一口咬上了男人正拎着他领子的右手臂。\
Ajar shows his teeth and bites the man hard on the right hand, which is dragging his collar.

**？？？**：嘶——！\
**???**: Hiss—ah!

小贼挣开那只因吃痛而松懈的手，飞速地滑入了人群中，向远处跑去。\
He lets go because of the pain. The little thief breaks free and quickly slips into the crowd.

**玛蒂尔达**：他跑了——糟糕，我的灵摆还在他手上……给我站住！\
**Matilda**: He's gotten away. My, my, my pendulum! He had my pendulum. Stop! You!

**阿贾尔**：呼……呼……噢，该死的，他们快追上来了！\
**Ajar**: *pants* D**n it! They are catching up!

**玛蒂尔达**：赶快停下，你这个偷东西的坏家伙！\
**Matilda**: Stop right there, you little thief!

**阿贾尔**：哼！\
**Ajar**: Humph!

恼羞成怒的男孩把灵摆狠狠地向远处一抛。\
The annoyed boy throws the pendulum into the distance with full strength.

**？？？**：喂，你这小子……站住！\
**???**: Ah, you, boy! Wait!

男人紧随其后，与男孩一起没入了彩色沙丁鱼群中。\
The man runs into the colorful schools of sardines in hot pursuit.

**玛蒂尔达**：你——糟了，那个东西不能摔！\
**Matilda**: You! No! It's fragile. Don't!

剔透的水晶在半空中划过一条优美的弧线，如流星一般向地面坠去。\
In a beautiful arc, the transparent topaz falls toward the ground like a meteor.

**伽菈波那**：……！\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...!

——而突然出现的一只手掌稳稳接住了它。\
Suddenly, a palm appears and catches it safely.

**伽菈波那**：呼——刚刚好。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Phew. Just in time.

**伽菈波那**：这是你掉的东西吗？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Is this yours?

**玛蒂尔达**：啊，是的……\
**Matilda**: Ah, yes.

女人微微俯下身，声音轻柔。玛蒂尔达抬头望向看着她的双眸，一时间没反应过来发生了什么。\
The lady leans forward and speaks in a soft voice. Matilda stares into her eyes, completely abstracted.

**伽菈波那**：拿好了，孩子。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Put it away, kid.

她的手掌微微倾斜，黄水晶从她的掌心轻巧地滑落到了玛蒂尔达的手心中。\
As she tilts her palm, the topaz falls swiftly into Matilda's hand.

**玛蒂尔达**：谢谢……\
**Matilda**: Ah, thank you.

**伽菈波那**：举手之劳。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: It's okay.

女人微微颔首，像是一阵风一般转身离去。\
The lady slightly nods and leaves like a gust of wind.

**玛蒂尔达**：她走得好快……\
**Matilda**: She left so quickly.

**玛蒂尔达**：哎！得赶紧核对下手里的资料，别只顾着追小偷弄乱了……\
**Matilda**: Ah, the documents. Hope I didn't mess them up in the chase.

**玛蒂尔达**：一……二……嗯？怎么少了两张？掉到哪里去了……\
**Matilda**: One, two, emm? Two pages are missing. Where did they go?

不远处的柱子后面，一颗小小的黑色脑袋探了出来。\
A small, black-haird head is peeking from behind a pillar nearby.

**坎吉拉**：……还好我提前就规划好了逃跑路线——至少阿贾尔在跑路上不会输给任何人！\
**Kanjira**: Thankfully, I've planned my way out in advance. Well, at least Ajar won't be caught by anyone!

**坎吉拉**：祝你顺利，可怜的阿贾尔……\
**Kanjira**: Good luck running away, poor Ajar.

女孩双手合十，颇为惋惜地晃了晃脑袋。\
She puts her palms together and wobbles her head to show her pity.

**坎吉拉**：我会好好带着你的份再次赚回来的。哼，不过是个金色的小肥羊，看我怎么——\
**Kanjira**: I will make a profit from her, including the part you failed to make. Humph, that easy mark with milky blonde hair, you'll see how Kanjira ...

**坎吉拉**：哇！脚底下这是什么……！\
**Kanjira**: Whoa! What did I step on?

**坎吉拉**：这……这好像就是她看的那份？没错……我的眼睛绝不会出错……\
**Kanjira**: Is this the thing she was looking at? Yes, my eyes won't fail me.

女孩儿皱着小脸，仔仔细细地辨识着。\
Her face puckers up as she examines the paper in front of her.

**坎吉拉**：没想到这真是藏宝图！瞧这儿还标着星星呢，和书里说的一样……\
**Kanjira**: It really is a treasure map! Look here. She even drew a star, just like those pictures in books.

**坎吉拉**：这下可捡到好东西了，坎吉拉！\
**Kanjira**: You lucky girl, Kanjira. This is really something valuable!

**坎吉拉**：我瞧瞧，哦，看上去得按标注才能……可这旁边写的什么……嗯？她怎么把词都拼错了？英文字母上面怎么还有花纹……\
**Kanjira**: Let me see. Oh, I have to read it together with the handwritten notes. What are these, hmm? She spelled these all wrong! Even added some lines above them.

**玛蒂尔达**：——很遗憾，那是法语！\
**Matilda**: Don't even bother trying. It's in French!

**坎吉拉**：嘿！谁敢来抢我的藏宝——哦。\
**Kanjira**: Hey! Don't even think about taking my treasure, oh.

金发女孩眼睛微眯，打量着眼前眼神游离的可疑人员。\
Matilda squints to scan the suspect, who is trying to avoid eye contact.

**玛蒂尔达**：你拿着我的地图在这里鬼鬼祟祟地嘀咕什么呢？\
**Matilda**: What were you muttering about with my map?

**坎吉拉**：呃，咳咳——\
**Kanjira**: Emm, ahem.

**坎吉拉**：我，我这不是帮您捡起来，等着帮您呐！\
**Kanjira**: I, uh, just pick it up and look for its owner. Hope I can help!

**玛蒂尔达**：帮我？哼，玛蒂尔达可从不需要别人的帮助！更别提你这个不知道从哪儿来的——喂！你，你别碰我！\
**Matilda**: Help? Humph! Matilda needs no one's help! Not to mention from a girl who just showed up out of nowher- ... Hey! Don't ... don't touch me!

满脸堆笑的女孩全然无视了她语气里的不屑，甚至直接上前，亲昵地挽住了对方的胳膊。\
Kanjira ignores Matilda's contempt. She holds Matilda's arm intimately, with a big smile on her face.

**坎吉拉**：哇，那您好厉害啊～\
**Kanjira**: Wow, you is so cool!

**坎吉拉**：您第一次来的？自己来的？来做什么？观光？探亲？还是找某些——\
**Kanjira**: Is this your first time in the village? On your own? What's the plan? Sightseeing? Family visit? Or looking for some ...

**玛蒂尔达**：喂，你先放……你问这些做什么？\
**Matilda**: Hey! Let go first. Why's that any of your business?

**坎吉拉**：咳咳，是这样的……您可能不知道，我是一位非常有个人追求的……向导！\
**Kanjira**: Umm, aha, I mean, perhaps not clear to you, but in fact, I am a guide who always give best service!

**玛蒂尔达**：有追求的向导？\
**Matilda**: A guide? Who always gives the best service?

**坎吉拉**：哦，或者说是导游？总之，我敢说，没人能比我更熟悉这个村子……\
**Kanjira**: A tour guide, maybe? Anyways, I tell you, nobody know this village better than I!

**坎吉拉**：诶，您别这么看着我嘛，我在这儿闲逛是有原因的——我有个小小的个人习惯：我只愿意为那些厉害的，优秀的，有眼光的家伙服务～\
**Kanjira**: Hey, don't stare at me like this. I'm wandering here for a reason: I only give services to outstanding and cool people. They have good taste!

**坎吉拉**：所以我刚才一眼就注意到了您！我最伟大的服务对象！\
**Kanjira**: That why I find you at the station from all travelers! My most great, great customer ever!

**玛蒂尔达**：优秀的，有眼光的……哼，算你眼神好使。\
**Matilda**: Ah! The outstanding and impressive people, you say. Humph, at least you have sharp eyes.

玛蒂尔达努力控制着自己嘴角上扬的弧度。\
Matilda tries hard to suppress her complacent smile.

**坎吉拉**：您看，您选择的这个位置就与众不同！\
**Kanjira**: See, the place you is visiting is different from others!

**坎吉拉**：这神庙除了本地人没几个游客愿意……咳，知道！目前也只开放了三个窟，但如果是我——\
**Kanjira**: This shrine, only few tourists are willing to ... ahem, only the locals know! And now, people can only go into three caves out of four. But, if you choose I ...

黑发女孩伸出手去，拍了拍地图上五角星的位置。\
The black-haired girl reaches out and pats the map on the star.

**坎吉拉**：您标记的这个北窟，我同样能带您好好享受～\
**Kanjira**: I can take you go north cave, even if it's not open!

玛蒂尔达皱起眉毛，眼中闪烁着质疑。\
Matilda frowns in response. There is suspicion in her eyes.

**玛蒂尔达**：那你打算怎么带我去呢？\
**Matilda**: How are you going to take me there?

**坎吉拉**：怎么带……怎么带比较合适？呃，当然是靠人脉啦！\
**Kanjira**: How, how I do that? Um, my local connections, of course!

**玛蒂尔达**：原来如此。怪不得资料和旅游手册上有出入……咳咳，当然了，这种小事，我早就知道了！\
**Matilda**: I see. No wonder there were some discrepancies between the documents and the tourist brochure. Ah-ahem, well, of course, I knew this all along!

**坎吉拉**：噗——咳。\
**Kanjira**: Heh heh.

**玛蒂尔达**：嗯？你笑什么？\
**Matilda**: Hmm? What are you laughing at?

**坎吉拉**：不不，客人，我只是打了个喷嚏……\
**Kanjira**: No, no, no, my dear guest, it's just sneeze.

**坎吉拉**：您看，只是想赚点小钱，您瞧我这样小的个子，就算有经验，也根本抢不过那些大人……\
**Kanjira**: Well, you see, I just make a living here. I'm short and thin, can't compare with adults.

她微微偏头，那角度像是精心设计过一般，恰到好处地泫然欲泣着。\
She tilts her head slightly—the angle is so perfect that it seems to be a result of countless practices—and sheds tears naturally.

**坎吉拉**：您这样厉害的人，也不会忍心看我这种幼小又脆弱的孩子因为赚不到钱而饿肚子吧——\
**Kanjira**: And you is so great. You will not let I, weak poor kid, get hungry for no money, will you?

**玛蒂尔达**：呃唔……你，你就算这样看着我——\
**Matilda**: Err. Even if you look at me with those puppy eyes ...

**坎吉拉**：而且，您是有眼光的，我一眼就瞧得出——您就像只聪明又勇敢的沙漠猫……\
**Kanjira**: First sight I know, you is a lady with great taste, just like a sand cat, brave and smart.

垂下去的绿色眼眸微不可察地抬了抬，时刻观察着对面女孩的神情变化。\
Kanjira's downcast green eyes subtly steal a covert glance up at Matilda, secretly reading the signs on her face.

**玛蒂尔达**：沙，沙漠猫？听起来好像很聪明的——\
**Matilda**: Sand, sand cat? It does sound like a smart animal.

**坎吉拉**：哎呀，遇到我，算是客人您的好运气～\
**Kanjira**: Anyways, you is lucky to meet me, my lady!

她一边说着，一边像是下了很大决心似的摆了摆手。\
Kanjira waves her hands as if she has made a big decision.

**坎吉拉**：我这次为了您这样的好顾客，只能吃大亏了！只要二百卢比，不光是神庙，我带您玩儿遍整个摩卢旁卡村～还附赠烛星节特殊观景点！\
**Kanjira**: Well, well, for a great customer like you, I can only suffer some loss! Just 200 rupees, and I'll show you the shrine and the whole Mor Pankh village! With a special Dīpa Festival tour on the house!

**坎吉拉**：——或许您还需要介绍旅店吗？那些我也很熟……\
**Kanjira**: Want me to recommend a hotel? I know good hotels, too.

**坎吉拉**：怎么样，客人？厉害的客人？您就帮帮我——\
**Kanjira**: Yes or no, my dear guest? My most great guest? Please ...

**玛蒂尔达**：好啦好啦……哼，看在你这么可怜的份儿上，就暂且允许你做我的帮手……\
**Matilda**: Fine, fine. I will allow you to be my temporary assistant, for your life has been so sad already.

**坎吉拉**：哦！太好了，那客人我们赶紧出发寻宝——咳呃！观光吧！\
**Kanjira**: Yay! Let's go treasure hunting, hmm, sightseeing!

**玛蒂尔达**：很好，那你有安排好接应的旅游巴士吗？\
**Matilda**: Excellent. Have you arranged a shuttle bus for the travel?

**坎吉拉**：哼哼——客人，我这儿有比巴士更为灵活的东西～\
**Kanjira**: Heh heh, I have something gooder than bus for you!

女孩带点脏污的小脸上露出了神秘的微笑。\
Kanjira puts on a mysterious smile on her stained face.

**坎吉拉**：保证能让您体验——绝佳的速度！\
**Kanjira**: And I promise you, quick like flash!

## JMP-03 寻宝新骑兵 / The Young Indiana Jones

**坎吉拉**：哈哈！好嘞，坐稳了——！\
**Kanjira**: Woo-hoo! Alright, sit tight!

**坎吉拉**：出发吧！\
**Kanjira**: Let's GO!!

**玛蒂尔达**：哇啊啊——？！\
**Matilda**: Waaaaah?!

**村民**：咳咳……又是你这个崽子！该死的，我都说了多少次了……辛哈怎么总是把这种惹人烦的人类玩意儿借给你！\
**Villager 1**: *coughs* You little j**k again! D**n it, Sinha, for one last time, don't borrow that annoying human thing to her!

明黄色的电动三轮在松软的路面上甩出一道优美的弧线，把路人的咒骂声遮掩在了黄灰色的沙砾里。\
The bright-yellow tuk tuk drifts in a beautiful arc on the soft road, the brown sand kicked up in the air covering up the curses of the passer-by.

**玛蒂尔达**：好快，好快，太快了啊！\
**Matilda**: Slow down, slow down! We are going too fast!

**玛蒂尔达**：呜哇哇哇！这是怎么回事啊——？！\
**Matilda**: Waaaah! Is this thing really under control?!

**坎吉拉**：嘿！\
**Kanjira**: Hey!

三轮顶上的万寿菊挂饰在风尘中扬起花瓣。\
As the tuk tuk roars along, the marigold petals are flying wildly in the wind.

**坎吉拉**：这才是刚开始呢！抓紧那根棍子——！！\
**Kanjira**: Not yet best part! Hold that bar tight!

**玛蒂尔达**：哇，哇啊啊啊——\
**Matilda**: Waaah ...

**玛蒂尔达**：呼……呼……\
**Matilda**: Whuu ... phew ...

**坎吉拉**：呜呼！客人，感觉如何啊？\
**Kanjira**: Woo-hoo! How you feel, my guest?

**玛蒂尔达**：……\
**Matilda**: ...

**玛蒂尔达**：呕……\
**Matilda**: *vomits*

**坎吉拉**：噢，真是抱歉，看来您还不太习惯这个。来，用这个擦擦……\
**Kanjira**: Oh, I'm sorry. You must not be used to this. Here, use it.

玛蒂尔达抬眼看着对方递来了自己的裙角，默默地掏出了自己口袋里的手帕。\
As Kanjira passes over the hem of her skirt, Matilda takes out a handkerchief from her pocket in silence.

**坎吉拉**：如果您更愿意弄脏丝绸的话……那好吧！毕竟客人您看起来挺讲究的……\
**Kanjira**: If you want your silk dirty. Fine, you look very decent after all.

**坎吉拉**：喏——就是这儿了。\
**Kanjira**: And, here it is.

寺庙的石砖斑驳，显然是有了一定的年头，空气中的香料味湿润黏稠，几乎封住了呼吸。\
The shrine is apparently an old one, judging by the worn bricks. The smell of sticky spices in the air is almost suffocating.

**玛蒂尔达**：这味道，怎么这么……咳咳……\
**Matilda**: What's this smell? Is it ... *coughs*

**坎吉拉**：饱满的白麝香与檀香，凝神静气的圣木与肉桂——唔，有没有感觉脉轮都打开啦？\
**Kanjira**: Smell of full white musk and sanders, calming palo santo and cinnamon. Hah! You feel your chakra open?

**坎吉拉**：但我更在意的是——嗯……闻起来有很多芒果……真香啊。\
**Kanjira**: But, I can also smell, hmm, a lot of mango. That smells good.

坎吉拉大致扫了下石墙的高度，点了点头。\
Kanjira glances at the stone wall to measure its height and then nods.

**坎吉拉**：很好……从这儿翻进去就可以了！\
**Kanjira**: Okay. Jump over this wall, and we are in!

**玛蒂尔达**：翻进去？！我以为至少会有个隐蔽的旁门！\
**Matilda**: Jump over it?! I thought there is at least a hidden side door!

**坎吉拉**：想要看到不开放的石窟，总要付出点代价嘛！\
**Kanjira**: To see the closed cave, you must pay a price!

**玛蒂尔达**：好啊，原来这就是你嘴里的“人脉”？\
**Matilda**: Ah. So this is your "local connections"!

**坎吉拉**：嗯……哦～那是三轮车的部分，客人！这个村的电三轮再没第二辆这么快的了。辛哈大叔的那份和善可是用我牙缝中省出来的好处交换的～\
**Kanjira**: Um. Well, that mean tuk tuk, my guest! No tuk tuk this village is faster than that! Uncle Sinha is not so nice and lend me if I don't give him my lunch money!

**坎吉拉**：这还能省下一笔门票钱呢，客人您该夸赞我的路线绝佳才对！\
**Kanjira**: My route don't need entrance ticket! Shouldn't you give me credit?

黑发女孩毫无被拆穿的尴尬，甚至神色里还多了几分得意。她伸出双手，组合成了一个方便蹬踏的台阶。\
Even if she is busted, Kanjira is not embarrassed at all. On the contrary, she looks a bit proud. She puts her hands together to form a temporary "stepping stone."

**坎吉拉**：来吧，我想您可能不太习惯这些“粗鲁”的行……\
**Kanjira**: Now come! Although I think you don't like this "rude" behavi- ...

**玛蒂尔达**：哼！\
**Matilda**: Humph!

无视了那个“台阶”，玛蒂尔达径自伸直双臂，轻巧一跃。\
Ignoring the "stepping stone," Matilda raises her arms and jumps up the wall deftly.

**坎吉拉**：嗯？\
**Kanjira**: Hmm?

**玛蒂尔达**：我不拿你的裙角擦鼻子可是为了你好，你竟敢小瞧我……这种高度对我来说，根本就是小菜一碟！\
**Matilda**: I was thoughtful and considerate enough not to wipe my nose on your skirt, yet you repay my kindness with contempt. Climbing over a wall of this height is really a piece of cake!

**玛蒂尔达**：怎么样？要不要我拉你一把？\
**Matilda**: So? Do you need a hand getting up here?

金发女孩骑在墙头，得意洋洋地看着下面。\
Matilda looks down proudly from the top of the wall.

**坎吉拉**：……\
**Kanjira**: ...

**坎吉拉**：嘿！奇怪的家伙。\
**Kanjira**: Huh! Weirdo.

神庙内被浓厚的烟雾笼罩着，虔诚的信众穿梭其中。远远望去，烟雾变成了一群长了腿，富有着香料香气的云。\
The shrine is shrouded in thick smoke and packed with pious believers, resembling a legged cloud with the smell of spices.

而两个小小的身影左右闪躲，鬼鬼祟祟地潜入了墙角的阴影之中。\
The two small figures sneak into the shadow in the corner while avoiding the believers in their way.

**玛蒂尔达**：真不知道为什么要这么偷偷摸摸的！你别是什么骗……\
**Matilda**: I don't know what this skulking was for! You'd better not be lying!

**坎吉拉**：嚼嚼……\
**Kanjira**: Nom nom.

**玛蒂尔达**：喂，你手里……？！\
**Matilda**: Hey, what's that in your hand?!

**坎吉拉**：您也想来一口？过来祈福的家伙虔诚得很，带过来的果子不会差的……唔，和我猜的一样！这芒果真甜……\
**Kanjira**: You want a bite? The prayers are so pious, so don't worry, the fruits is tasty! Nom nom, like I expect, so sweet.

**玛蒂尔达**：你什么时候——你怎么能随便拿别人的贡品！\
**Matilda**: When did you ... Did you take it from the offerings?!

**坎吉拉**：不用在意这些小事情！曼咔，回来。\
**Kanjira**: Don't mind! Manka, come back.

黑色的小蛇悄悄游上她的手臂。\
A little black snake creeps up her arm quietly.

**坎吉拉**：顺便一提，希望您不害怕蛇——我和别人比，稍微有些特殊……\
**Kanjira**: By the way, I hope you is not afraid of snakes. I'm a special kind.

**玛蒂尔达**：你指什么？哼，是指特别的粗鲁，还是特别地令我恼火？\
**Matilda**: And I'm curious about what exactly you are referring to. Specially rude, or specially annoying?

**坎吉拉**：咦，您这就恼火——我是指，咳咳，我是一名……神秘学家。希望您不会被我吓得跑掉，放心，我属于里面比较……\
**Kanjira**: Why so angr- ... I mean, um, I'm arcanist. Hope I don't scare you. Relax, I'm not like others.

**玛蒂尔达**：你在开玩笑吗？你看不出我也是一名优秀的——最优秀的那种——神秘学家？\
**Matilda**: Are you serious? Can't you tell I'm also an excellent, one of the best, arcanist?

玛蒂尔达激动地弹跳了一下，注意到人群，又不得不迅速蹲下身子。\
Matilda jumps up with a jerk out of excitement, but then she notices the crowds and has to crouch down again very quickly.

**玛蒂尔达**：你果然是骗子！还说什么眼光好，看得出我的……\
**Matilda**: So you were lying to me! Spoke about all those good virtues you can see in me.

**坎吉拉**：嘿，这不怪我，您一点儿也不像！\
**Kanjira**: Hey! It's not my fault! You doesn't look like one!

坎吉拉抛掉手中的芒果核，略带惊讶地将玛蒂尔达上下打量了一番。\
Kanjira drops the mango core and scans Matilda in slight surprise.

**坎吉拉**：我以为，除了我之外的所有神秘学家都会像……\
**Kanjira**: I thought all arcanists except me are like ...

**玛蒂尔达**：像什么？\
**Matilda**: Like what?

**坎吉拉**：……像这里的村民，一些迂腐的老头子和大叔，见到人类总是大呼小叫，像是看到了讨人厌的猴子或是尖叫的鸡，甚至会把来帮助他们的人类赶出他们的地盘——\
**Kanjira**: Like the villagers, those old mans, yell when they see humans, like annoying monkeys or crowing chickens. They even drive humans away, don't care they is here to help.

**坎吉拉**：不然您以为，为什么只有那个火车站光洁如新？其他地方的人类，早被他们赶走啦！\
**Kanjira**: Why you think only the train station is tidy and clean? Humans in other places is all drive away!

**坎吉拉**：我是因为……算了，总之，我从未想过除我以外还有……\
**Kanjira**: I'm not like them because ... Anyways, I never thought there is more arcanist like me.

女孩儿的声音逐渐放轻，脸上出现了一丝不解。\
Kanjira speaks in a quiet voice. A confused look appears on her face.

**玛蒂尔达**：哼，要我说，你只是读的书太少，见识不够多罢了！\
**Matilda**: Humph, if you ask me, I'd say you read too little and know too little.

**玛蒂尔达**：建议你跟着我好好学学，学习一下真正的神秘学家应有的姿态……\
**Matilda**: I suggest you follow my example and adopt the style of a real arcanist.

**坎吉拉**：哦哦，说得没错！曼咔说外面人不多！很好，挺胸抬头，就像咱们交了钱一样地走过去！\
**Kanjira**: Fine, fine! Oh, Manka say there is just a few people outside, so up your head, stay confident, and walk out like we paid!

**玛蒂尔达**：……\
**Matilda**: ...

**玛蒂尔达**：……你到底有没有在听我说话啊！\
**Matilda**: Have you been listening or not?!

云雾缭绕之中，玛蒂尔达跟随着坎吉拉来到石窟口。\
Following Kanjira, Matilda goes through the smoke and arrives at the entrance to the cave.

**坎吉拉**：很好，很好……像以往一样，一个人都没有！\
**Kanjira**: Ha! Nice. Nobody around as usual!

**坎吉拉**：不过还是建议您小心行事，鉴于……嗯，挖掘总是要破坏点什么的——总之一定要破坏的话，别和我扯上关系就行！\
**Kanjira**: But I still suggest you be careful, since ... Hmm, I understand the damage when digging. Just don't involve me if you must break something!

玛蒂尔达抬头望去，全然没听进去女孩细碎的话语。\
Matilda looks up, not hearing a word of her mutter.

**玛蒂尔达**：这就是……“毗因陀之首”吗……\
**Matilda**: So this is "the Head of Vindre"?

石窟的顶部像一口黑洞，不知延伸向何处，也不知会吞没什么。\
The top of the cave looks like a black hole. No one knows where it will lead or what it will devour.

**坎吉拉**：啧啧啧，黑黝黝的，看着真吓人。但这就是寻宝的必经之路，就像那句“芝麻开门”一样！不是吗？\
**Kanjira**: Tsk tsk, dark and scary. But this is what must go through on the way to treasure, just like you must say "Open Sesame," right?

**玛蒂尔达**：真不懂你一直嘟囔的寻宝究竟是什么……你不会是误会了什么吧？\
**Matilda**: I really don't know what to make of this "treasure" you've been mumbling about. I hope you didn't get the wrong idea.

**坎吉拉**：啊——您的意思，我很明白！放心，守口如瓶，我绝对不会说出去的。\
**Kanjira**: Ah. I see what you mean here. Relax. I will zip my lips and tell no one.

她在嘴巴旁做了一个关上拉链的手势，真挚地点了点头。\
She zips her mouth shut and nods sincerely.

**坎吉拉**：那么，我就不进去了，祝您一切顺利！\
**Kanjira**: I'll just stay here, then. Everything good luck!

**玛蒂尔达**：嗯？虽然你总在嘟囔着些奇怪的东西，但终归是把我带到了目的地……那就这样吧！多谢你啦。\
**Matilda**: Ah? Anyway, despite all the strange things you've been talking about along the way, you have successfully taken me here as promised. I guess here is where we part! Thank you.

玛蒂尔达摆摆手，一边翻开着资料，一边转身向石窟内走去。\
After bidding her goodbye, Matilda turns around to walk toward the cave while browsing the documents in her hand.

很快，那片深不见底的黑暗便隐去了她的身影。\
Soon she is devoured by the bottomless darkness.

**坎吉拉**：衷心地祝福您，勇敢的客人！不论是巨蛇还是巨龙，如果您真找到了传说中的宝藏，我们就一定还会再见面的～嘿嘿～\
**Kanjira**: Sincerest wishes to you, my brave guest! Whether a giant snake or dragon, as long as you find the legendary treasure, we'll meet again! Hee hee.

脚步声层层回荡在窟内，仿佛一首音律不齐的打击乐。\
Footsteps echo inside the cave like a piece of poorly composed percussion music.

**玛蒂尔达**：这个壁画……看起来真的和那个神话有关系！资料在……这儿！让我看看……\
**Matilda**: This mural seems to be related to that myth! Here, on this paper! Let me see.

在视线所能达到的尽头，巨大的浮雕壁画赫然其上。\
There is a huge mural carved on the wall, spreading to the end of her sight.

女孩快速地翻动着笔记的纸页。\
She turns the pages of the notebook quickly.

**玛蒂尔达**：找到了！……“彗首降世之初，毗因陀之首以北有石生长……”\
**Matilda**: Found it! "Before the Serpent struck in night sky, the stone house of Asura rose to the north of the Head of Vindre."

**玛蒂尔达**：“石之子，处处生足，处处生目，并阿修罗之相，使致人之子庇佑之处倾塌……”\
**Matilda**: "The master of the stone has acted, with countless feet, with countless eyes, to trip, to pry, in bringing the blessed house of men to rest."

**玛蒂尔达**：哇……真厉害，说不定这就是某种神秘动物的起源……\
**Matilda**: Wow, impressive! Perhaps this is the origin of some arcane creature.

**玛蒂尔达**：“彗首”……也就是说……天体能量的最佳修习时间，是要等到流星降落的时刻？\
**Matilda**: "The Serpent struck," that is to say, the best time to practice on the celestial energy is when the comet goes across the sky?

**玛蒂尔达**：“继而彗发临地，人子没入虚妄域，因欲而堕……”\
**Matilda**: "Long darkness reaches the men as the Serpent's tail reveals itself. Some are sent down the great slopes and never return ..."

**玛蒂尔达**：“……因妄念而不可回。”\
**Matilda**: "... for desire is the infallible devourer. "

**玛蒂尔达**：妄念啊……嗯，感觉在修习前还是得先进行冥想才好……\
**Matilda**: Desire, hmm, I should meditate before practice.

**玛蒂尔达**：“万物终于彗尾，皆……”\
**Matilda**: "The circle of everything ends at the tip of the great tail, all ..."

“咚！”\
THUD!

**玛蒂尔达**：……！\
**Matilda**: ...!

回响消失了。\
The echo has disappeared.

身后，只有无尽的黑暗。\
Behind her, there is nothing but boundless darkness.

**玛蒂尔达**：是我听错了吗——\
**Matilda**: Did I hear it wrong?

**玛蒂尔达**：……！是真的有声音。\
**Matilda**: No ...

**玛蒂尔达**：出来！是谁！\
**Matilda**: Come into the light! Who, who is there?

声音在石窟中仍只是被荡了一层又一层。\
Her voice ripples out. Its echoes and the echoes of the echoes reverberate between the walls of the cave.

无人应答。\
There is no response.

**玛蒂尔达**：……不对。\
**Matilda**: This doesn't seem right.

**玛蒂尔达**：这个雕像，刚刚是这个姿势吗？\
**Matilda**: Was this statue posing like this earlier?

就在玛蒂尔达犹疑的时候，视线中的石像动了起来。\
While Matilda is still wondering, the statues in her sights start to move.

**玛蒂尔达**：呀！\
**Matilda**: Aah!

那些或作佛观，或盘踞而坐的石像扭曲着，挣扎着，自墙壁上探身而出。\
The benevolent-looking statues, which were sitting in lotus position, are now struggling in a twisted way to break free from the wall.

**玛蒂尔达**：不好！赶紧离开这里……\
**Matilda**: Not good! Time to retreat.

玛蒂尔达试图转身向外跑去，地板却如同正在被收起的地毯一般迅速后撤。\
She turns around immediately and runs toward the exit, yet the ground is pulling her back like a rolling carpet.

**玛蒂尔达**：什——呜啊！好痛！\
**Matilda**: What?! Aah!

她感觉自己的下巴狠狠地在岩石上磕了一下。\
She can feel her chin hitting hard against the rock.

一只手臂，两只手臂，更多的手臂自石像两侧分裂开来，每一只掌心内都嵌着一颗明润的眼珠。\
One arm, two, three, and more of them are growing out from both sides of the statues, each with a glossy eyeball embedded within.

**玛蒂尔达**：这是……这是什……\
**Matilda**: What? What is this!

细微的响动，让每一道视线都集中到了仰倒在地面的女孩身上。\
Following the slight noise, every eye turns to the girl lying on the ground.

**玛蒂尔达**：呜，呜……快点，振作起来！要把平时所学的东西，全，全都用上……！\
**Matilda**: Oh! Hurry up. Get yourself together! Think what you have learned and practiced in the past!

## JMP-04 交织线 / Intersecting Lines

**玛蒂尔达**：哈……哈……痛……好痛……！\
**Matilda**: Aah, ouch, it hurts!

**玛蒂尔达**：怎么……怎么会有这么多的石像……！\
**Matilda**: How ... how come there are so many of them!

暗黄色的石雕如同野草，仿佛有着无尽的生命力，倒下一个，就有更多新的自各处诞生而来。\
Like overgrown grass, more and more statues are coming out of the walls, no matter how many Matilda destroys.

布满尖碎石子的地上，玛蒂尔达捂着自己的腰间吃痛地喘息。\
Matilda lies against the sharp gravel on the ground. She covers her waist and gasps in pain.

**玛蒂尔达**：不行，不行……得赶紧想想办法……\
**Matilda**: Not good, not good. Think, Matilda.

鲜血像是止不住一般自指缝间涌出，生命力似乎与血液一起从躯体中被抽离了出去。\
Blood is running out from between her fingers unstoppably, taking away her vitality like a water pump does.

面前的石雕高高举起了手中宝伞。\
The statue in front of her raises the umbrella in its hand.

**玛蒂尔达**：不，不可以……！\
**Matilda**: No, don't ...!

女孩的双手被血液浸润，几乎握不住手中的水晶球。\
Her hands drenched in blood, she can no longer hold the orb.

**伽菈波那**：站起来！\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Get on your feet!

**玛蒂尔达**：嗯？\
**Matilda**: Hmm?

无力的四肢突然在瞬间充满了力量。\
The moment she hears the strange voice, Matilda regains strength in her limbs.

**玛蒂尔达**：啊！\
**Matilda**: Aah!

玛蒂尔达整个人如提线木偶一般不受控制地向上弹起。\
She can't help but bounce up like a puppet controlled by some invisible threads.

**伽菈波那**：做得好……小占卜师。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Well done, little diviner.

**伽菈波那**：&\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: &

**玛蒂尔达**：腿怎么自己……血和伤口……消失了？\
**Matilda**: My legs, they heal themselves. Where are the wounds?

**伽菈波那**：闭上眼睛，什么都不要看。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Close your eyes. Don't look at anything.

**伽菈波那**：幻觉会摧毁你的意志。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: The illusions would destroy your will.

**玛蒂尔达**：什么？刚才的居然是……\
**Matilda**: Wait. That, that was ...

**伽菈波那**：%\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: %

**玛蒂尔达**：哈……哈……\
**Matilda**: *pants*

石窟内恢复了最初的阴冷黑暗，仿佛什么都没发生过一般。\
Silence and cold fall again, as if nothing has happened.

玛蒂尔达低头反复确认着自己的双腿，将大腿拍得啪啪作响。\
Matilda looks down at her legs, slapping them to check if she's dreaming.

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

然而，它们光滑，灵巧，无比健康——除了被拍打出来的轻微的红印，不曾受过任何伤害。\
However, they are smooth, nimble, and healthy. There are no signs of injury on her skin other than the light red marks from the slaps.

**玛蒂尔达**：为什么会这样……难道那是某种致幻的神秘术？\
**Matilda**: How come ...? Is it some kind of hallucinating arcane skill?

**玛蒂尔达**：你，你是车站里的那个……\
**Matilda**: You are the lady from the train station.

她抬头，看向一旁伫立的女人。\
She looks at the lady in confusion.

**伽菈波那**：看来我们有一部分命运纠缠在了一起，孩子。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Looks like part of our destinies are now tied together, kid.

伽菈波那轻轻地露出一个安抚性的微笑。\
Kaalaa Baunaa responds to her with a reassuring smile.

**伽菈波那**：你怎么会来这样的地方？这里应当不会对游客开放……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: What are you doing here? I don't think this place is open to tourists.

**玛蒂尔达**：我……\
**Matilda**: I ...

**伽菈波那**：……！\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...!

石窟深处的黑暗微不可察地扭曲着。\
Something is churning imperceptibly in the dark.

**玛蒂尔达**：它们……又出现了！\
**Matilda**: They are coming again!

**玛蒂尔达**：这次也是幻觉吗？\
**Matilda**: Is it another illusion?

手，手，和更多的手。熟悉的暗黄色雕像像是某种刚冲破卵壳的新生之物，黏着撕扯着自黑暗中剥离出来。\
Hands, hands, and more hands. The familiar dark-yellow statues are like newly hatched creatures, slimy and ugly. They are trying hard to break the shell of darkness.

**伽菈波那**：不，不对。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: No, they are not.

**伽菈波那**：……请站到我身后来。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Please, stay behind me.

女人的声音里带着一丝困惑。\
Kaalaa Baunaa sounds a bit confused.

**伽菈波那**：它们看上去……是实体……？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: They look ... real?

**玛蒂尔达**：——小心，它们过来了！快躲开！\
**Matilda**: Careful! Watch out! They are coming again! Move!

**伽菈波那**：咳咳，你没事吧？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: *coughs* Are you alright?

伽菈波那拉着女孩掩藏在岩石后方，她的手指小心翼翼地拨开金色的头发，一道伤口裸露了出来。\
Hiding behind the rock, Kaalaa Baunaa carefully brushes away Matilda's milky blonde hair to find a wound.

**伽菈波那**：……这不再是幻觉了。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Not illusions this time.

**伽菈波那**：这下糟了。可恶！库玛尔是怎么做到的……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Too bad. D**n it! How did Kumar do this!

**玛蒂尔达**：呜——！好痛……这一切都是怎么回事？我只是来……\
**Matilda**: Aarh! The pain ... What is happening now? I was only here for ...

**伽菈波那**：抱歉，但现在不是解释的时候。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Sorry, but it's not the time for explaining.

**伽菈波那**：你看，我们就快到出口了，你记住，出去之后尽快离开，离开这个村子，不要再……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: We are at the exit soon. Remember, leave this village as soon as possible after you're out. Do not ...

**伽菈波那**：——！\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...!

话音未落，她如同感应到了什么，护住女孩的头部迅速地向侧方滚去。\
Before she finishes the words, Kaalaa Baunaa seems to have sensed danger and immediately rolls to the side while covering Matilda's head.

巨大的岩石落下，用以躲藏的岩石应声化为了一摊齑粉。\
Huge rocks fall to the ground. The rock they hid behind is now a pile of powder.

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

石窟在石像的攻击下颤抖着。\
The cave shakes under the strikes of the statues.

**玛蒂尔达**：呜……\
**Matilda**: Um.

**？？？**：嘿——\
**???**: Hey!

陌生的声音自身旁擦过。\
They hear a strange voice.

**？？？**：——当心头顶！\
**???**: Watch your head!

玛蒂尔达感觉环着她的怀抱紧张似的收紧了一些。\
Kaalaa Baunaa seems quite nervous; her arms are holding Matilda even more tightly.

略微眼熟的身影轻巧地攀上石像高处，挥出了拳头。\
A familiar figure leaps onto the statue's shoulder and raises his fist.

**？？？**：——嗬！\
**???**: Hah!

石像的左脸飞了出去。\
The left half of the statue's face flies across the cave.

**？？？**：啊哈，还挺结实！原来这石像还会自己动……老爹可没告诉过我这个。\
**???**: Huh, harder than I thought! Dad hadn't told me those statues could move.

**？？？**：再来——！\
**???**: Again!

被男人击碎的巨大石像崩落开来，无数大块的碎石坠向地面。\
The giant statue breaks into pieces under his fist and falls to the ground.

**？？？**：喔！这也太危险了——\
**???**: Whoa! That's dangerous!

**？？？**：唔——！抱歉啦，虽然你们看着很酷，但你们也太不友善了……\
**???**: Sorry. Though you have a very impressive appearance as a statue, your attitude and manner are problematic.

**？？？**：……哈！\
**???**: Hah!

**玛蒂尔达**：哇哇！\
**Matilda**: Waah!!

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

伽菈波那轻轻拉住玛蒂尔达，向右前方挪了下步子。\
Kaalaa Baunaa grips Matilda's sleeve gently, pulling her one step to the side.

——紧接着，碎石擦着她们的发梢，狠狠地砸向了她们前一秒驻足的地方。\
The next moment, the falling rocks graze their hair and smash into the ground.

**玛蒂尔达**：……呜！\
**Matilda**: Ugh!

石窟内终于回归了安静。\
The cave goes quiet again.

被击落的石像碎片形成了一座小丘。\
The debris of the statue piles up in front of them.

**？？？**：唔呃——嘿！\
**???**: Hah-ah!

眼前的大块岩石被丢到一边，男人从碎石里探出头来，扑落着肩膀上的尘土。\
A huge rock is cast aside. The man emerges from the ruins, patting the dust off his broad shoulders.

**？？？**：呼——！压死我了……\
**???**: Phew! I almost got killed.

**？？？**：嘿！你们没事吧，这些东西真是太吓人了！\
**???**: Hey, you guys alright? These things are freaky!

他摇摇晃晃地从石堆上滑下来，向着玛蒂尔达她们的方向靠近。\
As he speaks, he waddles down from the huge pile of rocks and walks toward Matilda.

**？？？**：不过……或许你们知道这些东西是从哪儿来的吗？我刚走到门口就差点被它们敲碎脑壳……\
**???**: So, do you know where they came from? My head almost got smashed when I reached the entrance.

男人的动作不算快，但嘴上却一刻都没有歇着。\
He walks at a slow pace, but he keeps his tongue busy.

**？？？**：唔，我有十一……或者是十二年没回这儿了？刚回来就遇到这个，真是个惊喜，是吧？\
**???**: Hmm, it's been 11 or maybe 12 years since I left this place. I'm welcomed by these things as soon as I'm back. What a surprise, huh?

**玛蒂尔达**：……？\
**Matilda**: ...?

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

**玛蒂尔达**：他在和我们说话吗……？\
**Matilda**: Is he talking to us?

男人在玛蒂尔达眼前站定，突然微微皱起眉头。\
The man walks over to Matilda. His eyebrows are drawn together in bewilderment.

**？？？**：哎……等等。\
**???**: Mmm. Wait.

那团眉毛迅速地松开，高高扬起。\
But quickly, his face brightens up.

**？？？**：你不是那个在车站被人偷了东西的小家伙嘛！还记得我吗？\
**???**: Aren't you the little one from the train station? I helped get your stuff back, remember me?

男人胡乱抹了一把自己的脸，试图让玛蒂尔达看得更清楚些。\
The man quickly wipes his face, hoping that Matilda can see him more clearly.

**玛蒂尔达**：噢……哦……！\
**Matilda**: Huh? Oh!

玛蒂尔达想起了那个在火车站的巨大身影。\
The tall figure takes her back to the train station.

**玛蒂尔达**：是你……！被那个扒手咬了一口的大叔！\
**Matilda**: It's you, the man bitten by the thief!

**？？？**：噢，没错，那一口咬得非常实在……\
**???**: Yeah, that's me. That was one merciless bite.

他咧开一个笑容。\
He cracks a smile.

**？？？**：真是令人惊喜的巧合——虽然这环境有点尴尬，但咱们没得挑……\
**???**: Ha! What a happy coincidence! Well, maybe this is not the best place for a reunion, but the occasion is not for us to decide.

**鬃毛沙砾**：哦，自我介绍一下，我叫鬃毛沙砾，虽然之前没帮成你，让那个小崽子跑没影了……但看来这次还挺成功的！\
**Shamane**: Oh, I should introduce myself this time. The name is Shamane. Sorry, I wasn't much of a helping hand earlier and let that kid get away. But this time, I have made it up to you, eh? Eh?

**玛蒂尔达**：哦，呃……\
**Matilda**: Oh, emm.

玛蒂尔达心有余悸地瞟了一眼脚边的碎石。\
Matilda casts a hesitant glance at the ruins.

**玛蒂尔达**：……或许算成功……吧？\
**Matilda**: You have made it up, I guess?

**伽菈波那**：抱歉……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Sorry to interrupt you.

站在一旁的女人微微抬手，打断了二人的谈话。\
Kaalaa Baunaa raises a hand and interrupts them.

**伽菈波那**：我想目前这里的安全或许只是暂时的，尽快离开这个地方应当是更稳妥的选择。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: But I think this place is safe only for now. It'd be a wise choice to leave as soon as possible.

她的语速比原来快了一些。\
She speaks a bit faster.

**伽菈波那**：不，不仅是指离开这个石窟，实际上……你们似乎是这里的游客？我更希望你们可以在这几天离开这个村子……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: And I mean more than this cave. Actually, are you tourists? I'm hoping you can leave this village in a couple of days.

**玛蒂尔达**：嗯？\
**Matilda**: Hmm?

**伽菈波那**：我知道这有些奇怪，但请你们先相信我——\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I know this sounds weird, but you need to trust me.

她略带匆忙地将手探入风衣的口袋，试图拽出一叠文件。\
She reaches inside the pocket of her coat and tries to take out a stack of files.

**伽菈波那**：嗯？该死，我的证件去哪儿了——啊！\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Huh? D**n, where's my ID? Ah!

手指一滑，文件散落一地。\
Her finger slips, and the files litter the floor.

**鬃毛沙砾**：哦，哇哦，哦……不急，女士，不急……慢慢来，我们在听。\
**Shamane**: Whoa, whoa, whoa. Easy, lady. Take your time. We're listening.

鬃毛沙砾也跟着弯下身来，帮助对方将那些纸张重新规整到一处。\
Shamane hunkers next to her, helping her pick up the files.

**鬃毛沙砾**：啊，你的证件在这儿！伽菈——波那小姐？拿好了……\
**Shamane**: Oh, here's your ID! Ms. Kaalaa Baunaa? Hold it.

**伽菈波那**：谢谢……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Ah, thank you.

伽菈波那伸手去接，意外的是，对方却没放松手上的力道。\
Kaalaa Baunaa reaches for the card, but he doesn't loosen his hand.

**伽菈波那**：……？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...?

鬃毛沙砾一脸不可思议，抬手指着女人的腰间。\
Shamane points at her waist with a shocked look on his face.

她顺着目光看过去，断了一只镜腿的玳瑁色眼镜正如往常一样挂在那里。\
She follows his gaze and looks down. A pair of tortoiseshell spectacles hangs on her belt, one temple broken.

**鬃毛沙砾**：这是……我绝对没认错……\
**Shamane**: This is ... No, I can't be wrong.

**鬃毛沙砾**：库玛尔的东西怎么会挂在你身上？\
**Shamane**: How come you have Kumar's stuff on your belt?

**伽菈波那**：……！\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...!

她下意识地捏紧了证件。\
Without conscious thought, she tightens her grasp on her ID.

**伽菈波那**：你——你认识库玛尔……？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: You ... You know Kumar?

**玛蒂尔达**：嗯？库玛尔？谁……？\
**Matilda**: Hmm? Kumar? Who's that?

玛蒂尔达将滑到远处的文件拾了回来。\
Matilda returns to their side with the files she found nearby.

**玛蒂尔达**：而且你们俩怎么停下了……不是说要先离开这里吗？\
**Matilda**: And what's with the shock? I thought we need to leave now.

她困惑地嘟囔着，自顾自地拾起地上的最后一张纸片。\
She mumbles in confusion and picks up the last piece of paper on the ground.

**玛蒂尔达**：好的，一个也没落下！我看看，这边是第一页，第二页……\
**Matilda**: Okay, that's the last one! Let me see, Page 1, Page 2 ...

纸张被展平，颠倒，翻动，快速地回归到自己本来的位置。\
As she speaks, the files are flattened, moved around, and rearranged.

**玛蒂尔达**：第五……嗯？\
**Matilda**: Page 5, hmm?

熟悉的内容让翻动的动作停滞了。\
She stops at a page with familiar content.

**玛蒂尔达**：哦……？\
**Matilda**: What?

那是一张数据分析图，周围的字迹娟秀，却显得有些匆忙混乱，甚至有些字眼的旁边还被打上了问号。\
It is a data analysis chart. Some notes, hastily written in graceful handwriting, are left next to it. Some words are even highlighted with question marks.

**玛蒂尔达**：这是有关彗星能量的……这不就是我想修习的那个吗？！\
**Matilda**: These papers are on celestial energy and exactly the one I want to practice on!

**玛蒂尔达**：嗯嗯，没错，这部分的神秘学能量分析和我查到的几乎一致……\
**Matilda**: That's right. The analysis on the arcane energy is very similar to that in the materials I found.

**玛蒂尔达**：可它看上去……\
**Matilda**: But not completely. This one looks ...

统计图里黑色的曲线形成了一个令人不安的陡峭的趋势。\
The black curves in the chart make her stomach sink.

玛蒂尔达的目光飞速地下滑，直到页脚处的最后一个标注了问号的单词。\
Her gaze slides down the page and fixes on a word with a question mark next to it.

**玛蒂尔达**：……“重塑之手”？\
**Matilda**: Ah! Manus Vindictae?

**玛蒂尔达**：什么……？！\
**Matilda**: What?!

## JMP-05 菩提树 / The Sacred Fig

**坎吉拉**：嗝，吃得真饱……♪～\
**Kanjira**: Burp. What a good meal.

**坎吉拉**：嗯？怎么里面还是一点儿动静都没有？那家伙不会……真的被什么怪东西吃掉了吧？\
**Kanjira**: Hmm? Still nothing happened after so long? She won't really be eaten by some monster, right?

**坎吉拉**：唔……呃……算啦！\
**Kanjira**: Hmm. Forget it!

**坎吉拉**：随便什么神，保佑那个傲慢的笨蛋已经顺利逃跑了——哦，并且没带走宝贝！\
**Kanjira**: Lord whoever, bless that stupid moron has escaped from there. Oh, and without the treasures!

坎吉拉用裙角擦了擦嘴，朝石窟里迈进。\
Kanjira wipes her mouth with the hem of her skirt and steps into the cave.

**坎吉拉**：悄悄地，悄悄地……哦？\
**Kanjira**: Be careful. Don't be spotted. Oh?

**坎吉拉**：啊！那家伙还好好的——他们怎么在那么里面……而且还多了两个人？\
**Kanjira**: Huh! She's fine. What is she doing in the depths? Who are those two?

她轻巧地爬上一块岩石。\
She quietly climbs on a rock nearby.

**坎吉拉**：唔……嗯——！\
**Kanjira**: Oomph. Mmm!

**坎吉拉**：这里怎么多了那么多石头……啊……差一点点就能爬——上——去——\
**Kanjira**: I didn't know there were so many rocks here. Okay. Keep climbing, almost there.

脏脏的脚丫努力地向上够着，试图攀上岩石上那个恰好的凸起。\
She kicks her dusty feet in the air, struggling to climb onto a raised edge of the rock.

**坎吉拉**：呜……？\
**Kanjira**: Huh?

有东西抓住了她的脚踝。\
Something grabs her ankle.

**坎吉拉**：什么东……\
**Kanjira**: What is it?

她皱着眉将目光下移——\
She frowns and looks down ...

那是一只断手。\
It is a severed hand.

**坎吉拉**：啊——！！\
**Kanjira**: AHHH!!

坎吉拉条件反射般猛地将腿踢了出去。\
Impulsively, Kanjira kicks her leg.

原本就布满裂痕的断手被甩向半空，在落地的时刻应声而碎，再没有了动静。\
The hand, already covered with many cracks, is thrown into the air and smashes into pieces on the ground.

**坎吉拉**：呼……呼……\
**Kanjira**: Whuu ... phew ...

那是什么？谁的手？这里为什么会有手？\
Is that a hand? Whose hand is it? Where does it come from?

女孩的心脏砰砰地跳着。\
Her heart beats violently.

她屏住呼吸，大着胆子凑到那些碎片前面去瞧。\
She holds her breath and gathers enough courage to look closer.

**坎吉拉**：……石头？\
**Kanjira**: It's stone?

犹豫再三，坎吉拉伸手试探性地触碰了一下石块，随即手脚麻利地将它们拼到了一起。\
She tentatively touches a lump with her fingertip. Nothing happens. Feeling relieved, she starts putting them back together.

**坎吉拉**：……！\
**Kanjira**: ...!

**坎吉拉**：这看上去像里面那些丑丑的怪雕像……这里的雕像……会动？\
**Kanjira**: It looks like one of those ugly statues in there, so they can move?

**坎吉拉**：哇哦……\
**Kanjira**: Wow!

**坎吉拉**：这就像，就像……！\
**Kanjira**: It's just like, like the ...!

女孩的眼中迸发出兴奋的光芒。\
There's a twinkle of excitement in her eyes.

**坎吉拉**：就像那些书里写的事！\
**Kanjira**: Like the story in the book!

**坎吉拉**：对的，对的！那些“守卫财宝的石像”……\
**Kanjira**: Yes, that's right! Those "golems guarding the treasure."

**坎吉拉**：瞧吧！我早就说那些都是真的！什么“吃掉城堡的巨龙”、“砸碎海洋的宝石”、“芝麻开门”……\
**Kanjira**: They are true! I knew it! And "the dragon that eats the castle," "the gem that smashes the sea," "Open Sesame" ...

**坎吉拉**：夏尔贾还骗我那些只是童话故事！\
**Kanjira**: Ms. Sherjah is lying! They are not fairy tales!

**坎吉拉**：怪不得多了两个人——他们就是“寻宝小队”！他们打败了这些“守卫”！\
**Kanjira**: No wonder she has two helpers. They are the "treasure hunters"! They beat the "guards"!

女孩兴奋且笃定地点了点头，对自己的想法深信不疑。\
She nods at her thought, overjoyed by the conclusion.

**坎吉拉**：噢，这太好了！只要我继续偷偷跟着，总能从他们的牙缝儿里取点“财宝”！就像卡希姆从斗上取下金币……\
**Kanjira**: Oh, yes! Just follow them secretly, and I will get at least a bit of the "treasure" they leave behind! Like how Kasim got the coin from the scales.

她被自己的发现鼓舞到了。\
She is heartened by the plan.

坎吉拉雀跃地转身，三两下就蹿回了那块岩石上，缓缓地靠近石窟深处的众人。\
She turns around, nimbly jumps on that rock again, and quietly follows the others in the cave.

**鬃毛沙砾**：好的，好的……虽然你说的每个字我都听得懂，但是它们连起来怎么这么难以消化……\
**Shamane**: Okay, okay. I think I understood every Hindi word, but none of them make any sense anymore when put together.

一片狼藉的石窟内，三人面面相觑。男人敲着脑袋，试图消化伽菈波那句子里的每一个单词。\
In the messy cave, the three of them look at each other speechlessly. Shamane is patting himself on the head, trying to understand Kaalaa Baunaa's words one by one.

**鬃毛沙砾**：你是说，库玛尔——那个我所认识的、从小到大只见过一面的姐姐……\
**Shamane**: You're saying, Kumar, that Kumar I know, the sister whom I've only seen once in my life ...

**伽菈波那**：——也就是我大学的导师。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ... is also my tutor in the university.

**玛蒂尔达**：还是个与重塑有关系的坏家伙？！\
**Matilda**: Plus, she's a bad guy associating with the Manus?!

玛蒂尔达将手中的文件慢慢放下。\
Matilda slowly puts down the files.

**玛蒂尔达**：……所以这个奇怪的增长曲线……天体能量的波动，是人为造成的？\
**Matilda**: So these abnormal growth curves ... The fluctuation of celestial energy is a man-made result?

**伽菈波那**：其实关于她与重塑的关联，我并没有十足的把握。但是……是的，你理解得没有错。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Actually, I'm not a hundred percent sure about their association, but yes, your conclusion about the growth curves is right.

她轻轻接过了被重新整理好的文件。\
Kaalaa Baunaa calmly takes over the files.

**伽菈波那**：天体能量的波动来源于一颗未被命名过的天体……而它的存在，只有我和库玛尔两人知道。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: The fluctuation was caused by an unnamed celestial body, and its existence is only known to Kumar and me.

**伽菈波那**：它曾是我们在班纳尔大学的研究项目。当时我们发现某些神秘学文献对研究非常有帮助……但后来……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: It was the object of our research at Banner University. At that time, we found some arcanum-related materials very helpful for our project, but then ...

伽菈波那轻轻摇了摇头。\
She gently shakes her head.

**伽菈波那**：神秘学在人类科学的研究内是被禁止的。我们被迫离开学校后分歧越来越严重，她太过激进……总之，我们最终分道扬镳。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: She was way too radical. Arcanum is strictly prohibited in the field of human science, and we were expelled from the university. After that, our disagreement got even worse. In the end, we took different paths.

**伽菈波那**：但显然，她和我都没放弃对这颗天体的研究。我们时常能从天体的变化中察觉到彼此的存在。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: But apparently, neither of us gave up on the research. We could frequently feel the existence of each other from the changes of the celestial body.

**伽菈波那**：而我在一次观测时发现了它的异常——此前从未有过这样剧烈而特殊的波动。但等我终于找到她研究所的位置时，那边的人说她早就已经离开了那里……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: And one day, I found an abnormality during the observation: the energy never fluctuated in such a fierce and peculiar way. I decided to contact her, but when I finally found the lab she had worked in, the staff told me she had already left.

她望向玛蒂尔达。\
She looks at Matilda.

**伽菈波那**：……我们共同的熟人曾告诉我，她偶然见到过库玛尔……跟着重塑之手的人离开了。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Our common friend told me she had seen Kumar by coincidence. She saw her leave with the Manus.

**玛蒂尔达**：……！\
**Matilda**: ...!

伽菈波那摊开左手，掌心之上，躺着一个脏兮兮的石块。\
Kaalaa Baunaa spreads her fingers and shows Matilda a dusty stone in her left palm.

它模糊的轮廓难以辨认，看上去似乎是一尊神像。\
Despite the misshapen outline, the stone seems to be a little idol.

**伽菈波那**：我在她留下的东西里发现了这个——我刚刚比对过缺口，它确实来自于这个石窟，而且……与那颗天体对应的神秘学文献有所关联。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: And I found this from what she left behind. I compared it to the hole in the wall. It does come from this cave, and it has something to do with the arcanum-related materials on that celestial body.

**伽菈波那**：但库玛尔从不出纰漏，这更像是她刻意为我留下的线索……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: But Kumar never makes mistakes. This one is more like a clue she left to me.

**玛蒂尔达**：唔……真是个奇怪的人……\
**Matilda**: Hmm. I don't understand her.

**伽菈波那**：但从目前的情况来看……她显然不只“邀请”了我……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Judging from the situation, apparently, I'm not the only one "invited."

她扬起右手上拿着的那个被不甚爱惜的、皱巴巴的信封。\
She raises her right hand, showing them the wrinkled envelope.

信封上面有着蓝色的邮戳，明黄色的蜡封上是一只象。而信封内，泛黄的信纸上空无一物。\
There is a blue postmark on the envelope and an elephant pattern on the bright-yellow seal. Inside the envelope, there is a worn piece of paper with nothing on it.

**鬃毛沙砾**：哦，在我看来这比刚才那些会动的石像还要怪！\
**Shamane**: Oh, this is getting even stranger than seeing those moving statues!

**鬃毛沙砾**：就像我说的，我是——嗯，现在应该说“几乎是”我家最后一个人了。\
**Shamane**: Like I said, I am, well, to be more precise, I "almost" am the last living member of my family.

他指了指蜡封上威风凛凛的大象。\
Shamane points at the majestic elephant on the seal.

**鬃毛沙砾**：这本应该是唯一一个，属于所谓继承人的印章——但很不幸，我早就不小心把那个印章丢到了熊肚子里了。\
**Shamane**: This stamp was supposed to come from a special seal that belongs to the heir of the family. Unfortunately, it was passed down to me, and I lost it to a bear many years ago.

**鬃毛沙砾**：而这个邮戳指向的位置，正是这个岩鸽都不来筑巢的石窟……\
**Shamane**: I checked the postmark on the envelope and found the letter came from this remote cave, where even rock pigeons don't bother to pay a visit.

**鬃毛沙砾**：鉴于那只黑熊自己乘坐交通工具来到这里给我寄信的可能性微乎其微，我觉得我有必要亲自过来瞧瞧这个情况。\
**Shamane**: Since it is highly unlikely that the bear with my seal in its belly would take transport all the way to a cave to send me a letter, I decided to come here myself and find out what this was all about.

**鬃毛沙砾**：不过你说的有一个地方有点奇怪……\
**Shamane**: But there's one thing I found weird in what you said.

鬃毛沙砾看上去有点犹豫。\
Shamane hesitates about what he is going to say.

**鬃毛沙砾**：就我所知，我姐姐作为神秘学家是非常……“不合格”的——她几乎和人类没有一点儿区别！连使用最基本的神秘术对她来说都难如登天！\
**Shamane**: As far as I know, my sister is even worse than "unqualified," if taken as an arcanist—She's almost like a human! It's nearly impossible for her to use the most basic arcane skills!

**鬃毛沙砾**：而这个——\
**Shamane**: And this ...

他摊开双手，示意着地下七零八落的石像肢体。\
He opens both of his palms and gestures in the direction of the broken statues on the ground.

**鬃毛沙砾**：这可不是一个普通的神秘学家能做到的事情……她可能操控这些东西吗？\
**Shamane**: This is not something a random person from our world can do. Is she really able to control these things?

**伽菈波那**：……她确实不能。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: No, she can't.

**伽菈波那**：但她知道方法，甚至知道了我不知道的方法……按理说，我们最多、最多只能创造出一些幻觉……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: But she has a solution—a solution even I'm not aware of. Theoretically, our skills can only create illusions and nothing more.

**伽菈波那**：尽管我不愿意相信……但如果真的是重塑给予了她帮助，这一切就是有可能的。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: But if the Manus really offered to help her, even though I don't want to think this way, she may be able to do that.

**鬃毛沙砾**：……噢，我忘了还有这一环。\
**Shamane**: Oh, I forgot the Manus part.

**鬃毛沙砾**：好吧，我这边知道的只有——如果这封信真是她的“邀请”……那估计没我什么好果子吃了。\
**Shamane**: Alright. All I know is, if this letter is really an "invitation" from her, I guess this won't be a delightful trip for me.

**伽菈波那**：关于她家里的事，我曾经有所耳闻……但我们的到来，应当并不是她的最终目的。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I've heard about that incident in her family, and I don't think her ultimate purpose is just to gather us here.

她转过身，郑重地面向玛蒂尔达。\
She turns around and looks at Matilda with a serious but sincere expression.

**伽菈波那**：谢天谢地，在这里遇到了你……小姑娘竟然是基金会的调查——\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Thank goodness I met you here, young lady. Can't believe I ran into a Foundation investigato- ...

**玛蒂尔达**：咳，咳咳，不，不用强调职位！每一位来自基金会的成员都有义务为了和平做出贡献——更何况是我这么出色的神秘学家！\
**Matilda**: Ahem. Don't, don't mind the title! Every member of the Foundation is obliged to contribute to the cause of peace, let alone an arcanist as extraordinary as I am!

**伽菈波那**：这真是太好了，看来娑罗室伐底还愿青睐于我……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: That's great. Sarasvati blessed me.

**玛蒂尔达**：嗯嗯，是的，基金会有我这样优秀的学员真是太好了……\
**Matilda**: Yeah, yeah, exactly. How fortunate the Foundation has been to have such an excellent subordinate like I am.

**伽菈波那**：——我以天文学教授及神秘学家的身份向基金会正式提出申请。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I hereby apply for assistance to the Foundation as an astronomy professor and an arcanist.

**玛蒂尔达**：嗯，嗯？\
**Matilda**: Em, emm?

**玛蒂尔达**：伽菈波那小姐……？\
**Matilda**: Yes, Ms. Kaalaa Baunaa?

**伽菈波那**：比起找到库玛尔和重塑，我们眼下有个更重要的问题。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Rather than find Kumar and the Manus, we have something more important to do now.

**玛蒂尔达**：更重要？\
**Matilda**: Something more important?

**伽菈波那**：希望基金会可以协助我尽快疏散摩卢旁卡村的居民与游客，目前，那颗近地……不，不……它不算小行星……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: We need the Foundation's assistance to evacuate the villagers and tourists in Mor Pankh village as soon as possible because that near-earth astero- ... No, no. It's not an asteroid.

**伽菈波那**：那颗我们研究的、无法以人类科学观测到的……天体，正以极快的速度接近该村，该星体的都灵危险指数为5，巴勒莫撞击指数预计为……0.01。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: That celestial body we study, not able to be observed by human technology, is approaching this village at a dangerous speed. It reaches level 5 on Torino Scale and 0.01 on Palermo Scale.

**玛蒂尔达**：什么？\
**Matilda**: What?

**伽菈波那**：简单来说，烛星节的流星雨即将演变成一场陨石灾难。我近期曾尝试过向周边地区的机构寻求支援，但村子的地理位置特殊，不在昌迪加尔的辖区内。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: In brief, the meteor shower that is occurring during Dīpa Festival will become a disaster of meteorites. I tried to ask organizations in the surrounding areas for help, but this village is out of Chandigarh's jurisdiction.

**伽菈波那**：除此之外，该村的民众也拒绝信任一切与人类有关系的社会机构……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Besides, the villagers refuse to accept help from any social organizations related to humans.

**鬃毛沙砾**：……\
**Shamane**: ...

**伽菈波那**：好在现在距离烛星节正式开始还有几天时间，如果现在疏散这里的村民，一切都还来得及……我也会尽快找到库玛尔，阻止她继续——无论她要继续做什么。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: The good news is, there are still days before the Dīpa Festival starts. We still have time to evacuate the people. Meanwhile, I will do whatever I can to find Kumar and stop her, no matter what her next step is.

**伽菈波那**：如果基金会同意支援，我将提供一切有效支持。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: If the Foundation offers its assistance, I will provide any support when needed.

**玛蒂尔达**：所以，这，这才是……\
**Matilda**: So this, this is her real ...

**伽菈波那**：是的——现在看来，石窟里发生的事很可能只是她的一次实验……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Yes. In this case, what happened in the caves was probably nothing more than an experiment.

**伽菈波那**：我不知道她究竟要用它做什么——但我不能看着她利用我们的研究、我们的心血做这种事。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I'm not sure why she's doing this, but I won't allow such an abuse of our hard work.

**伽菈波那**：这毕竟与我脱不了干系……所以，我一定要阻止它的坠落。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: It is our work, after all. That's why I must stop the star from falling.

**坎吉拉**：……！\
**Kanjira**: ...!

**坎吉拉**：该死……\
**Kanjira**: D**n it.

**鬃毛沙砾**：嗯？\
**Shamane**: Hmm?

**鬃毛沙砾**：你们有听到什么声音吗？\
**Shamane**: Did you guys hear anything?

**坎吉拉**：嘿——！\
**Kanjira**: Hey!

矮小的身影灵巧且迅速地翻过墙壁，急匆匆地沿着街道往另一个方向跑去。\
The small figure vaults deftly over the wall, running down the road in the opposite direction.

**坎吉拉**：呜……这是最糟、最糟的那种故事……！\
**Kanjira**: Ugh. This is the worst, worst fairy tale ever!

**坎吉拉**：没有财宝就算了，怎么还……怎么还会有石头掉下来啊！\
**Kanjira**: It has no treasures, and now even rocks are falling down!

**坎吉拉**：呼……呼……得赶紧回去……\
**Kanjira**: *pants* I, I have to go back.

**坎吉拉**：……必须告诉大家！\
**Kanjira**: And warn everyone!

她轻车熟路地转过几个弯，翻入一座破破烂烂的院子里。\
She seems to know the place well. She takes a few turns, climbs over another wall, and lands in a deserted yard.

**坎吉拉**：快，快跑……阿贾尔，你带着大家……\
**Kanjira**: Run, run. Ajar, you need to take everyone to ...

**坎吉拉**：呼呼……好累，喘死我了……\
**Kanjira**: *pants* I-I'm out of breath.

**？？？**：坎吉拉？\
**???**: Kanjira?

**坎吉拉**：……呃？夏尔贾老师？！你，你怎么找到这里的……\
**Kanjira**: Um, Ms. Sherjah?! Why, how you find this place?

**夏尔贾老师**：我当然得在这里了。这里是你们的秘密基地，啊，是吧？\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Of course, I can find it. It's your secret base, right?

她伸出手去，将难得出现紧张神色的女孩拉到自己面前。\
She reaches out and drags the nervous-looking girl to herself.

**夏尔贾老师**：擅自把别人的房子当作秘密基地——好啊……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: A secret base in other's house without the owner's permission? Well, well, well.

**坎吉拉**：呜哇……不，不不，夏尔贾老师，你先不要急着训我，这次是真的有大事……\
**Kanjira**: Aw. No, no, no, Ms. Sherjah. It's not time to judge me. Something huge just happen.

**夏尔贾老师**：抱歉，可爱的小糖饼。你的花招儿在我这里从没奏效过。\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Sorry, sweet Jalebi. Your tricks never worked on me.

年轻的女人拎起捣蛋鬼的一只耳朵。\
Sherjah catches the ear of the troublemaker.

**夏尔贾老师**：教唆阿贾尔偷窃，闯入无人住的老屋，让我看看——口袋——果然！这是谁的皮夹？看来我教给你的东西都忘干净了？\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Taught Ajar to steal? Broke into an old house? Let me check your pocket. I knew it! Whose wallet is this? Did you forget what I've taught you?

**坎吉拉**：是，是！这些都是我做的！对不起夏尔贾，可是……快放我下来——现在再不跑就真的晚了！这个村子就要被毁啦！\
**Kanjira**: Ye-yes! I do all these! I'm sorry, Ms. Sherjah, but LET ME DOWN!! It's too late if we don't leave now! The village is going to destroy!!

**夏尔贾老师**：你又在胡乱说些什么？\
**Ms. Sherjah**: What are you babbling about this time?

**坎吉拉**：是真的，是真的！我像个蠢蛋一样一路从神庙跑回来，都忘了自己从辛哈大叔那儿借来了车——\
**Kanjira**: It's real, not lie! I even run all the way back from the shrine like idiot, and leave tuk tuk I borrow from Uncle Sinha there.

**夏尔贾老师**：啊！你还去神庙偷吃了！你这小崽子……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Ah! You went to the shrine and ate the offerings again! Young Miss!

**坎吉拉**：呜呜，我真的知道错了！但是这次你一定要相信我啊！其他人呢？他们都去哪儿了？得赶紧告诉他们，越快越好，最好能爬上今天的火车……\
**Kanjira**: *sobs* I'm really sorry! But you must believe me this time! Where are the others? Where they go? We must tell them now. They must take train and leave this place today.

**夏尔贾老师**：唉，他们去街上做生意了……究竟是怎么回事——\
**Ms. Sherjah**: *sighs* They went to the street for business. What on earth is happening?

**坎吉拉**：你听我说！\
**Kanjira**: Li- ... listen to me!

坎吉拉停下来，用手在半空中挥了个巨大的圆。\
Kanjira stops, drawing a huge circle in the air with her hands.

**坎吉拉**：我在神庙的石窟里被一个石头手拽住了脚腕！还遇到了“寻宝小队”！我偷听到了他们说话……\
**Kanjira**: I'm, I'm catch by a stone hand in the shrine's cave! And, and I see the "treasure hunters"! I hear what they say.

**坎吉拉**：他们说，在几天后的烛星节上，会有那种叫“陨石”的大石头掉下来——把村子砸平！\
**Kanjira**: They say a big big stone called "meteorite" will fall and smash the village when Dīpa Festival start!

**夏尔贾老师**：唉，亲爱的，我说过那些只是故事……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: *sighs* Honey, I told you they are just fairy tales.

**坎吉拉**：不是！是真的！那石像真的动了……\
**Kanjira**: No! It's true! Those statues actually move.

坎吉拉在这栋老屋里急得团团转，没留意到屋外的脚步声愈来愈近。\
Inside the old house, Kanjira is so busy persuading Sherjah that she has not noticed the approaching footsteps from outside the door.

**鬃毛沙砾**：哦，这门锁都坏了。但没关系……这位置我绝不会记错，尽管库玛尔后来也没使用过几次，但是总比漫无目的地找——\
**Shamane**: Ah, the lock's broken, but that's okay. I know the place well. Though Kumar hasn't come here very often in the past years, it's a good place to start with, at least better than randomly searching like a headless chicken.

**坎吉拉**：……！\
**Kanjira**: ...!

**玛蒂尔达**：……\
**Matilda**: ...

**夏尔贾老师**：你们是……？\
**Ms. Sherjah**: You are ...?

隔着老屋院门，两队人马面面相觑。\
The two groups look at each other in silence through the door.

玛蒂尔达的视线在沉默中滑向夏尔贾手中的皮夹。\
As the silence goes on, Matilda notices the wallet in Sherjah's hand.

**玛蒂尔达**：嘿！\
**Matilda**: Hey!

**玛蒂尔达**：你手上的那个——那个是我的钱包吗？\
**Matilda**: That in your hand ... Is that my wallet?

## JMP-06 银手镯 / The Silver Bangle

破旧的小屋在众人的衬托下显得更加逼仄。\
Crowded by these many people, the old house seems even shabbier.

五个人围坐在唯一一张可以称之为“桌子”的家具旁。尴尬像只灵巧的雀儿，在众人的头顶上盘旋。\
The five of them sit around a piece of furniture that can barely be used as a table. The awkwardness surrounds them like a naughty bird.

**夏尔贾老师**：感谢你们的原谅，鬃毛沙砾先生、玛蒂尔达小姐。\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Thank you so much for your understanding, Mr. Sharma and Ms. Bouanich.

**鬃毛沙砾**：哈，别这么说，女士，对于您义务照顾这群孩子的行为我只有钦佩——况且这间屋子，从名义上来说早就已经不属于我了。\
**Shamane**: Ah, please, Madam. You have my admiration for voluntarily taking care of these kids. Besides, technically speaking, this room doesn't belong to me anymore ...

**鬃毛沙砾**：现在，它仍是属于库玛尔——我姐姐的东西……啊，但你们刚才也听旁边的这位小姐说了……\
**Shamane**: ... but to my sister, Kumar. I wish I could leave the house to you for future use.

他伸手示意一旁的伽菈波那。\
He gestures for Kaalaa Baunaa.

**鬃毛沙砾**：如果可以，真希望这之后房子还能给你们用！但是，以现在的状况……我可不太确定这儿能不能抵挡住一颗陨石。\
**Shamane**: But you heard what the lady said—I don't even know if the house will survive the meteor.

这不是一个开玩笑的好时机。寂静之中，众人不约而同地思考着可能到来的危机。\
This is probably not the best time for a sense of humor. Everyone in the room falls into silence. The coming crisis makes them heavy in mind.

椅子显然是这个空间的奢侈品，几人只能坐在积了一层灰的地面上。男人变戏法儿似的从自己的行李里掂出了几只泥陶制的杯子。\
They sit on the dusted ground. Shamane magically takes out several ceramic cups from his luggage.

**鬃毛沙砾**：新鲜的大吉岭～前几日我徒步时那边村里人给的好东西，哦呦，小心烫……\
**Shamane**: This is the latest batch of Darjeeling tea. Some locals gave it to me when I went across their village. Ah, careful. It's hot.

男人伸手试探了一下杯壁的温度，缓缓将陶杯们一一推了出去。\
He touches a cup to feel its temperature and passes out the cups one by one.

玛蒂尔达却一把抢过坎吉拉的杯子，气愤填膺。\
Matilda snatches Kanjira's cup angrily.

**玛蒂尔达**：你竟然和那个小子是一伙的！好哇，原来从一开始你就想骗我！\
**Matilda**: You two are in it together? You've been lying to me all this time?!

**坎吉拉**：哎呀，在夏尔贾面前你小声点……\
**Kanjira**: Hey, quiet before Ms. Sherjah.

**坎吉拉**：大小姐，你又没吃什么亏，就别再和我计较啦～你先把饼干递给我，我吃饱了还要去忙活呢！\
**Kanjira**: You don't lose anything, my lady. Please forgive me, will you? Now pass me cookies! I need fill my belly and get to work!

**伽菈波那**：很抱歉，夏尔贾女士。我明白这一切非常突然。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: My apologies, Ms. Sherjah. I know this is totally out of the blue.

伽菈波那再次将那些文件拿了出来。显然，她为了说服他人已经做了尽可能充足的准备。\
Kaalaa Baunaa takes out her files again. She has carefully prepared herself to persuade the others.

**伽菈波那**：尽管确切的数据还有待考证……但时间是目前最宝贵的东西，而等待则是最愚蠢的做法。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: And the details are yet to be verified, but our valuable time is running out. The last thing we should do is keep on waiting.

**夏尔贾老师**：唔……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Emm.

她的目光滑过一行行晦涩的数据与身份证明。\
Her gaze sweeps the difficult and obscure data and words.

**夏尔贾老师**：伽菈波那……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Kaalaa Baunaa.

她突然露出一个笑容。\
Her face suddenly brightens up.

**夏尔贾老师**：噢，我认识这个名字！你和希玛妮教授发布过的那篇论文我曾读过……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: My! I think I know this name! I've read the paper co-authored by you and Professor Himani.

**伽菈波那**：……？你读过我的论文？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Huh? You've read my paper?

**夏尔贾老师**：噢，呃……是的！我目前在昌迪加尔的一所公立大学借读……在那边，我常能接触到一些新鲜东西。\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Emm, yeah! I'm studying in a public university in Chandigarh. I get to learn a lot of new stuff there.

**夏尔贾老师**：曾有一段时间，我对天文学产生了一些兴趣……我记得，那好像是在一本期刊上见到的。\
**Ms. Sherjah**: I had a whim to study astronomy before, and I remember reading it in a periodical.

年轻女孩用手比划着文件上的数据。\
She gesticulates at the papers.

**夏尔贾老师**：啊，是的，是你的名字……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Yes, I'm sure it's the same name.

**夏尔贾老师**：这些……还有这些！我曾见过相似的东西。呃，不过旁边的这部分……我还从没见过……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: This part and this part! I've read them in your paper, but emm, this one on the side, I don't know anything like it.

**伽菈波那**：没关系，那是涉及神秘学的部分。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: It's okay. That one involves the knowledge of arcanum.

伽菈波那微微放松了身体。\
Kaalaa Baunaa relaxes a bit.

**伽菈波那**：这样就太好了，太好了……但你在这里是因为……？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Anyway, this is good news—no, great news. So what are you doing in Mor Pankh?

**夏尔贾老师**：我在没课的时候会过来这边照顾孩子们……他们大多是人类……也有少量神秘学家的孩子。\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Oh, I take care of the kids here in my spare time. Most of them are humans, but there are arcanists, too.

**坎吉拉**：……\
**Kanjira**: ...

**伽菈波那**：原来如此。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I see.

**夏尔贾老师**：唔，那现在你们准备怎么做呢？\
**Ms. Sherjah**: So, what are you going to do now?

夏尔贾的声音里除了困惑，还有一丝担忧。\
Her question contains both confusion and worry.

**夏尔贾老师**：让村子里的大家尽快离开确实是目前最正确的选择……距离烛星节还有不到四天，我们的时间并不多。但……村子里的情况——有点特殊。\
**Ms. Sherjah**: I know the top priority is to evacuate the villagers, but we don't have much time since the Dīpa Festival will start in less than four days. Besides, things are complicated in this village.

她皱起眉头，像是想到了非常棘手的事。\
She frowns at the thought. This could be tricky.

**夏尔贾老师**：这村中的大部分家庭——比如我——早就搬到了昌迪加尔。\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Most of them, including me, had moved to Chandigarh.

**夏尔贾老师**：剩下的……唉……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: And the rest of them ... *sighs*

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

**伽菈波那**：在来时的路上，我有所耳闻。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I've heard about that on the way here.

**伽菈波那**：大多数村民都十分抗拒离开这里，我尝试过游说那些看上去年轻一点的神秘学家……但很可惜，也并没有什么效果。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Most villagers are reluctant to leave, no matter what I say. I tried by starting with those young arcanists, but shame! It didn't work at all.

**伽菈波那**：但好在玛蒂尔达小姐会为我们提供帮助。我们会想办法尽快与基金会取得联系。不过目前，我仍认为村里能离开的人越多越好……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: The silver lining is, we have the helping hand of Ms. Bouanich. She will try to make contact with the Foundation as soon as possible. But we still need to evacuate every villager we can.

**夏尔贾老师**：……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: ...

**伽菈波那**：我们现在对库玛尔知之甚少……至于她人在何处，又抱有怎样的心思……我们还无法提供确切的信息。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: We know almost nothing about Kumar's plan now, not to mention her whereabouts or purpose.

尽管尴尬缓和了许多，但气氛并没有向轻松的方向发展。\
The ice has been broken between them, but their moods have not yet lightened.

**鬃毛沙砾**：别紧张，现在的情况下，我们仍然还有两条出路——\
**Shamane**: Relax. For now, we have two solutions to the problem.

鬃毛沙砾举起两只手，掌心向上。\
Shamane raises both of his hands, palms up.

**鬃毛沙砾**：一，找到我那个聪明的坏姐姐，这样我们的天文学家就能有办法，阻止那颗星星；二，让这儿的所有人，乘坐最早一班的火车，尽快离开这里！\
**Shamane**: First, let's find my clever, evil sister so that our astronomer friend can figure out a way to stop the meteor. Or, spread the word and tell everyone to take the earliest train and leave the impact area!

**鬃毛沙砾**：不能说是乐观，至少还算有点方法，能让它看上去没那么糟～\
**Shamane**: It's hard to be optimistic given the situation, but at least there is something we can do to reduce the damage.

**鬃毛沙砾**：但是再拖下去可就不一定了，来吧，让我们想想……\
**Shamane**: But if we continue to sit around waiting, the situation will only worsen. Come, let's think.

屋外的野地杂草丛生，玛蒂尔达站在一处相对空旷的地面，小心翼翼地从口袋里掏出来一个银色的电子机械。\
Bushes and weeds grow throughout the yard. Matilda finds a relatively open area, taking out a silver device from her pocket with great caution.

熟悉地形的夏尔贾与坎吉拉早已匆匆行在疏散村民的路上。而寻找库玛尔线索的两人正将老屋里折腾得尘土飞扬。\
Sherjah and Kanjira, the two people who are most familiar with the village, have set out to evacuate the villagers. Inside the house, Shamane and Kaalaa Baunaa are turning the room into a cloud of dust to find any possible clues about Kumar.

女孩只得躲到了院子里，履行自己“基金会调查员”的职责。\
The only quiet place left for Matilda to perform her duty as "Foundation investigator" is this long-deserted yard.

**玛蒂尔达**：很好！它终于可以派上用场啦……\
**Matilda**: Great! It finally comes in handy.

**系统音**：欢迎使用SPF-I型便携联络装置。\
**SPF-I**: SPF-Ⅰ Portable Contact Device activated. Welcome.

**系统音**：已开启神秘术验证。请保持未装备施咒术杖的状态。清晰念出屏幕上随机出现的神秘术咒语，注意声调平稳。\
**SPF-I**: Arcane skill verification activated. Please make sure you are not equipped with any wands. Read out the random incantation displayed on the screen clearly. Make sure your tone remains stable.

**玛蒂尔达**：咳咳……火光灼灼。\
**Matilda**: Ahem, Fuego Burn.

**系统音**：……验证成功。登录人员：玛蒂尔达·布翁尼。目前开放权限等级——D。\
**SPF-I**: Verification success. Registered user: Matilda Bouanich. Access level: D.

**系统音**：目前，您的周边未发现异常神秘学波动。D级权限范围内仅支持快速汇报功能。\
**SPF-I**: No abnormal arcane skill fluctuation detected in the area so far. Level D access only supports Quick Report.

**玛蒂尔达**：嗯？权限不足？！说明页在……啊，意思是，只有调查员才能用它申请支援。\
**Matilda**: Hmm? Insufficient access?! The description says ... Ah, so only an investigator can request backup through this system.

**玛蒂尔达**：那我一直带着它有什么意义嘛，还以为可以在关键时刻派上用场……\
**Matilda**: So what's the point of carrying it around all along? I thought it would be useful for emergencies.

**玛蒂尔达**：呜，天体能量泡汤了不说，这下不是连抓住重塑都没有机会了？\
**Matilda**: No. Does this mean I will miss the opportunity to study the celestial energy, plus blow my chance to capture the Manus?

**玛蒂尔达**：这边的通讯又糟得要命……该怎么样才能联系上基金会啊——！\
**Matilda**: The reception is terrible here. How am I going to get in touch with the Foundation!

**鬃毛沙砾**：噢，听外面那声音，她那边的进展可不太顺利。\
**Shamane**: Oh, that doesn't sound like any progress with her.

**鬃毛沙砾**：而我这儿……书之外还是书，除此之外什么都没有！\
**Shamane**: And what I have here is only books! Books and books and books. Nothing else!

**鬃毛沙砾**：《犊牛的饲养与管理》……我姐姐真的是天文学家吗？没搞错什么吧……\
**Shamane**: "Calf Feeding and Management" ... Is my sister really an astronomer? Was I mistaken about anything?

**鬃毛沙砾**：嘿！玛蒂尔达，你愿意的话，那桌子上应该还有最后两块派尔拉饼干【Plera-J】！记得泡着茶吃，不然可能会噎坏你的好嗓子——\
**Shamane**: Hey, Matilda! If you like, there should be the last two pieces of Plera-J on the table! Remember to have them with tea, or it's going to hurt your throat and ruin your beautiful voice.

**鬃毛沙砾**：坎吉拉那小崽子太能吃了，临走前还拿了三块。呼，希望那个善良的人类女孩能带着那帮小家伙顺利到火车站……\
**Shamane**: Kanjira was ecstatic about those cookies. She even took three pieces with her when she left. *sighs* I hope that kind human girl will get to the train station safely with those kids.

**鬃毛沙砾**：再瞧瞧你……这是……\
**Shamane**: Now, let's take a look at you. What are you doing?

**鬃毛沙砾**：是库玛尔留下的那块石头？\
**Shamane**: Is this the stone Kumar left to you?

伽菈波那正小心翼翼地剥开岩石的外壳，其中，一尊小小的神像渐渐显露了出来。\
Kaalaa Baunaa carefully parts the stone. An idol emerges from it.

**鬃毛沙砾**：……是毗湿奴？\
**Shamane**: Vishnu?

**伽菈波那**：由梵天创造，由湿婆毁灭，而毗湿奴横卧于宇宙海之上，维护着万物的平衡……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Brahma creates, Shiva exterminates, and Vishnu safeguards the balance of the world, lying on the Ocean of Stars.

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

**伽菈波那**：在文献……唔，对于普通人来说或许用神话来解释更合适。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: According to the materials ... Well, maybe I should explain it with mythologies for non-researchers.

**伽菈波那**：神话中曾提及了三尊神像，但在她留下的东西里我只见到了这个。想必另外两尊在她那里。或许……这也证明了库玛尔早就放弃了中间的道路。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: They mentioned three idols, but Vishnu's is the only one left, so she must have taken the other two. Perhaps it's proof that Kumar abandoned the path of maintaining the balance in the first place.

**伽菈波那**：那个石窟里面的壁画——她和我说过，她家族曾一直传颂着它……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: That mural there ... She said the mythology on it has been passed down in her family.

**鬃毛沙砾**：唉，那倒是。那个故事我至少背过二十回……壁画讲述的那段，说实话，没头没尾的！\
**Shamane**: *sighs* That's true. I've recited that story at least 20 times, but the part on the mural, to be honest, it feels so out of place to me.

**鬃毛沙砾**：它就那么被突兀地塞进那些传颂得更广的神话里，唔……就像给马的脑袋上安了一副牛角……\
**Shamane**: It was more like foisted into those well-known myths, like, emm, a pair of ox horns on a horse's head.

伽菈波那微笑着摇了摇头。\
The comparison brings a smile to Kaalaa Baunaa's face. But she shakes her head.

**伽菈波那**：奇妙的比喻。但实际上，它正是连结起诸多神话的重要一环。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: An unusual metaphor. But actually, it plays a significant part in connecting all the mythologies we know.

**伽菈波那**：我们一直以来将这些神话作为研究的蓝本，试图用基础神秘学理论去反证人类科学。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: These mythologies are the primary material of our research. We've been trying to prove human science with basic arcanum theory.

**伽菈波那**：二者之间确实存在着关联，它们之间相辅相成……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: In fact, there is a connection between them, and they can support each other.

她叹了口气。\
She sighs.

**伽菈波那**：如果两个族群不是如今那么水火不容的状态……我想，我们生存的世界可能会进步得更快。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: If arcanists and humans could get along, I suppose the world would have developed faster than it does now.

感受到对方困惑的目光，女人似乎在重新编排准备说出口的词句。\
Sensing Shamane's confusion, Kaalaa Baunaa pauses to reorganize her language.

**伽菈波那**：唔，具体情况想要三言两语解释清楚会非常困难，但简单来说，有另外一个如同鸽卵的宇宙影响着现实世界。我们通常称之为“幻境”……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: It's not easy to explain it through, but in short, there is another universe in the shape of an egg affecting reality. We call it the Meditator's Realm.

**伽菈波那**：就像我们通常会做的梦一样。沉睡，你便进入了那个地方……而我们则是用一些特殊的冥想方式，将自己的一部分灵知与其相连。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Just like our daily dreams, you can enter it once you fall asleep, but that's not how we do it. We connect part of our Gnosis with the Realm through a special kind of meditation.

**伽菈波那**：这并非像听起来的一样轻松，要么像我们一样掌握纯熟的技巧，要么利用特殊的介质作为锚点……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: It's not as easy as it sounds. One needs to either master the meditation skills like we do or use a special medium as an anchor.

她抬起手，示意着手中的毗湿奴神像。\
She raises her hand, showing the Vishnu idol to them.

**伽菈波那**：某些神话便是最初对幻境的解析代码，只要与现实一一对应，就可以找到那些原本不在这个世界视野内的存在——我们就是这样定位到了那颗天体。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Some mythologies are the original translation of the Realm. An existence that cannot be observed through the methods in this world can be located as long as it is included in mythology. That's how we located that star.

**伽菈波那**：只是很可惜，如果不用人类科技所呈现的实际数据来证明，我们的发现就是一纸空谈。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Sadly, if we can't prove its existence with data recorded by human technology, our discovery is useless.

**鬃毛沙砾**：……没想到她从未放弃有关我们家族的神秘学研究。\
**Shamane**: I'm surprised. For all this time, she has never given up on studying the old arcanum tale of our family.

**伽菈波那**：她甚至热衷于此。可是……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: You can even say she's fanatic about it. It's just ...

伽菈波那皱起眉头。\
Kaalaa Baunaa frowns.

**伽菈波那**：尽管在幻境里我们能做到很多超出现实中的事——如果你的心绪足够平稳，或者锚点足够扎实，你甚至可以在幻境里为所欲为，但这仅限在其内部。\
