**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Indeed, we can do a lot of supernatural things in the Realm. If your mind is calm or your anchor is strong enough, you can even do whatever you want. But it's limited inside there.

**伽菈波那**：还记得我说它像梦吗？那最多算是可以自行控制的梦……幻境里的一切基于现实而生——它才是“镜子”，理应不存在影响现实的可能性。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Remember I said it's like our daily dreams? Just think of it as a controllable one. Everything in the Realm is created based on reality. In other words, it's nothing but a "mirror," and the images in a mirror can never affect reality.

**伽菈波那**：我们什么也带不进去，更不要提带出来。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: It's impossible to bring anything into the Realm, not to mention taking anything out.

**伽菈波那**：但石窟里的神像……却是实实在在，可以触碰到的。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: But the statues in the cave actually exist in this world. They are tangible.

**伽菈波那**：她的研究显然比我成功多了——她掌握了我并不知道的方法。但我不明白，她的神秘学能力……如果不是重塑之手的帮助，她又是怎么……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: That means she's gone much further than I do. She mastered a method I'm not aware of. What bewilders me is her arcane skill. How did she do that if not for the Manus's help?

**鬃毛沙砾**：哦，别太伤心，她对那个石窟不是也比我要熟悉多了？\
**Shamane**: Oh, c'mon, she also knows that cave a lot better than I do, right?

男人走到一边，随手翻开了书堆最上方的一本《地下生存手册》。\
Shamane goes to the book pile on the other side of the room and casually opens the Underground Survival Guide on top.

**鬃毛沙砾**：我与她相处的时间并不长。也许有一个月，或者是半个月？我还把她的眼镜坐坏了——喏，就是你腰上的那个。\
**Shamane**: We never hung out much. How long did she stay in the village on her last visit? A month maybe, or two weeks? I'm not sure. I even crushed her glasses by accidentally sitting on them. Those are the same glasses you have on your belt.

**鬃毛沙砾**：当时我还以为她是哪来的远房亲戚，在这个村子里难得有那样聪明、眼界又开阔的家伙，我还把这间屋子借给她——嗐，这里当初可是我自己的秘密基地！\
**Shamane**: At that time, I thought she was a distant relative I don't know of. After all, it's rare to meet someone so clever and open-minded in this village. I even lent this room to her. *sighs* This was my secret basement, you know!

**鬃毛沙砾**：结果，直到和她告别之后，我才从我父亲那里得知，那个人竟然是我的亲姐姐，被他们嫌弃神秘学天赋平平，亲手送出去的好女儿！\
**Shamane**: But only after we parted did my father tell me that she's my sister—the daughter they sent away for lack of arcanum talent!

**伽菈波那**：……关于那段时间，我有些印象。那时候我去研究所，总是见不到她的身影，有很长一段时间，我都是独自一个人。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I do remember those days roughly. Back then, I couldn't find her in the institution. I was all alone for a long time.

**鬃毛沙砾**：总之……这件事不可避免地成为了我日后叛逆的一颗种火——\
**Shamane**: What happened to her has inevitably affected me. I grew more and more rebellious against the family rules.

**鬃毛沙砾**：一个讲起来很经典的故事：我放弃那些训练，懒得听我父亲的教诲，逃避一切可逃避的练习，死活不想当那个被所谓“继承”束缚住的蠢人！\
**Shamane**: It's like a story full of cliches: giving up the training, refusing to listen to my father, skipping all the practice I could possibly avoid. I didn't want to be the blockhead hedged by the so-called "family heritage"!

**鬃毛沙砾**：当然，故事的最后——我仍然为此付出了代价。\
**Shamane**: Of course, at the end of the story, I paid my price for breaking away.

他抬了抬那只做工粗糙的手臂，翻书的手停了下来。\
He raises the rough prosthesis and stops turning the pages.

**鬃毛沙砾**：……不过我想，她可能比我更加难越过那座高墙。\
**Shamane**: But I think, for her, it is even harder to break free.

他从那本书中轻轻拿起一张纸片。\
He gently takes out a photo from the book.

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

**鬃毛沙砾**：我猜，她的计划是将我“邀请”到这里——到这个给她带来烂回忆的坏地方，再用一颗星星“咻——”地一下把我们这些让她心烦意乱的东西一口气解决掉！\
**Shamane**: I guess her plan is to "invite" me over to this dump full of bad memories, and "Swoosh ... BOOM!" Smash all the annoyances with a star.

**鬃毛沙砾**：嗯……挺有仪式感的！但很可惜，她恨的那些家伙早就不在啦……\
**Shamane**: Hmm. That's a solemn ending! Pity the ones she hates are all gone now.

伽菈波那接过他递过来的相片。\
Kaalaa Baunaa takes the photo from him.

**鬃毛沙砾**：但你为什么也被邀请了……你也得罪她了？\
**Shamane**: But, how come you're invited, too? Did you upset her as well?

**伽菈波那**：唔……这么说的话，仇恨或许确实是最有可能的原因。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Hmm. That's a good point. Hatred could be the most likely reason.

**伽菈波那**：其实……我们在离开大学之后，关系并不融洽。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Actually, we didn't get along well after we left the university.

伽菈波那的指尖轻轻碰了碰相片中的女孩。\
Kaalaa Baunaa touches the girl in the photo with her fingertip.

**伽菈波那**：从我们二人的神秘学家身份暴露之后，就很难继续在研究所待下去了。也是那时候，我们之间有了分歧……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Ever since our identities as arcanists were exposed, we couldn't stay in the institution anymore. That's also the beginning of our disagreement.

**伽菈波那**：我总以为，在证明自己——在证明我们自己的这条路上，彼此是对方唯一的朋友、最棒的同僚。没有她，我又怎么能在那个满是人类的大学里坚持下来呢？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I always thought that, on the way to proving myself, ourselves, we were each other's only friend and best partner. How could I finish my study in campus full of humans without her?

小小的神像躺在手心，有着微凉的触感。\
The small idol in her palm is a bit cool to the touch.

**伽菈波那**：可是那之后就变了……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: But then my mind was changed.

她的声音低了下去。\
Her voice lowers.

**伽菈波那**：……如果只是希玛妮的几句话，我是不会把库玛尔和重塑联系到一起的。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I wouldn't have connected Kumar with Manus Vindictae, if Himani's words were all I heard.

**伽菈波那**：但我知道，那并不是他们第一次接触。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: But I know that was not the first time they made contact.

**鬃毛沙砾**：你是说……\
**Shamane**: You mean ...

**伽菈波那**：是的，重塑之手在很早之前就联系过她，我不知道是什么吸引到了那些人……她当时把他们拒之门外，但我感觉得到，在那之后她就变了。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Yes. I don't know the reason, but the Manus has contacted her long ago. She gave them the cold shoulder at the time, but I knew something inside her had changed.

**伽菈波那**：那之后不久……她便带着所有的研究资料离开了我。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Soon after that, she left me, taking all the materials with her.

**鬃毛沙砾**：……\
**Shamane**: ...

**伽菈波那**：我知道，唯一能让我们再次相遇的方式就是……我也继续在研究那颗天体的道路上走下去。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I know the only thing I can do to meet her again is keep walking on the way to study that celestial body. That will lead me to her one day.

**伽菈波那**：我之前说过，我们常能通过这颗天体察觉彼此的存在……她能察觉到的比我更多。因为研究的特殊性，神秘术留下的痕迹总是更明显些。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: As I said, we could frequently feel the existence of each other from the changes of the celestial body, but she could always find more information than I do, because the traces left by arcanum are more obvious than those left by science.

**伽菈波那**：我就是这样坚信着，也以这种方式告诉她：总有一天，我们能重新以同僚的形式相逢。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: This connection between us conveyed my belief to her that one day we would meet again as colleagues.

**伽菈波那**：……只是没想到，走到尽头，我的观测会为我带来这样的结果……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I just didn't expect that this would be the final outcome of my observation ...

**伽菈波那**：……也没想到我们会成为彼此的对立面。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ... or that we would end up on the opposite sides.

**鬃毛沙砾**：唔……\
**Shamane**: Emm.

**鬃毛沙砾**：真是两个不适合当故事讲的……故事！\
**Shamane**: Can there be any lamer stories to tell than these two?

**伽菈波那**：……目前看来，在她的屋子里也没什么线索，或许我们应该再去一次神庙？你关于家族里的那个神话还记得多少，我们当初的研究……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: For now, we can't find more clues in her house. Maybe we should go to the shrine again? How much do you remember the myth of your family? As I just said, that was the primary material of our study.

**玛蒂尔达**：啊哈！我真是——天才！天才玛蒂尔达！\
**Matilda**: Ah-ha! A geeenius you are, Matilda!

**鬃毛沙砾**：哈哈，举着茶杯四处蹦跳……我能理解这样的乐趣……\
**Shamane**: Hahaha, running and jumping around with hot tea. I sure know the fun within.

**鬃毛沙砾**：但以我现在的年纪，我只能说注意安全，这很容易烫到你自己……\
**Shamane**: But at my age, with the benefit of hindsight, I have to tell you to be careful. You might get burned by the tea.

**玛蒂尔达**：不，不！是香料，里面的香料！\
**Matilda**: No, no! It's the spice! The spice in the tea!

**鬃毛沙砾**：还要再加些？唔……我大概随身携带十几种，你看起来很习惯……\
**Shamane**: More spice to it? Hmm. I do have a dozen kinds of different spices with me. Looks like you are very used to them in tea.

**玛蒂尔达**：没错，就是香料——\
**Matilda**: Exactly, these spices!

金发女孩得意地拍了拍自己的胸膛。\
Matilda pats herself on the chest proudly.

**玛蒂尔达**：现在是玛蒂尔达的回合了！\
**Matilda**: Now it's time for Matilda to show you her best shot!

**玛蒂尔达**：水晶球……小茴香……哦！你这里还有公丁香！太好了。\
**Matilda**: The orb, cumin ... Oh! You also have clove blossom here! Fantastic.

伽菈波那拈起一颗剔透的蓝色水晶。\
Kaalaa Baunaa picks up a transparent blue crystal to look at it.

**伽菈波那**：这就是水晶占卜……我和人类接触得太多又太长久，竟忘记了神秘学是这样方便的东西。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: The crystal divination. I've spent too much time in the human world to remember the convenience of arcanum.

**玛蒂尔达**：只要看到有关库玛尔的一点点预兆……一切就能迎刃而解！\
**Matilda**: If I can foresee any sign about Kumar, our problem will be ended!

**玛蒂尔达**：——当然，是在玛蒂尔达的英明指引下！\
**Matilda**: With the help of the great Matilda, of course!

**玛蒂尔达**：好的，深呼吸……我需要你们把手掌叠在我的手心上——没错，就是这样。\
**Matilda**: Hmm, okay, take a deep breath, give me your hands, rest them on top of mine. Yes, like that.

**玛蒂尔达**：现在，想象着你们脑海里的库玛尔……\
**Matilda**: Now, think of Kumar in your head.

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

**鬃毛沙砾**：……\
**Shamane**: ...

**玛蒂尔达**：……？\
**Matilda**: ...?

**玛蒂尔达**：奇怪……呼……\
**Matilda**: Odd ...

**伽菈波那**：……！\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...!

**鬃毛沙砾**：……？\
**Shamane**: ...?

**玛蒂尔达**：这，这是什么……这是那个火车站？\
**Matilda**: What, what is this? Is that the train station?

水晶球中的雾气不减反增，翻滚着，凝聚成一团黑色。\
Instead of showing the sign as usual, the fog in the orb grows unexpectedly. It surges and gathers into a mass of black slime.

**玛蒂尔达**：……！\
**Matilda**: ...!

**玛蒂尔达**：这是……\
**Matilda**: There are ...

玛蒂尔达猛地睁开双眼。\
Matilda snaps open her eyes.

**玛蒂尔达**：重塑……已经到摩卢旁卡了？！\
**Matilda**: The Manus already reached Mor Pankh?!

## JMP-07 泪水壶 / Drown in Tears

**坎吉拉**：快点，阿贾尔！叫上那些家伙也来！开着三轮赶紧去车站……我的大篷车上还能塞下几个！\
**Kanjira**: Hurry up, Ajar! Bring those guys, too! Take the tuk tuk to the train station. Here are a few spots in my caravan!

**阿贾尔**：好的，坎吉拉大姐!\
**Ajar**: Yes, Boss!

**坎吉拉**：不，等等，夏尔贾呢……怎么那么久？她没跟你们一起吗？\
**Kanjira**: No, wait. Where's Sherjah! What took her so long? Wasn't she with you?

**阿贾尔**：她……我刚刚看到夏尔贾老师去了村子的那边……\
**Ajar**: She ... I saw her went to the other side of the village.

**坎吉拉**：那边？那边我记得是……\
**Kanjira**: Over there? I remember that's ...

**坎吉拉**：……啧！\
**Kanjira**: Tsk!

**夏尔贾老师**：先生，您一定要相信我……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Sir, please, please trust me.

年轻的女人轻轻晃了晃脑袋，脸上写满了恳求。\
She wobbles her head while begging with sincerity.

**夏尔贾老师**：您一定要尝试说服您的父亲，这次与以往情况不一样……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: You have to convince your father. It's not like before.

**村民**：唉……夏尔贾，不是我不愿意和我父亲去说。\
**Rajesh**: *sighs* Sherjah, it's not that I don't want to talk to my father.

男人弯腰，将手中的蜡烛安置在地上，与台阶前的蜡烛群组成了整齐的一列。\
He bends over to place the candle before the stairs, lining it up neatly with the other candles.

**村民**：这已经是你第……不知道多少次来找我了。我父亲那边……就因为我让吉娜跟着你念那些乱七八糟的书本已经骂了我好几回！\
**Rajesh**: You have come to me ... I don't know, so many times. Father has already scolded me several times for letting Jina learn all those unorthodox stuff from you.

**村民**：你知道，就那些人类玩意儿……\
**Rajesh**: You know, those human books ...

他皱着眉头，满脸不悦。\
His eyebrows furrow, and his face grows red with anger.

**村民**：你看，现在，她妈妈在厨房也少了个好帮手——烛星节的星烛甚至要我亲自来准备！\
**Rajesh**: You can see, even Jina's mother has no help in the kitchen now. I even have to prepare the candles for Dīpa Festival myself!

**村民**：不管你这次说什么，我都不会再接受你的建议，我劝你在我父亲出来之前尽快离开。你也知道他看到人类会发什么样的疯……\
**Rajesh**: No matter what you say, I'm not taking your advice this time. You'd better leave before my father comes out. You know how mad he gets when he sees a human.

**老年村民**：嘿，拉杰什，你和谁嘟嘟囔囔呢——你，怎么又是你？！\
**Takal**: Hey Rajesh, who are you talking to? You, you again?!

**夏尔贾老师**：老先生，您先听我说……这次事态紧急，我……尽管我没办法与您细说，但这个村子就快被陨石毁了，您一定要带着家人尽快离开……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Sir, please listen to me. It's an emergency. I can't tell you the details now, but in a word, this village is going to be destroyed by meteorites! You and your family need to leave here now.

**老年村民**：去去，这样的话术你们至少用了十几回。别以为我们不知道你那点小心思，想让我们从这儿挪走？门儿都没有。\
**Takal**: Enough! You've played that trick a dozen times. We know what you are up to! Trying to get us out of this place? No way!

**村民**：父亲……您也别这么说，您也知道夏尔贾她一直……\
**Rajesh**: Please, Father. You know Sherjah has been ...

**老年村民**：这儿没你说话的份！你走不走？不走我就要……\
**Takal**: I am talking to her! Leave now, or I'll ...

老人抄起了门框处的扫帚。\
The old man snatches the broom from next to the door.

没人注意远处越来越清晰的奔跑声。\
No one pays attention to the running steps coming from afar.

**坎吉拉**：喷吉！拦住他！\
**Kanjira**: Punji! Stop him!

**喷吉**：嘶——\
**Punji**: Hiss!

**老年村民**：唔啊啊！哪里来的小鬼……你……你怎么敢帮着人类……\
**Takal**: Oh, oh, ah! Who are you, kid? Why ... why are you on human's side?

**夏尔贾老师**：坎吉拉！\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Kanjira!

**坎吉拉**：怎么，我不帮她，我帮你这种猪猡吗？不识好歹的老家伙！\
**Kanjira**: What, who else should I help if not her? You? An ungrateful old pig?

黑发女孩挤进二人中间，像只鳞片立起的小蛇。\
Kanjira squeezes in between them and confronts the old villager, like an upright snake ready to attack.

**老年村民**：你——\
**Takal**: You ...

**坎吉拉**：夏尔贾帮了你们多少次，吉娜跟夏尔贾又学了多少东西！你们只知道天天抓着她找麻烦，把神秘学家、人类挂在嘴边！\
**Kanjira**: How many times has Sherjah helped you, and how many things did Jina learn from her? You! You only know being mean to her and talking about something like arcanists and humans!

**坎吉拉**：你爱跑不跑！夏尔贾好心帮你们，一个两个不识好歹！让星星把你们都砸死算啦！\
**Kanjira**: Stay if you like! Sherjah is being so nice and saving your life, but no one is clever enough to listen! Better let the star fall on you and crush you into ashes!

**坎吉拉**：我们走！\
**Kanjira**: Let's go!

**夏尔贾老师**：真是抱歉，这孩子——\
**Ms. Sherjah**: I'm so sorry. She ...

**夏尔贾老师**：啊！\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Aah!

坎吉拉没再说一个字，她一把抓住夏尔贾的手腕，用尽全身的力气拉着她离开了。\
Without saying another word, Kanjira seizes Sherjah's arm and drags her away.

**夏尔贾老师**：坎吉拉，停下，别，你拉疼我了……！\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Kanjira, stop! Don't pull me! It hurts.

女孩收住脚步，胸膛因为愤怒剧烈地起伏着。\
Kanjira makes a sudden stop. Her chest is pumping up and down out of anger.

**坎吉拉**：……你都被他们那些人欺负多少次了，为什么还要过去找不痛快？\
**Kanjira**: They is always mean to you and bullying you! Why you must look for trouble?

**夏尔贾老师**：坎吉拉……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Kanjira ...

**坎吉拉**：你明明，一直是为他们好……他们怎么可以这样对你……你，你不要管他们了！快和我走，我这边还留了你的位置……\
**Kanjira**: After all the things you do for them, how can they treat you like that?! Just leave them alone! Come with me. I still have your spot on my caravan.

**坎吉拉**：车站每天进出火车的时间都是一样的！我记得很清楚……很快会有一列火车离开这里，现在一切都来得及……\
**Kanjira**: The time for entering and exiting the trains of the station is the same every day! I remember it well. There will be a train leaving here soon. There is still time.

**夏尔贾老师**：……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: ...

**夏尔贾老师**：坎吉拉，你先深呼吸——你听我说。\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Kanjira, take a deep breath and listen to me.

年轻的女人察觉到了女孩的情绪。她微微蹲下身子，轻轻地拉着她的手摇晃。\
Sherjah becomes conscious of her student's emotions. She bends down to the level of Kanjira's eyes, shaking her arms to reassure her.

**坎吉拉**：……\
**Kanjira**: ...

**夏尔贾老师**：我知道你是为我好，为我着想，才对他们说出这种话，我不怪你。\
**Ms. Sherjah**: I know you said all those things to them for me, and I appreciate that.

**夏尔贾老师**：但是，如果我也做了与他们同样的事，就这样眼睁睁地、放任他们失去性命——\
**Ms. Sherjah**: But think about it, if I treat them just the same way they treated me, just stand by and watch them head to death ...

她斟酌着词句，像是每次为他们讲解英语单词一样尽可能放慢着语速。\
Sherjah chooses her words carefully, as patient as she used to be in every English class.

**夏尔贾老师**：尽管我愤怒的情绪如此合理，可是这样，我与他们又有什么区别？\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Even if I'm doing this out of understandable fury, how would it make me any different to them?

**坎吉拉**：……！\
**Kanjira**: ...!

**夏尔贾老师**：无论是我帮助你们，还是我现在——你眼中的，“拯救”他们……这都不过是在践行我自己的意志罢了。\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Volunteering to help you, and, in your opinion, "risking my life to save them" ... They are all out of my own will.

**夏尔贾老师**：仇恨是不会无故停止的，坎吉拉，总要有人从自己开始停止这一切。\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Hatred doesn't end itself, Kanjira. It has to be ended by someone.

女孩仍旧困惑的目光在夏尔贾的脸上停留了片刻，缓缓移到了自己的足尖。\
Kanjira stares at her teacher's face in confusion. Slowly, she lowers her eyes and looks down at her feet.

**坎吉拉**：……不，我不懂……\
**Kanjira**: I, I don't understand.

**坎吉拉**：我在……我们在你眼里，就如此不重要吗？\
**Kanjira**: Do I ... Do we mean nothing to you?

**夏尔贾老师**：怎么会！你怎么会这样想？你们是我最重要的孩子……你们……你们都是我的宝物啊！\
**Ms. Sherjah**: How come?! What gave you such an idea? You are my most precious children. All of you are my treasures!

**坎吉拉**：你已经不是第一次选择他们了……\
**Kanjira**: This is not the first time you prefer they over we.

**坎吉拉**：每次遇到问题，你总是优先考虑那些家伙……\
**Kanjira**: You always put they first when there's a problem.

她明白这不是夏尔贾的错。\
She knows well that Sherjah should not be blamed for this.

但这并不能缓解一份被拒绝的酸涩。\
But this doesn't relieve her of the bitterness.

**夏尔贾老师**：……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: ...

**夏尔贾老师**：坎吉拉，你……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Kanjira ...

**坎吉拉**：我，我是不识字，但我已经不是个小孩子了。如果可以……我宁愿自己也不是个神秘学家……这样我和你，和阿贾尔他们就一样了……\
**Kanjira**: I, I am not able to read, but I'm not a kid now. If I can, I don't want to be an arcanist too, so me, you, and Ajar is the same.

这个时候并不适合说这些。\
They have no time for this.

坎吉拉试图努力忍住那些在眼眶里汹涌的泪水。\
Kanjira struggles to choke back the tears.

但她实在太害怕失去夏尔贾了。\
But she's overwhelmed by the fear of losing Sherjah.

**夏尔贾老师**：坎吉拉，不哭，坎吉拉……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Kanjira. Don't cry, Kanjira.

**夏尔贾老师**：原来你一直……噢，小家伙……你跟我们就是一样的呀！我们就是你的家人……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: So you've been thinking ... Oh, little one. You're just like us! We are your family!

**坎吉拉**：不，夏尔贾，你，你不懂……咳咳，嘶——别再说这些了，我，我不可能听得懂你的大道理，但你绝不能留在这里！\
**Kanjira**: No, you don't understand, Ms. Sherjah. Enough talk. Maybe I don't understand any of your lectures, but you can't stay here!

**夏尔贾老师**：……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: ...

**夏尔贾老师**：抱歉，坎吉拉……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: I'm sorry, Kanjira.

她鲜少感觉拒绝的话语如此难以启齿。\
Sherjah has never found it so difficult to refuse someone.

**夏尔贾老师**：我承认，他们的行为确实有些不可理喻……但就如同我刚才说的，现在不是计较这些的时候，你知道吗？那是生命，坎吉拉，我不能……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: I have to admit they're unreasonable, but as I said, we should put that aside now. It's a matter of life, Kanjira. I can't ...

**坎吉拉**：……\
**Kanjira**: ...

那份酸涩在胃部翻涌着——促使着坎吉拉做出冲动的决定。\
Kanjira feels her stomach churning due to the bitterness, urging her to act on impulse.

**坎吉拉**：你，根本没把我的话听进去……\
**Kanjira**: You ... you is not listening to me at all!

**坎吉拉**：算了！那你就去当你的救世主吧！我们自己走！\
**Kanjira**: Fine! Be a savior and go! We'll leave here on our own!

**夏尔贾老师**：坎吉拉！\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Kanjira!

挽留的手终究没能阻止她。夏尔贾只得眼睁睁地看着女孩消失在自己的视野里。\
Sherjah's hand only lands on empty air. Kanjira runs away and disappears from her sight.

**坎吉拉**：呜呜……呜……\
**Kanjira**: *sobbing*

女孩趴在方向盘上，用力地吸着鼻子。\
She leans on the steering wheel, sobbing.

**坎吉拉**：我，我再也不要管她了！\
**Kanjira**: I, I'm never talking to her again!

疾驰的车子停了下来，这个与小村格格不入的车站再次出现在了视野里。\
The caravan stops at the train station, which seems out of place in the small village.

**坎吉拉**：阿贾尔——！辛哈大叔——！\
**Kanjira**: Ajar! Uncle Sinha!

**坎吉拉**：奇怪，人呢？车站怎么静悄悄的……上午还有很多人啊……\
**Kanjira**: Hmm. Where are they? Why is here so quiet? It was crowded this morning.

“吧嗒。”\
*ooze*

**坎吉拉**：……这，这是……\
**Kanjira**: This, this is ...

**重塑·门徒**：ㄨㄛㄛ——！\
**Manus Disciple**: UGGGHHHH!

**坎吉拉**：……！\
**Kanjira**: ...!

**坎吉拉**：这……怎么会有这么多……血……\
**Kanjira**: Blood, so much blood ...

戴着面具的骇人怪物摇晃着，穿梭于车站的石柱间。\
The terrifying masked monsters are staggering among the stone pillars in the train station.

**坎吉拉**：不……阿贾尔——辛哈大叔——\
**Kanjira**: No! Ajar!! Uncle Sinha!!

柱子旁冒出一个机灵的脑袋。\
A smart head pokes out from behind the pillar.

**Ajar**: No idea! A bunch of dreadful people suddenly showed up. Each of them has a mask on their face. Over there, on the platform. There are a few more!

**Ajar**: They came out of nowhere and attacked the passengers for no reason.

小男孩似乎是想到什么，忍不住打了个寒噤。\
Ajar seems to be thinking of something. He can't help but shiver.

As Kanjira looks up, the first thing that comes to her tearful, blurry sight is a head with milky blonde hair.

**玛蒂尔达**：呼，呼……赶上了，还好赶上了……\
**Matilda**: *pants* Phew! So glad I caught up in time.

## JMP-08 小守护者 / The Little Guardians

巨大的菩提树伫立在宽阔的庭院中央。\
A massive sacred fig stands in the middle of the yard.

尽管它的年岁看上去比照片中的那棵久远得多，但其树冠之上毫无一物，只挺拔着光秃秃的枝丫，仿佛一具被燃烧殆尽的尸骨。\
It looks a lot older than it was in the photo, and it has become leafless, like a skeleton.

**鬃毛沙砾**：老兄弟，没想到你还在呢……\
**Shamane**: Old buddy, I'm surprised that you're still here.

His rough hands land on the equally rough bark. The tree responds with nearly imperceptible cracks.

**伽菈波那**：目前救下来的人都安置好了……没想到重塑之手的人有这么多……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: We have settled everyone so far. I didn't expect so many Manus members here.

伽菈波那看上去心有余悸。\
She's still haunted by the battle.

**鬃毛沙砾**：……库玛尔确实和重塑之手合作了。\
**Shamane**: Kumar did cooperate with the Manus.

**伽菈波那**：唔……！\

Shamane shakes his head.

**鬃毛沙砾**：那并非是一种选择，伽菈波那，你无需为自己的信任懊恼。信任有迹可寻，仇恨却从不遵从逻辑。\

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

**Shamane**: Let your guard down for even one second, the toxic idea will sneak into your mind, and it would be impossible to get rid of it.

**鬃毛沙砾**：它会灼烧你的理智，人将因此退行为一只恶兽，直到忘却自己姓甚名谁。\

**鬃毛沙砾**：它们走投无路，视野变窄，冥冥之中已知死局，却反而因此开始没来由地盲目自信，在没必要的地方孤注一掷……\
**Shamane**: It can't think of anything else, but at the same time, it strangely grows overconfident. It will take the gamble of escaping from its last way out, which is also going to be the entrance of the trap.

**鬃毛沙砾**：我很能明白那种感觉，那种眼前只剩下一条独木桥的感觉——\

She stares at his face for a long time. Eventually, she shakes her head.

**伽菈波那**：外面的重塑不知道会游荡到什么时候，还有一些村民没有被带回来。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: The Manus followers are still wandering about, and some villagers haven't been moved to safer locations.

**伽菈波那**：有些风险是必须的……在没有更好的道路出现之前，即便是陷阱，也有尝试的必要。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: But sometimes, we must take the risky path to get out of the dreadful situation, even though it is full of traps.

**鬃毛沙砾**：……\
**Shamane**: ...

他注意到了女人因紧张而反复握起又张开的手。\
He notices her fingers clutch and loosen repeatedly out of anxiety.

**伽菈波那**：即便不能解决问题，也不会全无收获。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: It may not solve all the problems, but it's better than doing nothing.

**伽菈波那**：况且……如果真的是陷阱，那就证明我一定会再次见到她。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: If this really is a trap, that means we will meet again.

**伽菈波那**：对我来说，这样直面她的机会……我渴望已久。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: And I have been waiting for a chance to talk to her face-to-face for too long.

**鬃毛沙砾**：……\
**Shamane**: ...

**伽菈波那**：自她走后，我一直在向着不存在的目标前进。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I have been chasing after an imaginary goal since she left me.

**伽菈波那**：我努力地观测夜空，记录下那颗星星……尽管我拼尽全力地寻找她，但我知道……这样漫无目的的努力毫无意义。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I watched that star closely, taking down everything that I could observe. However, despite all the efforts, deep down, I know better than anyone else—it's useless.

**伽菈波那**：我还记得那些日子，将近半途都是白茫茫的一片。可现在……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I remember those days, almost half of which were like living in a mist. But now ...

**伽菈波那**：现在……我，我感觉得到，我已经看到她的背影了。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: But now, I can feel it. Her silhouette is right there in front of me.

**伽菈波那**：……诚然，这个机会出现的时机并不算好。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: To be honest, this is not the best time to "seize this chance."

**玛蒂尔达**：伽菈波那小姐……\
**Matilda**: Ms. Kaalaa Baunaa.

**伽菈波那**：但无论站在哪个角度，我不能放弃的理由都太多了。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: But no matter how I look at it, this is too good an opportunity to pass up.

**鬃毛沙砾**：……\
**Shamane**: ...

鬃毛沙砾没有避开她直视而来的目光。\
Shamane meets her gaze squarely.

良久，他眨了眨眼睛，又败下阵来似的抠了抠脑袋。\
Then he blinks. He scratches his head, feeling a bit powerless.

**鬃毛沙砾**：唔……行吧，好吧……诶呀……\
**Shamane**: Emm. Okay. Fine. *sighs*

**鬃毛沙砾**：……如果你执意要做的话，我不会再拦你。\
**Shamane**: If you insist on doing this, I will not stop you.

**鬃毛沙砾**：毕竟谁没跌过跤呢……而且，你说得对，我们目前确实没有更好的办法。\
**Shamane**: We all have our lessons to learn. And you are right—we don't have any better options.

**鬃毛沙砾**：那句话怎么说来着？一分风险——一分收获！\
**Shamane**: What is it they say? No risk, no feast, huh?

**鬃毛沙砾**：只是你要知道，无论在里面发生了什么——请务必保护好你自己。\
**Shamane**: But please keep this in mind—no matter what happens, your safety will always be the top priority.

**鬃毛沙砾**：我们不能失去一个能把事情彻底解决的人。\
**Shamane**: We cannot bear to lose someone who is capable of putting this to an end.

**伽菈波那**：……我会的。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I will.

## JMP-09 篱笆墙之外 / Outside the Fence

人们聚在院子里的大陶缸前。\
They gather before the ceramic vat in the yard.

**鬃毛沙砾**：你确定……你要用这个东西吗？\
**Shamane**: Are you sure? To use this?

**伽菈波那**：怎么了吗？这罐子里的水刚刚好……我也正好能够进去。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: What's wrong with it? It has enough water to soak me in.

鬃毛沙砾看着破败的陶缸与其中混沌成一片的落叶与脏污，沉默了片刻。\
Shamane looks at the old vat and then checks the filthy water and rotten leaves inside. There is a silence between them.

**鬃毛沙砾**：唔，你对实用性的追求比我想象的高。\
**Shamane**: Hmm, you are much more practical than I thought.

**伽菈波那**：对了，还有……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Oh, before I go ...

伽菈波那将那枚毗湿奴神像交给了玛蒂尔达。\
She hands the Vishnu idol to Matilda.

**玛蒂尔达**：咦？伽菈波那小姐，你不带着它吗？\
**Matilda**: Hmm? Aren't you going to take it with you, Ms. Kaalaa Baunaa?

**伽菈波那**：不……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: No.

她摇了摇头。\
She slowly shakes her head.

**伽菈波那**：鬃毛沙砾先生说过的话……不无道理。这是我们的底牌，它离库玛尔越远越好。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Shamane has a point. This is our last chance to win this fight, and it should be kept away from Kumar as far as possible.

**玛蒂尔达**：唔……\
**Matilda**: Emm.

**玛蒂尔达**：那伽菈波那小姐，你带上这个！\
**Matilda**: Ms. Kaalaa Baunaa, take this with you then!

递过来的矿石晶莹剔透，仿佛一颗刚摘下来的星星。\
Matilda passes over a crystal. It is shining brightly, like a freshly picked star.

**伽菈波那**：……这不是你的……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: This is your ...

**玛蒂尔达**：我的灵摆！我珍藏的、纯度极高的珍品！这样好的水晶，我自己总共都没有几颗……\
**Matilda**: My pendulum! It's one of my collections, one of the purest! Even I don't have a lot of them around.

**玛蒂尔达**：我发现你所说的冥想理论，一定程度上和水晶占卜的某些理论根源非常相似～所以如果有水晶帮助你平衡磁场、引导灵知的走向……想必一切都会顺利很多——\
**Matilda**: I realized that the theory of meditation you've talked about is quite similar to some of the crystal divination theories. So, perhaps this will help you in the water, if the crystal can stabilize the magnetic field and guide you in there.

**伽菈波那**：你……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: You ...

**玛蒂尔达**：哼哼，不用惊讶，这是天才基本的反应速度！\
**Matilda**: Humph, no need to be surprised. This is how quickly a genius can think!

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

**伽菈波那**：……谢谢。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Thank you.

**鬃毛沙砾**：很好，看来不能理解“在水里冥想”这个行为的人只有我一个——但没办法，山岩就是多姿多样……\
**Shamane**: Ah, great. So, it's only me who can't understand this "meditation in water" thing. Well, it takes all sorts of rocks to form a mountain.

伽菈波那迅速地将腿探入陶缸内，如同感觉不到冰冷一般。\
Before he finishes his sentence, Kaalaa Baunaa has quickly submerged her legs in the water, as if the cold didn't bother her at all.

**伽菈波那**：好的……灵摆，还有足够多的液体……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Okay, the pendulum and enough liquid.

**伽菈波那**：现在，只需要……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: And all I have to do now is ...

**伽菈波那**：——想着库玛尔。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Think of Kumar.

卸掉双腿支撑的力，伽菈波那放任自己的身体滑入水中。\
She bends her knees and lets herself slide into the water.

声音迅速地远离了她的世界。\
Her world is immediately free of sounds.

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

寒意没过头顶，自四面八方侵袭而来。\
As soon as her head is completely submerged in water, the cold attacks from all directions.

**伽菈波那**：哈啊……！\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: *inhales*

或真或假，亦虚亦实，世界重新浮现于眼前。\
Be it real or false, delusional or real, a world reappears before her.

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

**伽菈波那**：……果然，会是这里。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Where else could it be more suitable ...

**伽菈波那**：我们第一次见面的地方。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ... than the place we first met?

眼前熟悉的石阶比记忆中的要长得多。粗砺的红色砖瓦，精心计算的圆弧，简塔·曼塔天文台每一处都有着独属于它的美感。\
The familiar stone stairs extend much longer than she remembers. The rough red bricks, the well-calculated and carefully designed arc ... Everything in Jantar Mantar has a unique kind of beauty.

**伽菈波那**：呵，看来库玛尔为这场会面下足了心思。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Hah. How thoughtful you were, Kumar ...

**伽菈波那**：竟然在幻境里还原出了这些……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ... to recreate the observatory in the Realm.

在顶端终点静立的身影就像一个黑色的奇点。\
The figure standing still on its top looks like a black singularity.

她知道那是谁。\
She knows who it is.

**伽菈波那**：我心中的幻影，罢了。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Just an illusion in my mind.

左脚踏上了第一层台阶。\
Now, her left foot is on the first step.

**伽菈波那**：……！\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...!

意料之中的困难出现在眼前。\
Resistance is expected.

**伽菈波那**：看来她把我小时候的样子记得很清楚。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: She remembered almost every detail of me as a child.

拦在面前的身影，与她小时候的模样相差无几，总是紧攥着拳头，脸上的表情永远像是在对抗着什么。\
The figure standing in front of her greatly resembles her younger self—always fist-clenching, always ready for confrontation.

而现在，“她”的愤怒或许来自于这场不请自来的入侵。\
And now "the girl" is irritated by the intrusion.

**幻影**：……！\
**Illusion**: ...!

“她”朝伽菈波那奔去，灵活地挥动着拳头。\
"She" rushes toward Kaalaa Baunaa and throws quick punches.

**伽菈波那**：唔，好疼……！\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Oh, it hurts!

**伽菈波那**：我小时候的拳头，有这么坚硬吗？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Did it hurt this much when I hit someone as a child?

**幻影**：出去，这不是你该来的地方！\
**Illusion**: Get out! You should not be here!

“她”驱赶着伽菈波那，体态明显受过严格的训练。\
"She" tries to drive Kaalaa Baunaa away, fighting her like a trained warrior.

**伽菈波那**：啊……是的。妈妈曾教过我……对付那些坏小子的招数。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Ah, yes. Mom had taught me a few moves to deal with those brats at that age.

**幻影**：离开！\
**Illusion**: Leave!

**伽菈波那**：……呃唔，真是……好奇怪的感觉。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Hmm. This feels weird.

**伽菈波那**：是库玛尔让你在这里的吗？让你保护着……这段时间的回忆？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Did Kumar put you here? To guard this fragment of memory?

**幻影**：……\
**Illusion**: ...

**伽菈波那**：看来必须过了你这一关，才能前往我想要到达的地方。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: This shall be the obstacle in my way to where I want to be.

**伽菈波那**：直面过去的幻影吧。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: It's time to face the illusion from the past.

**幻影**：啊……\
**Illusion**: Ah!

幻影消散了，又重新在远处聚拢。与此不同的是，“她”这次不再带有那样强烈的愤慨。\
The illusion is dispersed and then gathers again in the distance, but this time, "she" is no longer irritated.

**幻影**：呵呵……\
**Illusion**: Heh heh.

**伽菈波那**：……！\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...!

天文台的光影使“她”逐渐模糊，声音也愈发飘远。\
"She" gradually fades away in the light and shadow of the observatory, and her voice goes further and further.

**幻影**：从过去，到现在，到未来……\
**Illusion**: From the past, to the present, and the future.

**幻影**：你所要执着的，追逐的，面对的……是什么……\
**Illusion**: The thing you are clinging on to, facing, and chasing ... Think what it is.

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

伽菈波那低下头，看了看自己的手掌。\
Kaalaa Baunaa lowers her head to look at her palm.

**伽菈波那**：你还是像以前一样，总是问一些没有答案的问题。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: You are still asking questions that cannot be answered, just as you always did.

**伽菈波那**：你认为我追逐的“应该”是什么呢？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: What do you think I "should" chase after?

她收起手指，将手轻轻握起。\
Her fingers clench gently.

**伽菈波那**：别想误导我，库玛尔。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I won't be misled this time, Kumar.

**伽菈波那**：天文学这条路，从那天之后我就没有放弃过。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I have never given up studying astronomy since that day.

空旷的空间里，除了回音，什么也没有留下。幻影已经离开了。\
There is only an echo in the empty space. The illusion has gone.

她抬起头，看着几乎望不到顶的天阶。\
She looks up at the almost endless stairs.

**伽菈波那**：……继续前进吧。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Keep moving.

## JMP-10 硕鼠的智慧 / Rat and Its Days

**伽菈波那**：呼……呼……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Whuu ... phew ...

从幼时，到少年，再到青年。也只有在不符合逻辑的幻境中，人才能有机会直面这样多的、来自过去的自己。\
First, the child self, then the teenage self, and then the young adult self. Only in the Meditator's Realm can one face so many past selves ...

——并将他们一一击败。\
... and defeat them one after another.

**伽菈波那**：……20岁的我真够凶的。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: The 20-year-old me was fierce.

伽菈波那揉着自己布满淤青的面颊。\
Kaalaa Baunaa rubs her bruised cheeks.

**伽菈波那**：嘶……好真实的痛感。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: *hiss* That pain feels real.

**库玛尔**：你比我想的迅速，伽菈波那。\
**Kumar**: You came here sooner than I expected, Kaalaa Baunaa.

天文台顶端的风声凛冽。熟悉到不能再熟悉、甚至梦中都会见到的面孔，再一次地出现在了眼前。\
The wind feels like tingling knives on the rooftop. A familiar, if not too familiar, figure once again emerges in front of her.

**库玛尔**：我知道你会来的。\
**Kumar**: I knew you would come.

**伽菈波那**：库玛尔。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Kumar.

**伽菈波那**：我终于……见到你了。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Finally. See you again.

**库玛尔**：我也很想念你，我的孩子……希望在我不在的日子里，你一切都好。\
**Kumar**: I miss you dearly, too, my child. I hope you've been doing well while I was away.

**库玛尔**：希望你还满意我的安排。这个地方的环境我一直很喜欢——而且颇具纪念意义，很适合寒暄。\
**Kumar**: Hope you're happy with the surroundings I set. I always find it enjoyable here—a place full of memories and perfect for small talks.

**伽菈波那**：……我倒是希望你过得难受点，老师。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I'd rather you suffered, Miss.

**库玛尔**：哎呀，你和我说话真是越来越不客气了。\
**Kumar**: Ah, someone is having a worse attitude these days.

伽菈波那抬头，打量着周围的环境。\
Kaalaa Baunaa looks around to observe the surroundings.

**库玛尔**：别看啦，孩子。再怎么说我的研究也比你早了那么几年，在幻境中完美掩盖好现实中的踪迹，是最基本的技巧。\
**Kumar**: There's no need to look around, kid. I already had a few years of experience in the field before you started your research. And one of the most basic skills one has to master in the Meditator's Realm is to cover up the traces of reality.

天空阴沉着，像是肮脏玻璃器皿的表面。\
The sky is dark, like the surface of dusted glassware.

**伽菈波那**：可你竟然不肯在幻境里给自己一片星空。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Even so, you didn't even think about creating a starry sky for yourself here.

对方沉默了片刻，轻轻摇了摇头。\
Kumar is silent for a moment and then shakes her head.

**库玛尔**：……随时都可以见到的东西，没有必要。\
**Kumar**: Hmm. That would be unnecessary. You can see it any time outside this Realm if you like.

**伽菈波那**：你让我过来，有什么目的？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Why did you "invite" me here?

**库玛尔**：……\
**Kumar**: ...

**库玛尔**：我一向体恤你的努力，伽菈波那，就像当年我体恤我那个陌生的弟弟一样……哦，我想那封信成功寄到了，对吧？\
**Kumar**: I know you've put in a lot of efforts. I understand the difficulty within and sympathize with you, Kaalaa Baunaa. I always do, just like what I did with my younger brother. By the way, that letter has been delivered to him safely, I assume?

**库玛尔**：不过你还是很聪明的……你没将毗湿奴带过来。不会有人给你提醒了吧？\
**Kumar**: You're smart enough not to bring the Vishnu statue with you. Did somebody kindly remind you not to do that?

**库玛尔**：算了，它本来就对我没什么用处。\
**Kumar**: Never mind. That's not helpful.

**伽菈波那**：……我不明白。你为什么把他牵扯进来？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I don't understand. Why involve him?

库玛尔身后，一个老式望远镜指向天空。\
Behind Kumar, an old finderscope is aiming at the sky.

**库玛尔**：唔，或许……正如你们所说，是仇恨所致的报复心理吧。\
**Kumar**: Emm, maybe I was being vindictive out of "hatred," like you said.

**库玛尔**：我最开始的路，就被他们堵得死死的……尽管那孩子并不是始作俑者，但我的怒火总该找个人承担。\
**Kumar**: After all, they precluded me from doing anything even before I gave it a try. Although my misfortune was not my brother's doing, there's no one else left in the family to take my anger.

**库玛尔**：来吧，你还想知道什么——我现在都可以告诉你。你好奇的，你困惑的，你那小脑袋瓜儿永远琢磨不出来的事儿，我现在都可以告诉你了。\
**Kumar**: So ask me now. Ask me anything you wish to know. I can tell you everything. What you're curious about, what you're confused about, anything you can't work out in your little brain. I can explain it all.

她温柔地笑着，话语却是令人熟悉的刻薄。\
She smiles warmly, but her words are as cold as usual.

**伽菈波那**：你就不怕我找到你吗？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Hasn't the idea that I might locate you bothered you for even a second?

伽菈波那试探性地靠近一步。\
Kaalaa Baunaa takes a tentative step forward.

**库玛尔**：找到我？哈哈哈——哦！你还是像纸一样纯真，我的伽菈波那。脑筋不够灵活的小家伙——不可能的。\
**Kumar**: Locate me? Hahaha. You are still as naive as a child, my Kaalaa Baunaa. You little dummy owl. That is simply impossible.

**伽菈波那**：——这是你第一次质疑我的能力。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: This is the first time you doubt my capability.

**库玛尔**：不，我怎么会质疑你的能力——你是唯一能赶上我脚步的孩子。\
**Kumar**: No, why would I do that? Of all the students, you are the only child who is smart enough to follow my steps this far.

**库玛尔**：你只是……缺少了一点时间，以及缺乏了一点——良好的心态。\
**Kumar**: You just don't have time on your side and need a better mindset in dealing with the unexpected.

**库玛尔**：我早就试图纠正过这些，一些即兴演讲，你记得吗？很好的锻炼……\
**Kumar**: I've tried to teach it to you. Remember those impromptu speeches I asked you to give? Those were good practice.

**伽菈波那**：……你……什么意思？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: "Don't have ..." What do you mean?

**库玛尔**：你或许太相信我会依靠重塑了。比起重塑，我更信任自己的手段——当然也更信任你。\
**Kumar**: Perhaps you have put too much stock in the idea that I will rely on Manus Vindictae in this. Instead, I trust myself more than them. And, of course, I also trust you.

**库玛尔**：……更何况我也看不上那些家伙。但好在我什么都不像，又最习惯于伪装——就像我当初在班纳尔大学当教授的时候一样。\
**Kumar**: What's more, they were never good enough for me. But luckily, I have never been a real arcanist or a real human, only pretending to be either of them when necessary. I can easily act like an arcanist to gain their trust, just like I could act like a human when I was teaching at Banner.

库玛尔注意到伽菈波那一直盯着那个老式望远镜。\
Kumar notices that Kaalaa Baunaa has been staring at the old finderscope.

**库玛尔**：你怎么老看着这个？拿给你好了。\
**Kumar**: What are you staring at? Take it if you're interested.

**伽菈波那**：……！\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...!

女人轻巧一抛，被她摘下的寻星镜稳稳当当地落在了伽菈波那的手中。\
Kumar takes off the finderscope and throws it lightly to Kaalaa Baunaa. It lands precisely on her palm.

周围仍是不变的景色。看不出任何端倪。\
The surroundings remain the same. Kaalaa Baunaa can't find any loopholes at all.

**库玛尔**：怎么？你以为它像那些石像一样，是击破幻境的核心处？\
**Kumar**: What? You thought it is the key to cracking the Meditator's Realm, like those stone statues earlier?

**库玛尔**：虽然有点晚了，但我现在纠正你一点。\
**Kumar**: Though it is too late for hints, there is one thing I have to remind you of.

她就像她说的一样，十分贴心。\
She is indeed as thoughtful as she claims to be.

**库玛尔**：你没有追上“我”，也没有做出最优抉择……你只是追着那个名为“获胜”的饵一直走到了现在，帮我达成了我想要达成的一切。\
**Kumar**: You didn't catch up to "the real me," nor did you improve the situation by entering the Realm. You chased me all the way here, chased the hope of "winning" against me, but you only helped me complete my plan.

**库玛尔**：——从你进来的那一刻起，我的目的就已经达到了。\
**Kumar**: The moment you entered the Realm, the last step of my plan was done.

**伽菈波那**：帮你……什么……？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I completed what?

**库玛尔**：你也知道，想要让幻境影响现实是很难的，毕竟，它就如同现实世界的倒影……\
**Kumar**: As you know, exerting influence on reality through the Meditator's Realm is challenging. After all, this Realm is like the shadow of its real counterpart, a reflection of reality.

**库玛尔**：我费了好大力气，浪费了一尊神像——才让里面的东西，伸出一点点影子来。\
**Kumar**: I went to a lot of trouble, even wasted a statue, to finally stick out a corner of the shadow over the boundary of the two worlds.

**伽菈波那**：你是说，石窟里的……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: You mean the statue in the cave ...

**库玛尔**：是的。\
**Kumar**: Yes.

**库玛尔**：而我需要的，是一个由外向内的力，彻底帮我打破这层难以单向冲破的薄膜。\
**Kumar**: What I needed was an outside-in force to break the Realm, which is almost unbreakable from the inside.

**库玛尔**：毕竟镜子所映之物的能力有限，但如果镜子之外的现实有人来击碎它……那一切就容易得多了。\
**Kumar**: A mirror can reflect objects, but there's nothing it can do to itself. It can only be shattered into pieces by people not from the reflection, but reality.

**库玛尔**：——这样幻境中的流星坠落之时……\
**Kumar**: Whenever there is a shooting star streaking across the sky of this Realm,

**库玛尔**：在我们的现实世界，也会有一颗同样美丽的星星落下！\
**Kumar**: an equally beautiful star will fall on the real earth!

**库玛尔**：而这个击碎镜子的外力，真巧！正是现在你所做的这件事情。\
**Kumar**: And guess what? YOU are the force I'm looking for.

**伽菈波那**：不，怎么会……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: No. How?

**伽菈波那**：所以我观测到的波动，甚至是那个基金会小女孩感受到的天体能量……那些只是幌子……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: So the fluctuation I detected, the energy of the celestial body felt by the Foundation girl ... are just false alert?

**库玛尔**：哦不，我得承认，那个小姑娘的到来属于意外事件……不过——你理解得非常正确！\
**Kumar**: Oh, no, I have to admit, that young girl was not part of my plan. But, at least, you are on the right track about what happened!

**库玛尔**：要怪就怪你自己的——冠冕堂皇。你的救人之心终究输给了与我竞争之心——人命在你心里……并不如在我面前证明你自己重要。\
**Kumar**: If anything is to blame, it's your ego. You were trying to win, but not by saving people. The idea of proving yourself to me outweighed their lives.

**库玛尔**：我想像得到你有多么努力地在说服自己。\
**Kumar**: You must be wondering, "How could she lay such a trap with her insignificant arcane power"?

**库玛尔**：但你知道吗？其实你在想：“哦！库玛尔的神秘术连抬起个土块儿都困难，又哪里有能力做那些精巧的局呢？一定是依靠了重塑！”\
**Kumar**: "She can barely lift a lump of clay. She must have had the Manus Vindictae on her side to help!"

**库玛尔**：别对自己这么没自信，你仍旧是我最好的学生——差那么一丁点智慧就能和我同台竞技的好同事。\
**Kumar**: All that being said, you don't have to feel yourself to be a lesser version of me. You're still my best student, my best colleague, and my strongest rival—well, with some room to improve.

**库玛尔**：这次你也没输给我的智慧——而是输给了一点我对你的了解。\
**Kumar**: Even this time, you didn't lose the game for lack of wits, but for the fact that I know you a bit better than you know me,

**库玛尔**：……以及捕猎者的经验罢了。\
**Kumar**: and I simply have more experience hunting a prey.

**伽菈波那**：我在此之前，从未……从未将重塑与你……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: You and the Manus ... I've never, never thought that.

无意义的辩白被堵在喉咙里，在天文塔顶端的微风中，伽菈波那觉得自己的呼吸震耳欲聋。\
Kaalaa Baunaa feels her explanation is meaningless and stuck in her throat. She's almost choking for breath in the gentle breeze.

**伽菈波那**：所以，所以如果我这次没有来见你——\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: That means if I didn't enter the Realm to see you ...

**库玛尔**：那我就棘手了。你们将享受一个快乐的烛星节，而我只能在你们不知道的阴暗角落里，哭丧着脸认输。\
**Kumar**: Then things are going to be tricky for me. You would be enjoying a happy Dīpa Festival, while I would be crying in a dark corner nobody knows of.

**伽菈波那**：你，你为什么——\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Why? Why would you ...?

**库玛尔**：哦，时间差不多了。这么重要的问题，下次记得早问，孩子。\
**Kumar**: Well, time's up. Remember to ask the most important question first next time, child.

**库玛尔**：不用感谢我的贴心，也别自作多情，解释这么多并不是为了你——我只是想要彻底的胜利。而你的绝望，正包含在这份胜利之内。\
**Kumar**: Don't thank me for that suggestion, and don't think too much of my kindness. I didn't explain all these things for your sake. I told you everything, because only by doing so can I enjoy the victory to its fullest. Your desperation is a good prize for me.

**库玛尔**：——你也知道，我的个人趣味向来烂得离谱。\
**Kumar**: You know I have a bad taste for entertainment.

**库玛尔**：回去享受你们的烛星节吧——好消息是你们也能和我一样，能亲眼见见那颗漂亮的星星长什么样子了。\
**Kumar**: Go back to the Dīpa Festival. At least there's one good thing left for you—you will get to see that beautiful shooting star with your own eyes, just like I will.

**伽菈波那**：……！\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...!

**库玛尔**：<再见啦。>\
**Kumar**: Goodbye.

## JMP-11 以卵击石 / Straws Against the Wind

**坎吉拉**：唔……我的脚已经不痛了！\
**Kanjira**: Hmm. My ankle hurts no more!

坎吉拉试探性地活动了下被包扎得严严实实的脚踝。\
Kanjira tries to move the tightly wrapped ankle.

**坎吉拉**：……\
**Kanjira**: ...

然而无论是菩提树下盘膝而坐的男人，还是绕着陶缸不停打转的女孩——他们都没能分出精力去看一眼那个已经康复了的脚踝。\
Shamane is sitting under the sacred fig, and Matilda is anxiously walking round and round the vat. Neither of them is in the mood to check Kanjira's ankle.

**玛蒂尔达**：她已经，已经进去了——四分二十六秒……\
**Matilda**: She's been in there for, emm, 4 minutes 26 seconds.

**玛蒂尔达**：唔，这是合理的数字吗？我记得选修课有提及过冥想的最佳时间……\
**Matilda**: Is this a reasonable length of time? I remember I once learned about the ideal time length for meditation in one of the elective classes.

**玛蒂尔达**：而且，伽菈波那小姐是在水下……\
**Matilda**: What's more, she's holding her breath underwater.

**鬃毛沙砾**：……\
**Shamane**: ...

树下的男人双眼微阖。\
Shamane closes his eyes.

喧闹声、脚步声、树干深处难以忽视的龟裂声，逐渐变成了熟悉的、火焰迸裂的噼啪声。\
The noise of people, the footsteps, and the light cracks coming from the inside of the tree gradually turn into the crackle of flames.

当通往对岸的道路，只有一条独木桥的时候……你很难再去选择其他的路程。\
When there is only one way to the destination, you have no choice but to take it.

早已愈合的断肢处传来隐痛。\
Pain is coming from his scar of the mutilation, which healed up long ago.

你不得不让自己迈出那痛苦的一步，然后在意料之内的重心偏移中，抱着绝望叱责自己的愚蠢。\
You have to force yourself to take that painful step, and then blame yourself for being such a desperate fool to move and lose balance.

是的，毕竟谁没跌过跤呢？\
Who has never made a mistake?

想必那时的自己，有着与她们同样的目光。\
There was a time when he was just like them.

如果没有走上错误的独木桥，菩提树早应枝繁叶茂，投下庇护的浓荫。\
If he had chosen the other path, the sacred fig wouldn't have died, and they would be sitting in its shade.

**鬃毛沙砾**：……\
**Shamane**: ...

——可又是否应以未至的“美好”来界定过去的对错呢？\
But who says that would be the better future?

**鬃毛沙砾**：……\
**Shamane**: ...

但好在接下来你将重新落回坚实的土地。\
But the silver lining is, it's just a stagger on the solid ground.

站稳自己的脚跟。\
And you will eventually regain your footing.

**伽菈波那**：咳咳，咳咳咳——\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: *coughs*

沉寂了五分钟的陶缸倏然迸裂。水泄向四周，像是中央那个狼狈身影投射出的影子。\
The vat bursts into pieces after the five-minute silence. The water splashes onto the ground, like strange shadows cast in all directions.

**玛蒂尔达**：——！伽菈波那小姐！\
**Matilda**: ...! Ms. Kaalaa Baunaa!

**伽菈波那**：……！\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...!

可怜的陶土缸变得四分五裂，浑浊的液体逐渐铺满整个地面。\
The poor vat breaks into pieces. The muddy liquid spreads in all directions and covers the ground.

女人的长发狼狈地贴在身上。\
Her wet hair is clinging to her tightly. She looks as miserable as a drowned rat.

**伽菈波那**：快跑，咳咳——快，快带着所有人——呕——\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Leave here. *coughs* Now, and get everyone.

她痛苦地干呕着，似乎这样就能将悔恨连同呕吐物一起赶出这个躯壳。\
She vomits in great pain, as if she could expel the regret from her body this way.

**玛蒂尔达**：你，你成功见到库玛尔了？！这是……\
**Matilda**: Did, did you see Kumar?! What happened?

**伽菈波那**：我才是始作俑者……该死的……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I'm the one to blame. D**n it!

**鬃毛沙砾**：……\
**Shamane**: ...

**伽菈波那**：我——我太蠢了。我早该想到自己根本不是库玛尔的对手……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I'm such a fool. I should have known that I'm not a match for Kumar.

她知道那意味着什么——冲破了那层薄膜，就意味着那颗天体坠落的时间被缩短到了一个无法令人忽视的地步。\
She knows what that means. If the boundary between the Realm and the reality is broken, that celestial body will fall on them in no time.

她痛苦地、无法自抑地评价着自己。\
There's no easy way to forgive herself.

——或许就是今天，或许就是现在。\
Maybe it will destroy them today, maybe in the next minute.

**伽菈波那**：说着为了救人，为了村子……到头来自己一个人……和她立的靶子打得起兴！\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Keep telling myself I did all these things to save the people, to save the village. Turns out it was me fighting against a dummy she set up!

**伽菈波那**：把大家都……害了……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I messed up everything for everyone.

她看着自己的手指，指甲陷入松软的地面。\
She looks at her fingers. The nails have sunk into the soft ground.

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

视野内出现的，是一块皱皱巴巴的粗布。\
A wrinkled piece of coarse cloth comes into her sight.

**伽菈波那**：……对不起。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I'm sorry.

**伽菈波那**：我应该听你的。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I should have listened to you.

她的头压得更低了。\
She lowers her head even more.

**伽菈波那**：如果我更理智一点……放弃这条不可理喻的道路，不去尝试什么该死的“陷阱”……一切就都不会变成现在这个样子。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: If I were more sensible and just left this path, this stupid d**n "trap," nothing would have turned out this way.

**鬃毛沙砾**：……\
**Shamane**: ...

**鬃毛沙砾**：哦，你是这样想的？\
**Shamane**: Oh, is that how you see it?

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

**鬃毛沙砾**：你说出这种话，有两种可能性。要么，这只是一次失败之后颓丧的违心之言——\
**Shamane**: I assume you think it this way because you have failed in the mission and thus feel depressed and indulge yourself in some negative thinking.

**鬃毛沙砾**：可以理解，把一切问题揽在自己身上，确实可以让自己的愧疚之心好受一点。要么，就是你完全没听明白我的意思～\
**Shamane**: Which is totally understandable. Blaming it all on yourself, telling yourself you will be the only one to suffer the consequence so as to alleviate the guilt. Or, you didn't understand what I said to you earlier at all.

**伽菈波那**：什……么？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: What?

女人诧异地抬起头来，只觉得那轻松的语气仿佛是自己的幻觉。\
She looks up with confusion, wondering if that relaxed tone is another illusion.

**鬃毛沙砾**：别这么说，伽菈波那。还记得我说的吗？——你无需为自己的信任懊恼。同样，也不要因勇敢而谴责自己。\
**Shamane**: You have to stop it, Kaalaa Baunaa. Remember what I said? "You don't have to feel bad for trusting people." And here's another piece: Don't blame yourself for being brave.

**鬃毛沙砾**：她是怎么说的？说是因为你的愚蠢才让大家都倒了霉？\
**Shamane**: What did she tell you? "You're a fool, and you ruined everything"?

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

男人蹲下身，直视着对方眼中的自己。\
He crouches down and looks straight at his reflection in her eyes.

**鬃毛沙砾**：得了吧！你我都知道，这不是事实。\
**Shamane**: Come on! Both of us know this is not the case.

**鬃毛沙砾**：勇敢还是鲁莽，谨慎还是退缩——这不全是行动前的定义，更多时候，它们是一切发生后，他人的总结。\
**Shamane**: Brave or reckless, prudent or cowardly ... Comments like these could be predictions, but most of the time are hindsight.

**鬃毛沙砾**：好消息是，现在……还没到总结的时候。\
**Shamane**: The good news is, we still have time to change that.

**鬃毛沙砾**：要知道，被捕兽夹伤过的熊，是最令猎人恐惧的存在。\
**Shamane**: You know what kind of bears the hunters fear the most? The ones which were once trapped but eventually got away.

**鬃毛沙砾**：——无人能永恒立于捕猎者的位置之上，况且……\
**Shamane**: Nobody can remain a predator forever. We don't know what will happen in the next encounter. What's more ...

**鬃毛沙砾**：算计，说白了也是自然发展的一环！熊吃鲑鱼，狼食幼兔，而它们的皮毛到最后都会变成我们最柔软的毯子。\
**Shamane**: Life is a long fight where we outsmart one opponent and get outsmarted by the other. That's the wisdom of nature! Bears eat salmon; wolves eat rabbit; but eventually, bears or wolves, their skin will become our blankets.

**鬃毛沙砾**：老虎有老虎的力量，硕鼠有硕鼠的智慧——你的胜利，不需要建立在她败北之上。\
**Shamane**: A tiger might have strength, yet a rat also has its wits. You don't need to defeat her to validate your victory. You can win this war in another way, a way to your advantage.

**鬃毛沙砾**：咬饵之后，才是角力的开始。\
**Shamane**: When will the wrestling between a fisherman and a fish begin? When the fish bites the bait.

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

**鬃毛沙砾**：所以如果你现在还站得起来，能厘清我们现在的状况——那就帮大忙了，毕竟听你的语气，我们不像是有继续冥想的时间了……\
**Shamane**: So, if you still have some strength left in you to get back on your feet and think straight, that'd be most helpful. After all, I don't think we have the time for another round of meditation.

伽菈波那接过了那块粗布。\
Kaalaa Baunaa takes the cloth.

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

她将脸埋入其中，狠狠地将它自眼眶抹过——脸上传来的刺痛教人立刻清醒过来。\
She buries her face into it, wiping hard across her eyes—the pain brings her senses back.

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

**伽菈波那**：上次用这样的东西擦脸，我还在和妈妈练习摔跤呢……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: The last time I wiped my face with this, I was wrestling with my mom.

她深吸一口气，试着让理智重新夺回大脑的控制权。\
She takes a deep breath, trying to get her brain working again.

**伽菈波那**：库玛尔……利用我打破了幻境与现实的界线，坠星很可能要提前了。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Kumar ... She broke the boundary between the Meditator's Realm and reality through me. I'm afraid the falling star will arrive early.

**玛蒂尔达**：什么？！就没什么办法能阻止她吗？\
**Matilda**: What?! There's no other way to stop her, then?

**伽菈波那**：如果能找到她本人……或许还有转圜的余地。但很抱歉，我在幻境中没有发现任何线索，现在——\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: There might be a way to stop her by locating her in person, but I didn't spot any clue in the Realm. And now ...

**鬃毛沙砾**：而现在，这种像是被罗摩用弓指着一样的危机状况……比起留恋这个地方，不如早点保住那些我们能保住的东西。\
**Shamane**: We are in a dangerous situation, almost as urgent as the time when Rama was facing the arrow nocked to a full bow. Instead of getting caught up in nostalgia, we should take action and protect what can be saved.

**玛蒂尔达**：基金会给出的预计到达时间是……凌晨六时！唔，如果流星提前降落的话，这时间肯定不够……\
**Matilda**: The estimated arrival time of the Foundation backup is 6 a.m. It will be too late if the meteor really falls early.

**玛蒂尔达**：我们需要一个能抵挡——或者躲避流星的地方！除此之外，还要先把落单的村民集中起来。\
**Matilda**: We need a shelter that can withstand the impact! Also, we have to gather all the villagers.

**玛蒂尔达**：还有，还有……呜！实战演练的课程还教过我们……\
**Matilda**: And, and ... Ah! In the field training, the instructor also told us to ...

**坎吉拉**：我也要和你们一起去！\
**Kanjira**: I'll go with you!

黑发女孩一瘸一拐地走上前来。\
Kanjira staggers her way to them.

**坎吉拉**：我和你们一起去……我更熟悉路程！况且……夏尔贾还没回来……\
**Kanjira**: I'll go with you. I know the way better! Besides, Sherjah is not back yet.

**坎吉拉**：如果她真出了什么事……我绝对不会原谅那时候的自己。\
**Kanjira**: If anything happens to she, I will not forgive myself I say those words.

**玛蒂尔达**：……\
**Matilda**: ...

**伽菈波那**：……唔。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Hmm.

**伽菈波那**：我要留在这里。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I'm staying.

**坎吉拉**：嗯？\
**Kanjira**: Hmm?

**伽菈波那**：如果可以计算彗星的伤害范围……我们或许能在彗星到来之前，撤到一个安全的位置。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: If I can calculate the range of damage of the comet, we may retreat to a safe location.

女人把湿漉漉的长发向后一甩。\
Kaalaa Baunaa flings her wet hair back.

**伽菈波那**：硕鼠有……硕鼠的智慧。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Every rat has its day.

**伽菈波那**：……我在尽力尝试了。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: And "this rat" is doing her best.

**鬃毛沙砾**：哈！别摆出这副表情——你可不是什么硕鼠，我瞧得出，你是货真价实的虎崽子……真正的硕鼠可在门外溜达着呢！\
**Shamane**: Hahaha! Don't put on a face like that. You are not some rat, I can tell! You are the tiger cub. In the meantime, let's not forget—the real rat is still out there looking smug!

镌刻着层层保护咒的石门外，是一场预料之内的长线战斗。\
It is predictable that there will be a long-term battle outside the stone door enchanted with protection incantations.

他转过身去，有点局促地搓了搓手。\
Shamane turns around and rubs his hands, feeling a bit uneasy.

**鬃毛沙砾**：记得躲着点我打飞出去的东西——呃，很多时候，我真的不是故意的！\
**Shamane**: Watch out for the things I knock off. I didn't do it on purpose!

## JMP-12 芝麻开门 / Open Sesame

**夏尔贾老师**：呼——\
**Ms. Sherjah**: *exhales*

随着轻微的吐息，最后一盏星烛也熄灭了。\
The last butter lamp has been blown out by the quiet breath.

掩体背后，黑暗笼罩了下来。\
Darkness falls on the people who are still in hiding.

**夏尔贾老师**：只要不被他们发现，目前我们就是安全的……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: We are safe as long as they can't find us.

年轻女人将昏倒的妇人与女孩安顿在安全的阴影之后。\
Sherjah hides the fainted woman and the girl in the shadow to keep them safe.

**吉娜**：呜呜……夏尔贾老师，我害怕……\
**Jina**: *sobs* Ms. Sherjah, I'm scared.

女孩死死地握住了女人的手，如同抓着一棵救命稻草。\
Jina holds Sherjah's hand so tightly, as she is the only lifesaver now.

**夏尔贾老师**：不要害怕，吉娜。爸爸和爷爷不是和你说了吗？在这里好好等着，他们很快就回来，你哥哥也在帮忙……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Relax, Jina. Remember what Dad and Grandpa said? Just wait here, and they will be back soon. Your brother is also helping them out.

**吉娜**：呜呜，可是……那些怪物好恐怖……妈妈，妈妈也……\
**Jina**: *sobs* But those monsters are terrifying. Even, even Mother ...

**夏尔贾老师**：……唔。\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Hmm.

女人回忆起目睹的惨状，不禁闭上了双眼。\
Recalling the tragic scene, Sherjah can't help closing her eyes.

**夏尔贾老师**：妈妈只是暂时晕过去了，你放心，她很快就……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Mother just passed out. Don't worry. She will ...

**村民**：可恶，该死的怪物！\
**Rajesh**: D**n it! F**king monsters!

**重塑·门徒**：ㄠㄠ——！\
**Manus Disciple**: AAARRRHHHH!

男人念着咒语，舞动弯刀，试图与对面的怪物拉开距离。\
The man casts an incantation while wielding the ram-dao to keep the monsters away.

**老年村民**：哼，肮脏的东西！\
**Takal**: Humph! Filthy maggots!

**村民**：父亲！他们的数量根本不见少……\
**Rajesh**: Father! There are still a lot of them.

**老年村民**：别窝窝囊囊的，拉杰什！拿出点男子汉的样儿来，哼，还要拜托人类小姑娘来帮我们……\
**Takal**: Don't be such a coward, Rajesh. Be a man! Humph! Can't believe we are even counting on a human girl now.

弯刀向前飞去，一只带着黑色黏稠液体的手应声落地。\
The ram-dao cuts through the air. An arm covered in black slime falls to the ground.

**重塑·门徒**：ㄝˋ……\
**Manus Disciple**: UUUGGGHHHH!

**老年村民**：真是丢脸！咳咳……\
**Takal**: Shame on us! *coughs*

**村民**：父亲，小心——\
**Rajesh**: Father, watch out!

**重塑·门徒**：ㄡ——！！\
**Manus Disciple**: AAARRRHHHH!

**夏尔贾老师**：——老先生，小心背后！\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Sir! Watch your back!

身体比头脑先一步行动。冲出阴影的一瞬间，脑中的理性已发出了危险信号。\
The body acts before the mind. The moment Sherjah exposes herself and rushes into the light, her senses scream to warn her of the danger.

**夏尔贾老师**：……！\
**Ms. Sherjah**: ...!

**重塑·门徒**：ㄡㄠˋ——\
**Manus Disciple**: EEERRRHHHH!

赤手空拳的人类对上重塑神秘学家——注定是以卵击石。\
There is no doubt a bare-handed human challenging a group of Manus followers is throwing straws against the wind.

**鬃毛沙砾**：嗬——\
**Shamane**: Hah!

最后一位重塑门徒应声倒地，连面具都碎成了可怜的两瓣。\
The last Manus follower falls to the ground, the mask broken in half.

——而男人维持着举着拳头的动作，显然连自己都没反应过来。\
Shamane freezes, his fist still in the air. Even he himself doesn't realize what has happened.

**鬃毛沙砾**：噢，真是……吓我一跳。\
**Shamane**: Oh, boy! That was close!

他低下头，对上夏尔贾同样有些惊惶的视线。\
He looks down and meets Sherjah's equally confused eyes.

**鬃毛沙砾**：呼——！夏尔贾女士，我虽然很钦佩你的勇气，但这实在是有点太刺激了……\
**Shamane**: Ah, Ms. Sherjah, I admire you for your courage, but this is getting a bit too nerve-racking.

他收回手臂，心有余悸地擦了把汗。\
He withdraws his arm, a bit scared by what has happened.

**坎吉拉**：夏尔贾！\
**Kanjira**: Ms. Sherjah!

**夏尔贾老师**：坎吉拉……？还有——你们怎么找到这里的！\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Kanjira? Wait, how did you find this place?

**坎吉拉**：对不起，夏尔贾，我不该跟你发脾气的！刚刚真的……差点吓死我了……呜……\
**Kanjira**: Sorry, Ms. Sherjah. I should not is mad at you! That scares me so ...

**夏尔贾老师**：抱，抱歉……我身体不由自主地……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: S-Sorry. I couldn't control myself, and my body just ...

**老年村民**：嗯？等等，你小子……\
**Takal**: Hmm? Wait, young man!

老年人一把抓住了鬃毛沙砾的左臂。\
The old man grasps Shamane's left arm.

**老年村民**：这个手……你，你是那个沙尔玛家的！\
**Takal**: This arm ... You! You are the Sharma boy!

**鬃毛沙砾**：嘿！这不是卡塔尔叔叔吗——真是好久没见！\
**Shamane**: Hey! Aren't you Uncle Takal? It's been such a long time since we last met!

**老年村民**：你，你，你怎么——\
**Takal**: How, how did you ...

老人的表情像是见到了活着的亡魂。\
The old man seems to be looking at a living ghost.

**鬃毛沙砾**：哦，卡塔尔叔叔，虽然我也很想和你们寒暄，但是情况稍微有那么一点紧急——\
**Shamane**: Oh, Uncle Takal, I wish I could talk to you for a bit more, but the situation seems to be less than ideal.

他热情地避开了老人的疑问。\
Warmly greeting the old man, he avoids the question.

**鬃毛沙砾**：简单来说，这个地方就快被陨石砸穿了～更坏一点的消息是，不出意外的话，意外会比基金会的救援先到——\
**Shamane**: To put it simply, this place is about to be smashed into an impact crater by a meteor. Even worse, the meteor will arrive here sooner than the Foundation's rescue.

**鬃毛沙砾**：但你们运气真的很不错——你们是第一批被我们找到的幸运儿！\
**Shamane**: But, among all the unfortunate people, you are the lucky ones! You are the first group we found.

**鬃毛沙砾**：来吧，上车，先去我的宅子里坐坐，我想卡塔尔叔叔甚至还记得路……\
**Shamane**: Come on, get in, we will have a get-together at my place. Uncle Takal, you remember the way to our house, right?

**老年村民**：什么？！那幢被烧过的老宅？！不，我绝不会——\
**Takal**: What?! That burned old house?! No way! I will never ...

**鬃毛沙砾**：噢，那抱歉了，叔叔——这次就算是用绑的，我也要给您绑过去。\
**Shamane**: Well, I will have to apologize to you for this then, Uncle. You must come with us, even if I have to tie you up and drag you there.

**老年村民**：不——别——！你这大逆不道的小子——\
**Takal**: No! Stop it! You deviant brat!

村民们与他们的嘟囔声一起被塞进了车里。\
The villagers are pushed into the tuk tuk with their complaints.

**鬃毛沙砾**：好了——总之很高兴看到你没事，夏尔贾女士，但是抱歉，我们目前需要你的帮助。\
**Shamane**: Alright. I'm glad to see that you're fine, Ms. Sherjah. We are in dire need of a helping hand.

**坎吉拉**：夏尔贾，我记得你很熟悉这里！\
**Kanjira**: Ms. Sherjah, I remember you know this place well!

**夏尔贾老师**：是，是这样……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Yes, I do.

**鬃毛沙砾**：我们现在要把所有人——无论是人类还是神秘学家，都尽快转移到安全的地方。\
**Shamane**: We need to transfer everyone here—humans and arcanists—to a safe place.

**坎吉拉**：我想……你是最熟悉，也是最好的人选。\
**Kanjira**: And you're the best person to do that.

**夏尔贾老师**：我……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: I ...

**夏尔贾老师**：……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: ...

**夏尔贾老师**：没问题，只要能帮得上忙——我一定不遗余力。\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Alright. I'll do whatever I can, as long as it helps.

**鬃毛沙砾**：噢，真该让我父亲瞧瞧……这可比我可靠多了！\
**Shamane**: Wish my father could see this. Isn't she a lot more reliable than I am?

**鬃毛沙砾**：我早说过人类比神秘学家靠谱得多——唉。\
**Shamane**: Told the old man a million times that humans make more decent work partners than arcanists. *sighs*

**玛蒂尔达**：——别傻站着啦！\
**Matilda**: Hurry up, you people!

玛蒂尔达打开车门，着急地催促他们上车。\
Matilda opens the door and urges them to get in.

**玛蒂尔达**：嘿，快一点，你们几个！可没时间磨磨蹭蹭的！\
**Matilda**: You can chat later!

**鬃毛沙砾**：好的——夏尔贾，麻烦你简单描述下周围的情况。我们需要尽快接到所有的人。\
**Shamane**: I hear you. Sherjah, please briefly tell us what the neighborhood is like. We need to pick up everyone in the town as soon as possible.

**鬃毛沙砾**：而我们要注意规划出最优的路线——尽可能地避开路上的那些怪家伙。\
**Shamane**: We need to find the quickest way to do it and avoid all the enemies on the way.

**鬃毛沙砾**：放轻松，如果实在避不开——我们就从他们身上开过去！\
**Shamane**: Hey, relax. We can't run away from them—we will just run over them!

## JMP-13 无星之地 / No Starry Sky

**伽菈波那**：现在情况怎么样？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: How is everything now?

**夏尔贾老师**：唔，效率很高。村子里的年轻人和游客早在我四处劝说的时候就离开得差不多了，现在的多是一些老人和无法远行的孩子，还有……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Well, it's going smooth. The young people and tourists left as soon as I persuaded them. Only the old and the children are left here. It's not that easy for them to move, and ...

**阿贾尔**：嘿，你说好分我一半的，坎吉拉大姐怎么还耍赖啊？\
**Ajar**: Hey, you promised to give me half of it! Now what, the boss cannot keep her own promise?

**坎吉拉**：哼！我在外面跑了一天，当然做得多，吃得多啦！\
**Kanjira**: Humph! I do most messenger work! More food for more work!

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

**夏尔贾老师**：这些因为是人类而被遗弃、赶出来的孩子……坎吉拉能和他们玩儿得这么好，我真的很高兴……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: These kids were abandoned and driven away by humans. I'm glad to see Kanjira get along with them.

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

伽菈波那垂眼看着手中的星盘。\
Kaalaa Baunaa looks down at the astrolabe in her hand.

**伽菈波那**：如果她曾经……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: If she could enjoy a life like this ...

**夏尔贾老师**：……？\
**Ms. Sherjah**: ...?

**伽菈波那**：不……没什么。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: No. Nothing.

她轻轻笑了一下，神情有一瞬间的恍惚。\
Kaalaa Baunaa chuckles. There's a faraway look on her face.

**伽菈波那**：我想起来了，我妈妈也是这样的人。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: You just reminded me of my mother.

**伽菈波那**：……夏尔贾，或许像你们这样的人，才是拯救我们的关键。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Sherjah, perhaps people like you are the key to saving all of us.

**伽菈波那**：刚才我又尝试了一次观测。情况确实不容乐观，但好在我依然能根据这些计算出具体的数据。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I just observed it again. The figures are showing a grim picture. Luckily, I've worked out the specific range of damage.

女人在地图上画了个不小的圆圈。\
She draws quite a large circle on the map.

**伽菈波那**：只要我们能逃到这个范围外，就可以避开人员的伤亡……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: As long as we can get out of this radius, there will be no casualties.

**伽菈波那**：至于其他的损失……恐怕我就无能为力了。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: As for other losses ... they are beyond my ability to cover.

**玛蒂尔达**：唔……\
**Matilda**: Emm.

**玛蒂尔达**：基金会的飞艇已经在路上了，至少一定时间内不会缺少基础的水源补给。\
**Matilda**: The airship of the Foundation is on the way. At least our water supply is secured for now.

**玛蒂尔达**：可问题是，这样的距离……\
**Matilda**: But the problem is, in such a distance ...

笔尖自地图上轻轻划过。\
She draws a straight line on the map lightly.

**伽菈波那**：这样的距离……就算是直线，我们带着老人和孩子也不可能在几小时内到达。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: The distance ... Even if we follow the straight line, it is impossible for us, with the elders and the children, to get out of it within hours.

**玛蒂尔达**：呜……可恶，明明就差一点了……\
**Matilda**: Err, why! We are getting so close to success.

**玛蒂尔达**：要是能藏到地底下的话……！\
**Matilda**: If only we could go underground ...

**鬃毛沙砾**：地底下……？等下！\
**Shamane**: Underground? Wait!

**鬃毛沙砾**：我记得父亲曾教过我……在这间房子的下面，有一条连通着外部山林的隧道，目的就是为了应对灾难……\
**Shamane**: I remember my old man told me about an emergency tunnel leading to the forest on the mountain. Its entrance is right here, beneath the floor of this very room.

**伽菈波那**：隧道？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: A tunnel?

**鬃毛沙砾**：当时他教我这些，是为了让我以后能承担起管理村子的重任。如果我没记错，那片山林——刚好就在这片范围之外。\
**Shamane**: He told me this, hoping that one day I will take over his responsibility to look after the village. If I remember it correctly, that forest, which is also the exit of this tunnel, is right outside the impact area.

粗糙的指尖在红色马克笔的范围外轻轻地点了两下。\
He taps on a spot outside the marked range with his rough finger.

**伽菈波那**：这太好了……如果在隧道里的话，即便不足以及时赶到山林，我们也能避开陨石碎片造成的危险……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: That's great. In the tunnel, even if we don't make it to the forest in time, we can still avoid the damage.

**鬃毛沙砾**：但是——\
**Shamane**: But, but ...

男人龇牙咧嘴地抓了抓胡子，脸上爬满了尴尬。\
He scratches his beard, hissing in embarrassment.

**鬃毛沙砾**：问题在于，想要进入隧道，必须得通过一扇门——事先声明！这是我爸的原话……\
**Shamane**: The problem is there's a gate to the tunnel. Now, just for the record, I'm only quoting my old man.

**鬃毛沙砾**：“只有被子民信任着的领导者才能开启”……的门。\
**Shamane**: "It is a gate which only opens to the leader who has earned his people's trust."

**玛蒂尔达**：……\
**Matilda**: ...

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

**坎吉拉**：哦哦，“芝麻开门”！这下真的是寻宝啦。\
**Kanjira**: Oh, "Open Sesame!" We is going real treasure hunting this time.

沉默中，显然只有一无所知的孩童是快乐的。\
Out of the silence, only the naive child is excited.

**鬃毛沙砾**：噢，拜托，这真的很老土——即便在当年也很老土！我压根儿没信！\
**Shamane**: Oh, well. My father's version was hardly as exciting as "Open Sesame"! I didn't believe him even as a child!

**鬃毛沙砾**：所以我小时候不信邪，偷偷尝试过无数次——没一次成功的！\
**Shamane**: I tried to open it by force many times. Well, it never worked!

**鬃毛沙砾**：当然，最坏的情况——就是我爸的话属实。\
**Shamane**: If my old man was telling the truth, things would be problematic for us …

**鬃毛沙砾**：那问题可就大了！我可不认为我能打开那扇门！首先，我的个人意愿不足，其次，他们的信任——听听庭院里那些老头子的骂街声吧！\
**Shamane**: Because I don't think I can get that gate open! Firstly, I've never wanted to be a leader, and speaking of "the people's trust" ... How do you think those cursing old men in the yard will feel about me?

**伽菈波那**：唔……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Emm.

伽菈波那侧耳倾听了片刻，承认他的话不无道理。\
Kaalaa Baunaa listens to "those cursing old men" for a while. She cannot contradict what he says.

**伽菈波那**：即便如此……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Even so ...

她的手指在地图上轻轻点动，节奏越来越快。\
She taps on the map, thinking.

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

**伽菈波那**：我们要想办法把那扇门打开。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: We will open that gate.

她抬头，望向一旁呆立的男人。\
She looks up at Shamane. He is standing in silence and has a blank look on his face.

**鬃毛沙砾**：……？\
**Shamane**: ...?

**伽菈波那**：哪怕是用拳头捶……？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Even if we have to smash it with our bare fists.

**鬃毛沙砾**：……\
**Shamane**: ...

**鬃毛沙砾**：我不确定你这句是不是讽刺……\
**Shamane**: I'm not sure if you were being sarcastic.

她不置可否，目光重新落回地图上。\
She doesn't give a clear answer. Instead, her eyes flit back to the map.

**伽菈波那**：这是目前，最好的办法了。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: It's the best way in the current situation.

庭院里侧的走廊上，有一处松动的地板——\
On the porch in front of the house, there is a loose floorboard.

将它挪开，沿着木梯向下，便能抵达隧道的入口。\
Under it, they see some wooden stairs, which appear to be the entrance of a tunnel.

**夏尔贾老师**：注意脚下……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Watch your steps.

众人在引导下缓缓进入了深处。\
One after another, they slowly go down the stairs.

厚重的灰黄色石门中央，象的前足高高扬起——并且纹丝不动。\
The gray and yellow stone gate has a pattern of an elephant raising its front feet in the middle. It is as immovable as a real elephant.

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

**玛蒂尔达**：果然鬃毛沙砾说的咒语没什么效用啊。\
**Matilda**: So the spell Shamane told us is truly useless.

**鬃毛沙砾**：哈哈，我早说过，这门从以前开始就和我无缘……\
**Shamane**: Hahaha, what did I say? This is never the gate for me to open.

他略带尴尬地笑了笑。而身后，意料中的批判如期而至。\
Shamane gives them an embarrassed smile. Behind him, the criticism comes as expected.

**老年村民**：嗤，沙尔玛家的小子能让人有什么指望……连自己家都保护不好，还来管别人的死活吗？\
**Takal**: Tsk, I knew we shouldn't have counted on you, Sharma boy. You can't even protect your own family. How are you supposed to protect others?

**村民**：噢，愿众神聆听我的祈祷，再次给予我们指引者……\
**Villager 2**: May the gods listen to my prayer and send us another guide ...

**鬃毛沙砾**：……\
**Shamane**: ...

瞧瞧，可以将人耳朵磨出老茧的抱怨，甚至音节都令人充满了——怀念。\
Oh, here they come again! The complaints Shamane has heard so many times. Those familiar syllables make him almost—nostalgic.

**坎吉拉**：……\
**Kanjira**: ...

坎吉拉点着脚尖，节奏越来越快——这是不耐烦的表现。\
Kanjira is tapping a foot faster and faster—it's getting hard for her to suppress the anger.

**老年村民**：和人类接触那么多，我们已经……\
**Takal**: After dealing with humans all these years, we are already ...

**坎吉拉**：……\
**Kanjira**: ...

**坎吉拉**：你们……！\
**Kanjira**: You!

**坎吉拉**：——都给我闭嘴啦！！\
**Kanjira**: SHUT UP YOUR MOUTHS!!

**鬃毛沙砾**：……！\
**Shamane**: ...!

**众村民**：……！\
**Villagers**: ...!

人群瞬间鸦雀无声。\
The crowd instantly falls into silence.

怀念的氛围烟消云散，男人低头，女孩脸上的烦躁还未完全散去。\
The spell of "nostalgia" is broken. Shamane lowers his head, surprised by her irritation.

**坎吉拉**：天天就这么两句话，念念叨叨的烦不烦！\
**Kanjira**: All you talk about is protect, family, and stuff. Give me a break!

**坎吉拉**：还有你！\
**Kanjira**: And YOU!

**鬃毛沙砾**：呃，啊？……我？\
**Shamane**: Emm? Me?

男人一愣，伸出手指着自己的鼻子。\
Shamane points at his own nose, brought up short.

**坎吉拉**：对，就是你！\
**Kanjira**: Yes, you!

**鬃毛沙砾**：我，我怎么……\
**Shamane**: W-what about me?

女孩扬起头看着他。\
Kanjira throws back her head and glares at him.

**坎吉拉**：你平常不是话挺多的嘛，怎么现在倒是这么安静？哼……白长这么大块头……\
**Kanjira**: You love talking, don't you? Now you go dumb? Humph! Big guy can't defend yourself!

**坎吉拉**：我真是搞不懂你，有不满就说出来啊，你在怕什么？\
**Kanjira**: I just don't understand. You feel bad. You say it. Why is you afraid?

**坎吉拉**：你又不欠他们的！\
**Kanjira**: You don't owe them!

**坎吉拉**：你看——\
**Kanjira**: See?

她伸出手，指着鸦雀无声的人群。\
Kanjira extends a finger at the hushed crowd.

**坎吉拉**：你明明可以让他们闭嘴的！\
**Kanjira**: You talk, and you shut them up!

鬃毛顺着她的手指望向那些熟悉的面孔。\
Shamane follows her pointing finger and looks at the familiar faces.

他突然意识到，即便过了这么多年……他仍没忘记他们，哪怕一星半点。\
He suddenly realizes that, after all these years, he still remembers each of them clearly.

**鬃毛沙砾**：……\
**Shamane**: ...

曾经那些目光咄咄逼人，但如今，他们只是沉默着，避开了他的目光。\
There is no longer anger or disdain in their eyes. They just remain silent and avoid his gaze.

**坎吉拉**：喏，早这样不就好了？！我们应该把精力放到、放到最重要的事情上去！\
**Kanjira**: Why don't you do this earlier? We need to focus on the most important thing!

**坎吉拉**：这可是“芝麻开门”啊！\
**Kanjira**: It's "Open Sesame" story!

坎吉拉满脸羡慕地嘟囔着。\
Kanjira mumbles admiringly.

**坎吉拉**：故事里，只有最聪明、最智慧的人才能打开它！怎么你反而在这里犹犹豫豫的……\
**Kanjira**: In the story, only the most smart and wise people can open it! Why do you hesitate now?

**鬃毛沙砾**：哈哈……\
**Shamane**: Haha ...

像是看到了什么有趣的故事，鬃毛沙砾笑出声来。\
Shamane laughs, as if she has said something most amusing.

**鬃毛沙砾**：小家伙，你觉得我是最聪明、最智慧的人？\
**Shamane**: Little one, you think I'm the smartest and wisest person?

**坎吉拉**：唔，我不觉得。\
**Kanjira**: Er, no.

**鬃毛沙砾**：噢。\
**Shamane**: Oh.

意料之外的回答让他垮下脸来。\
His laugh stops.

**坎吉拉**：但你为什么要问我？这是属于你的门呀！\
**Kanjira**: But why ask me? It is your gate!

**鬃毛沙砾**：……！\
**Shamane**: ...!

**坎吉拉**：我的观点不重要，他们的观点也不重要——所以我才说，你应该及时让他们闭嘴啦。\
**Kanjira**: My answer don't matter. Their answer don't matter, too. That's why I said you should shut them up!

坎吉拉翻了个白眼。\
Kanjira rolls her eyes.

**坎吉拉**：总会有故事为我准备一扇门的……到时候，我会用我的方式打开它！\
**Kanjira**: There will be a gate for me, and I will open it my way!

**坎吉拉**：哼，能决定怎么开门的人，只有我自己……我的咒语肯定比“芝麻开门”更长——更酷——\
**Kanjira**: I'm the one to decide how to open my gate. My spell will be longer and cooler than some "Open Sesame."

**坎吉拉**：我才不羡慕你呢！\
**Kanjira**: I'm not jealous you!

她赌气一般地背过身去，不再看鬃毛沙砾。\
She turns her back to him, refusing to cast a look at him.

**鬃毛沙砾**：……哈，哈哈哈哈……唉，真有意思……看来我爸说得对，我可没什么做领头羊的天赋。\
**Shamane**: Haha ... *sighs* Interesting! Looks like Dad was right. I'm not qualified to be a leader.

**鬃毛沙砾**：谢谢啦，孩子。\
**Shamane**: Thanks, kid.

**鬃毛沙砾**：……呼！\
**Shamane**: Phew!

**鬃毛沙砾**：是时候让这些咒语见鬼去了。\
**Shamane**: Anyway, times have changed. Forget the spell.

对，那是他父亲的门，是他的道路，他的方式——他的责任。\
That's his father's gate, his father's path, his father's choice of life, and his father's responsibility.

**鬃毛沙砾**：但现在站在这里的不是他。\
**Shamane**: But it is I who am standing here, not him.

他将声音抬高了些。\
He raises his voice.

**鬃毛沙砾**：我不知道我父亲以前承诺过你们什么——但是很抱歉，说到底，我对你们那些老掉牙的想法从始至终一点儿兴趣都没有……\
**Shamane**: Screw it. I have no idea what my father once promised you. In fact, I have no interest in what your old heads think.

**鬃毛沙砾**：唔，可我该做点什么不一样的呢？\
**Shamane**: Hmm, but what's my own way of opening the gate?

选一句咒语？唱一首歌？学山羊叫？\
Pick a new spell? Sing a song? Bleat like a goat?

拳头攥紧，他莫名想起一句调侃。\
His fist clenches. At this serious, crucial moment, he is strangely relieved by one sudden idea.

**鬃毛沙砾**：……\
**Shamane**: ...

对啊，哪怕是用拳头捶呢？\
He doesn't need any implements. He can just do it with his bare hands, figuratively and literally.

**鬃毛沙砾**：哈哈！\
**Shamane**: Hahaha!

**鬃毛沙砾**：没错，现在站在这里的是我——而不是一个新的沙尔玛。\
**Shamane**: And the one standing right here right now is me, not another Sharma.

肩膀放松，站稳脚跟，上臂发力。\
Keep the shoulder loose, stay steady, and engage with the upper arm.

这才是他更擅长的事。\
This is his way.

**鬃毛沙砾**：所以啊——\
**Shamane**: That is to say ...

**鬃毛沙砾**：嗬！\
**Shamane**: Hah!

那是他有史以来挥出的，最轻松的一拳。\
This is the easiest punch he has ever thrown.

似乎所有的包袱都在挥出的那一瞬间远离了他……那些早已放置在脚下的过去也随着这完美的弧线，彻底离开了他的视野。\
The burden from the past, the pain, and the stress are thrown out of his body at this moment.

噢……这扇门。\
Oh! Turns out the gate ...

原来这样脆弱。\
... is much more fragile than I thought.

夜晚的山林静谧，其间一块不大的空地上燃起了几丛篝火。\
It's a quiet night in the forest. A bonfire is lit in a small, open space.

**阿贾尔**：所以啊——这门今天我就算是捶，也会给它一拳捶开——！\
**Ajar**: "That is to say, I'll smash that door open, even if it takes the other arm of mine!"

**年轻村民**：哦！就是这里——好酷哦！\
**Villager 3**: Yes! That's what I'm talking about. So cool!

木棍轻轻一拨，篝火发出了清脆的噼啪声。\
As the stick pokes the bonfire, a clear snap can be heard.

**伽菈波那**：看来蛮力破门在你的意料之外？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I guess you didn't see that coming?

**鬃毛沙砾**：实不相瞒，我都做好被那扇大门弹开的准备了，就像我小时候一样四脚朝天……\
**Shamane**: To tell the truth, I had prepared myself to bounce off from that closed gate, like what had happened many times when I was a kid.

**鬃毛沙砾**：但是，哇，回想起来，我自己也觉得当时真是太酷了——\
**Shamane**: But, wow, see how I burst it open? That was cool.

男人兴奋地举起拳头，对着空气一阵手舞足蹈。\
He throws a few punches in the air excitedly.

**鬃毛沙砾**：嗬！嗬！哈——！哦！\
**Shamane**: Ho! Ho! Ha ...! Ah!

他心满意足似的收回拳头，又轻轻拨弄了一下篝火。\
He takes back his fist, content, and casually pokes the fire.

**鬃毛沙砾**：不过看来我爸的确是在哄小孩。\
**Shamane**: So, in the end, my dad was just telling nonsense to a kid.

火苗在他的眼中跳跃着。\
The flame is dancing in his eyes.

**鬃毛沙砾**：一些故弄玄虚的教导……无非是什么“足够的力量！”或者“责任心！”之类的……\
**Shamane**: Those so-called profound teachings, like one needs "adequate strength" or "a sense of responsibility" ...

**鬃毛沙砾**：这样拐弯抹角的表达方式，哈，确实是他会做的事！\
**Shamane**: Those were too abstract for a kid to understand. Ha, that's indeed his style!

**伽菈波那**：但是那扇门确确实实地开启了。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: But, in the end, the door was opened. That's for sure.

**伽菈波那**：这是个不错的结果——比起我的结局来说，要好一万倍。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: That's a good ending for a story. At least a million times better than mine.

**鬃毛沙砾**：哈哈，你离结局还早着呢！看你目前的状态，我觉得倒比最开始那副绷得紧紧的模样要好多了！\
**Shamane**: Haha, you have a long way to go before reaching the end! But I'd say you're in a much better place now than you were in the beginning.

**鬃毛沙砾**：可喜可贺，可喜可贺……\
**Shamane**: It's good progress. Trust me.

老旧的村子自山林之上望下去，只有半个掌心的大小。\
Observed from the top of the mountain, the old village is only as small as half a palm.

**鬃毛沙砾**：有遮蔽者，房门紧闭，将一切拒之门外……甚至是自己活命的机会。\
**Shamane**: He who only stays behind a closed door will turn away many things, including a chance to survive.

**坎吉拉**：好啦好啦！绝妙的烤兔子！夏尔贾，给你吃第一口！\
**Kanjira**: Alright, alright! Best roast rabbit ever! Ms. Sherjah, you have the first bite!

**伽菈波那**：无家之人……却拥有了属于自己的温暖。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: A person with no family yet radiates the warmth of family to others.

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

**伽菈波那**：……如果当初，有谁也给了库玛尔这样一个归宿，或许今天这样荒唐的事情就不会发生。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: *sighs* … If only Kumar had the slightest warmth from someone, maybe such an absurd thing would have never happened.

**鬃毛沙砾**：噢，我想她应该也不会太难过，没准儿正和咱们一样，坐在这样绝妙的角度，欣赏什么湿婆之舞呢！\
**Shamane**: I doubt she's upset about what happened. Maybe she has found herself a good seat to enjoy this dance of Shiva!

**伽菈波那**：嗯，她确实会选择一个视野优良的观众席。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: That's true. She is the kind of person who always finds herself the best seat to watch the show.

**鬃毛沙砾**：比起那些，我更想知道的是，她当时有没有说我什么坏话啊？\
**Shamane**: But, I'm curious. Tell me, did she say anything bad about me?

**伽菈波那**：坏话倒是没有……她只是承认了自己的报复心理……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: That was not a part of our conversation. She just admitted that she was being vindictive.

她微微皱眉，希望能从混乱的记忆中拾起碎片。\
Kaalaa Baunaa slightly frowns, hoping to find some clues in the chaotic memories.

**伽菈波那**：“……正如你们所说，是仇恨所致的报复心理吧。”\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: "Maybe I was being vindictive out of hatred, like you said."

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

她突然像是被篝火烫到了一般，迅速地从草地上爬了起来。\
She suddenly jumps up, as if she were burned by the bonfire.

**伽菈波那**：“正如你们所说”？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: "Like you said"?

**伽菈波那**：幻境中是不会有这样具体的……从理论上来说也不可能做到……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: The Realm can never extract every word I've said. It's theoretically impossible.

**伽菈波那**：这句话……她，她是从哪里听到的？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: How ... Where-where did she hear that part?

## JMP-14 博识者美餐 / Feast for the Savant

**伽菈波那**：难道她当时就在那间屋子里？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: She was in the same room?

**伽菈波那**：……这可能吗？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: How could it be?

伽菈波那轻轻掐动自己的掌心，试图以痛感让自己保持冷静。\
Kaalaa Baunaa pinches herself to keep calm.

**鬃毛沙砾**：以我对那间房子的了解……咱们几乎走遍了每一寸能走的地方——除非她挂在了天花板上。\
**Shamane**: I know that room well. We have searched every inch of it—Unless she was hanging on the ceiling right above us.

**伽菈波那**：但就像我刚才说的，她总是……总是选择观众席的最佳位置。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: But, as I said, she always finds herself the best seat.

**伽菈波那**：“既能与讲台上的瞩目者心照不宣，又能清晰地感受到周围的窃窃私语……”\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: "To be someone who can smile knowingly at the argument made by the lecturer, knowing full well the thinking process behind, while staying close to other whispering opinions."

**伽菈波那**：一个……置身事内的绝佳观景位。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: "Like a perfect observatory from which we witness the events in the universe."

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

迷雾慢慢自眼前散去。\
The fog has lifted.

**伽菈波那**：或许我一直都想错了。她并不是为了报复村子才创造了这场星体坠落……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Maybe I've been in the wrong direction. She didn't make the star fall as revenge on the village.

仰起头，天空晴朗得没有一丝云彩，星辰像是毗湿奴随手撒入乳海的一抔银沙。\
She looks up. The sky is completely cloudless, and the stars look just like the silver sand randomly scattered into the Samudra by Vishnu.

**伽菈波那**：那时，我们相遇的，幻境里的天空……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: The sky in the Realm when we met ...

肮脏玻璃器皿的表面般的天空再次浮现在了眼前。\
She recalls the sky in the Realm, which was like the surface of dusted glassware.

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

**伽菈波那**：鬃毛沙砾先生……她不是在天花板上。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Mr. Shamane, she was not on the ceiling.

**鬃毛沙砾**：你当真了？我只是想开个活跃气氛的玩笑……\
**Shamane**: Are you taking me seriously? That was just a joke to lighten up the mood.

**伽菈波那**：是……在地下。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: But, under the ground.

**鬃毛沙砾**：……\
**Shamane**: ...

伽菈波那缓缓抽出自己悄悄塞到腰间的相片。这张小小的纸片曾被浸湿，如今，表面的潮湿在篝火的烘烤下尽数退去。\
Kaalaa Baunaa pulls a photo slowly from her waist. It was soaked when she was in the vat, but now it is almost dried by the bonfire.

**伽菈波那**：夹着它的那本《地下生存手册》……她就在那间屋子的正下方。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Remember the Underground Survival Guide, where we found this photo? She's right under that house.

村民被疏散一空，夜晚的街道除了游荡的重塑门徒以外空无一人。\
The street is empty. All the villagers have been evacuated. There are only Manus followers wandering about at night.

**伽菈波那**：先去拐角那里……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: First, to the corner ...

但有人重新回到了这里。\
And the ones who have returned.

**鬃毛沙砾**：你们真是太疯狂了……简直超出了我的认知！\
**Shamane**: This is crazy. It has gone beyond my imagination!

**伽菈波那**：……很抱歉，其实你不用和我一起来的……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Sorry, but you don't have to come with me.

**鬃毛沙砾**：唉，这时候就别再和我说这个了。\
**Shamane**: *sighs* Say no more on that.

两个人影鬼鬼祟祟地从一个墙角溜到了另外一个墙角。\
The two sneak from one corner to another.

**鬃毛沙砾**：不让我亲眼见到我姐，我真的会被自己的好奇心折磨疯！究竟是怎么样的人才能硬生生挖出个地下室来……\
**Shamane**: If you don't let me see my own sister, I will be dying for answers! Who would dig a basement here?

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

**伽菈波那**：这你倒是提醒我了，库玛尔也有一部分——不，很大一部分，是因为她自己的好奇心才做了这种事。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: That reminds me. Her curiosity is one of the, well, the major reason she did that.

**伽菈波那**：她很可能在那次回乡假的时候就做足了准备……我以为她只是说说而已，没想到她早就预料到了我们要被踢出那个项目。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: It's possible that she was well-prepared last time she came back to Mor Pankh. I never thought she foresaw that we would be kicked out from the project.

**鬃毛沙砾**：所以，就像你刚刚推测的，她是为了亲眼见到那颗星星才做了这种事？\
**Shamane**: And as you just deduced, she did so to see that star?

**伽菈波那**：几乎是百分之百的可能性。离开了我之后，她的神秘术支持很可能全部来自于重塑之手。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Almost 100% sure. Without me, she must have asked the Manus to support her with arcane skills.

**伽菈波那**：——先走这边。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: This way.

闪过了还在游荡的重塑门徒，隐约已经可以看到老屋的门口。\
After avoiding the wandering Manus followers, they can almost see the entrance to the old house.

**伽菈波那**：她离开我的时候，精神就已经很不稳定了……这时候重塑那种组织想要招揽她，几乎只要轻轻推一下。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: She was extremely mentally unstable when she left me. It wouldn't take any effort if the Manus had the intention to recruit her.

**伽菈波那**：……她这次，根本没打算活着看完这场烛星节的流星雨。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Watching the meteor shower and being destroyed by it has been her plan all along.

**鬃毛沙砾**：很难说，明知可能会跟她同归于尽的咱俩，能比她强到哪里去。尽管我不愿意承认，但有时神秘学家的血液就是这么神奇！\
**Shamane**: At this point, it is hard to say who is worse, she or we, since we have prepared to die with her evil plan. However reluctant I am to admit this, sometimes arcanists are indeed strange creatures.

**鬃毛沙砾**：——这下咱们就像疯子开会了！哈哈哈……！\
**Shamane**: Heh heh ... It's like a madhouse party! Hahaha!

**鬃毛沙砾**：不过，你临走之前，教玛蒂尔达的那个是什么啊？\
**Shamane**: But what did you teach Matilda before we left?

**伽菈波那**：……是面对库玛尔幻境的唯一胜算……我在计算坠星灾害范围时想到的。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: That's our only chance to survive in her Realm. I came up with it when I was calculating the range of the fallen star damage.

**鬃毛沙砾**：……\
**Shamane**: ...

**鬃毛沙砾**：我就说你像只虎崽子——你那时候都没放弃要给你的对手一口。\
**Shamane**: As I said, you are the tiger cub, trying to take a bite in the arm, even when the hunter has had you in her grip.

**伽菈波那**：那个方法原本只有我们两人知道。我计算过，一旦增加更多的观测者，幻境就有可能坍塌。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: That method was between Kumar and me. There is another theory according to my calculation: if there are more observers, the Realm might collapse.

**伽菈波那**：那是唯一一条库玛尔不知道的理论……也是一条未经过严格实验的理论。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: It's the only theory Kumar doesn't know. At the same time, it is not yet strictly verified.

**伽菈波那**：但我相信那个孩子……她确实是个天才。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: But I have faith in that girl. She is indeed a genius.

**伽菈波那**：——只希望现在还是我们孤注一掷的好时机。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I hope it's not too late to make our last attempt.

**鬃毛沙砾**：……嗯，要我说，还说早了两分钟。\
**Shamane**: Hmm, if you ask me, it's not yet the time to make that attempt.

**伽菈波那**：什么……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: What?

二人几乎就要踏入那间旧屋的门槛。\
They are only one step away from the old house.

隆隆的巨响声中，巨大的湿婆神像拔地而起。\
A huge Shiva statue rises with the loud rumble.

**鬃毛沙砾**：看来是她留给咱的开胃前菜。\
**Shamane**: Haha! This must be the appetizer she served us.

**鬃毛沙砾**：——唉，伟大的湿婆神啊，但愿您的拳头打在我们身上就像那些脆球饼一样酥！\
