**Shamane**: *sighs* Great Shiva, I hope your fists feel as light and crispy as pani puri when they land on my body!

**伽菈波那**：呼……呼……真不容易。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: *pants* That's tough.

**鬃毛沙砾**：喂，你看那里……\
**Shamane**: Hey, look over there!

老屋的地板被石像破坏出了一道缝隙。\
The statue's attack has left a crack in the floor of the old house.

**伽菈波那**：……底下果然是，空的。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: It is empty down there.

## JMP-15 新观星者们 / The New Stargazers

**？？？**：♪～\
**???**: ♪

**收音机**：……流星雨将于今日凌晨四时降落，届时，彗星也将……\
**Radio**: The shower is estimated to fall at 4 a.m. today. By then, the comet will also ...

**？？？**：还有……三个半小时。噢，哦对了……音乐——\
**???**: Three and a half hours to go. Oh, almost forgot about this—music.

**？？？**：♪～\
**???**: ♪

幽暗逼仄的空间内，小提琴的声音悠然响起。\
In this dark, confined space, there arises a melody played on the violin.

这并不像是一个人类居住的空间。\
The place looks nothing like a livable space for humans.

墙上，桌上，地上。目光所及之处的平面几乎都被密密麻麻的演算纸尽数淹没。而粗糙的抹制墙壁上，刻满了密密麻麻的计数日期。\
The walls, the table, the floor ... Every surface in sight is covered with paper of seamless formulas. The only exception is a roughly plastered wall, which is full of symbols marking the passing of days.

一个老式望远镜立在演算纸之间，指向不存在的天空。\
An old telescope is standing in the mess, pointing at the blocked sky.

**鬃毛沙砾**：咳，咳咳……喂，你没摔倒吧……\
**Shamane**: *coughs* You alright?

**伽菈波那**：……我，我没事，刚刚好能下……来。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I-I'm fine. It's not too high for me.

二人踉跄地顺着缝隙滑了下来。\
They slide down through the crack.

伽菈波那扑落着尘土站起身。\
Kaalaa Baunaa gets back on her feet, patting the dust off her.

——然后僵在了原地。\
And then, she freezes.

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

**伽菈波那**：库玛尔……！\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Kumar!

**伽菈波那**：你怎么……变成了这个样子。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: What ... what happened to you?

**库玛尔**：噢，怎么……人来得这样齐？\
**Kumar**: Oh, well. I didn't expect so many visitors.

她显得有些恍惚。\
She seems a bit absent-minded.

**库玛尔**：既然来了，那请坐吧。这地方我自己修的。不大，隔音也差——\
**Kumar**: But since you're here, please take a seat. I built this place by myself. It's not a big room and not soundproof.

**库玛尔**：噢，你们在上面搜我房子时，我听得一清二楚——《犊牛的饲养与管理》，怎么就不能让天文学家读了？\
**Kumar**: Yes, I heard you very clearly under the ground when you searched the room and went through my stuff. What's wrong about an astronomer reading "Calf Feeding and Management"?

她颤颤巍巍地挪动着步子，喃喃自语着。\
She paces around shakily, muttering to herself.

**库玛尔**：你们……你们应该走的。唔，我现在已经不想……\
**Kumar**: You ... you should have left. Hmm, my plan has chan- ... changed.

**库玛尔**：……\
**Kumar**: ...

**库玛尔**：算了，算啦……这叫什么……命运？伽菈波那，你懂这个，对吧？\
**Kumar**: Let it be. Let it be. What do they call this? Destiny? You know about destiny, right, Kaalaa Baunaa?

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

**库玛尔**：和我一起看星星……挺好，挺好……就像以前一样。\
**Kumar**: Watching the stars with me. Good, good. It's like living the old days again.

她转过头，目光落在了鬃毛沙砾身上。\
She turns around. Her gaze falls on Shamane.

**鬃毛沙砾**：库玛……姐姐。\
**Shamane**: Kumar. Sister.

**库玛尔**：……\
**Kumar**: ...

**库玛尔**：呵呵……姐姐……姐姐……\
**Kumar**: Haha. Sister. Sister ...

她的嘴角向上扯了扯，又快速地垂了下去。\
A fleeting sneer appears on her lips.

伽菈波那的眉头紧锁。\
Kaalaa Baunaa frowns deeply.

**伽菈波那**：你明明，在幻境里不还是挺正——重塑之手到底对你做了什么？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: You looked much better in the Realm. What did the Manus do to you?

**库玛尔**：重塑？噢，他们挺好的，他们帮了我很多，厉害的神秘术，实验器械，还有……食物，很多的食物。\
**Kumar**: The Manus? Oh, they're fine. Helps me a lot. Impressive arcane skills, experiment apparatus, and food—lots of food.

顺着她的指尖望过去，烤饼堆满了一个角落，密密匝匝地爬着不知名的小虫。\
Following Kumar's fingertip, they see a pile of naans in the corner, which are under a layer of unknown insects.

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

**伽菈波那**：这，这……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: These are ...

**鬃毛沙砾**：……看起来不是她不去指挥那些游荡的重塑……只是她已经没有能力了。\
**Shamane**: Seems like she's no longer capable of commanding those wandering Manus.

他如今已经不会再惊讶于自己的冷静。\
He would have panicked, but he is calm this time.

鬃毛沙砾压低声音，小声提醒着伫立在原地的伽菈波那。\
He reminds Kaalaa Baunaa in a whisper.

**鬃毛沙砾**：但当务之急，先看看能不能阻止那颗星星，剩下的——\
**Shamane**: But the priority is to stop that star. We can deal with the rest ...

**库玛尔**：星星？你们要阻止那颗星星——你们又要！又要抢走我的星星！！\
**Kumar**: The star? You're going to stop the comet. You are taking it from me? Again?!

**伽菈波那**：库玛——啊！\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Kumar. Argh!!

原本恍惚的女人像是被打开了什么开关，突然爆发出了巨大的力量，一把将即将靠近的二人推了出去。\
Kumar, who was absent-minded a second ago, seems to be triggered now. She suddenly pushes the two out with enormous strength.

**库玛尔**：我绝不会……\
**Kumar**: I will never ...

周围逼仄的空间开始融解。\
The confined space starts melting.

**鬃毛沙砾**：……！\
**Shamane**: ...!

地下室不复存在。\
The basement is no longer there.

原本逼仄的空间变得广阔无垠，宇宙像幕布一般在眼前展开。星云在脚下翻滚着，柔软、轻盈、乖巧，如同孩童的安抚毯。\
Instead, the space opens up, unfolding before them like the vast universe. Nebulas are churning beneath their feet, like a colorful, harmless mist.

库玛尔伫立在虚幻的宇宙中，如同伫立在舞台的中央。\
Kumar stands in the void, like standing in the middle of a grand stage.

**库玛尔**：我绝不会让任何人阻止它——！\
**Kumar**: I will never let anyone set their hands on it!

## JMP-16 无昼无夜 / Neither Day Nor Night

**鬃毛沙砾**：呼，呼……\
**Shamane**: *pants*

**鬃毛沙砾**：我，呕——我要吐了。幻境里怎么……\
**Shamane**: I-I'm gonna throw up. It feels strange in here.

鬃毛沙砾脚步虚浮，一屁股跌坐在地上。\
Shamane feels his legs weaken. He sinks to the floor.

**鬃毛沙砾**：哦……哦……那是我师父的脸吗……呕……\
**Shamane**: ... Was that Master's face?

**鬃毛沙砾**：我还——可以——\
**Shamane**: I-I can keep up.

**伽菈波那**：……第一次进来的人是会不太习惯。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: It's hard to get used to it for the first time.

伽菈波那气息不匀，死死地盯着在幻境里恢复了状态的库玛尔。\
Though panting unstably, Kaalaa Baunaa is still staring at Kumar, who has regained elegance in the Realm.

**库玛尔**：还是在这里更舒服一些。很抱歉，伽菈波那。我想现实中的我已经没办法体面地与你久别重逢了。\
**Kumar**: I feel a lot better in here. I'm sorry, Kaalaa Baunaa. I don't think this body of mine can hold any longer for a more appropriate meeting in the real world.

**库玛尔**：你能回来找我，我很高兴——我承认，那些话是有些重了。\
**Kumar**: I'm glad you came back for me. What I said was indeed too harsh.

库玛尔又变回了她熟悉的样子。\
Kumar has turned back to herself.

**伽菈波那**：库玛尔……你为什么即便要变成那个样子，也要……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Kumar, why do you have to ...? Look at you. The price is too high.

**库玛尔**：……\
**Kumar**: ...

**库玛尔**：唔，在最开始的时候，我的想法确实没那么单纯。\
**Kumar**: Hmm, in the first instance, I did have other intentions.

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

**库玛尔**：我一直想象着，那对抛弃了我的父母，被这颗星星砸到脸上时，他们会是什么表情。\
**Kumar**: I kept imagining how my so-called "parents" would react when they were about to get crushed to pieces by the star.

**库玛尔**：……但我没想到，他们已经自食其果了。\
**Kumar**: Little did I know, they have already paid for what they've done.

她将目光移向远处那个不断干呕的身影，又飞速地挪了回来。\
Kumar casts a quick glance at her puking brother and looks back at Kaalaa Baunaa.

**库玛尔**：我付出了一切，但却没了目标。呵呵……那滋味真不好受。\
**Kumar**: I worked myself to the bone, but who knew I would lose everything, including my purpose? It really sucks.

**库玛尔**：但无所谓，这是个小小的挫折——远小于我曾经历过的那些……甚至不值一提。\
**Kumar**: But it's okay. Just a minor setback. Compared to what I've been through, it's not even worth mentioning.

**库玛尔**：所以，在最后，我改变了主意。\
**Kumar**: That's why I changed my mind.

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

**库玛尔**：……我想见见它。\
**Kumar**: I want to see it.

**伽菈波那**：见到那颗……看不到的星星……？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: To see it? The star we can't see with our eyes?

**库玛尔**：看来是我神智不清的时候，用词不够严谨了。\
**Kumar**: Seems like I was not very careful about my wording when my mind was clouded.

**库玛尔**：——那个天体。伽菈波那，那不是一颗星——它甚至可能是一个……运动着的黑洞。\
**Kumar**: It is a celestial body, Kaalaa Baunaa, not a star. It could even be a ... moving black hole.

她举起双手，那神态不像在星云散布的幻境中，更像是在研究所，在黑板前，在伽菈波那无数次投向她的求知的目光里。\
Kumar lifts her palms, like she has done so many times in Kaalaa Baunaa's inquisitive gaze and in the lecture hall of the university.

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

**伽菈波那**：……我倒宁愿你只是因为，恨那些抛弃你的人，甚至是恨我……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I'd rather you did this out of the hatred towards the people who abandoned you, or even towards me ...

**伽菈波那**：恨我因为粗心大意暴露了神秘学家的身份，导致你……失去了……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ... for I carelessly exposed my identity as an arcanist, and thus you lost your ...

**库玛尔**：我也想，我太想去恨一个人了——但是我做不到，孩子。\
**Kumar**: I wish the same. I wish so badly that I could just be filled with pure hatred towards someone. But I can't, kid.

她再次看向在幻境中晕眩的鬃毛沙砾。\
Once again, Kumar looks at Shamane. He still feels dizzy.

**库玛尔**：你很好运，弟弟。我那次本来是盘算着揍你一顿的，但是，看着那样一无所知的你……我下不去手。\
**Kumar**: You're the lucky one, young brother. I was going to kick your butt in our last encounter, but ... I just couldn't do it.

**鬃毛沙砾**：……\
**Shamane**: ...

**伽菈波那**：可是你，你因为重塑……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: But the Manus has made you ...

**库玛尔**：噢，孩子，班纳尔大学能让我发SCI，而重塑能让我触及宇宙……这二者对我来说并无不同。\
**Kumar**: Kid. Banner University can get my name on the SCI list, while the Manus allows me to touch the universe. They are not that different to me.

**鬃毛沙砾**：……老姐，母亲和我提及过——你的体质无法承受这样强度的神秘术，重塑他们应该知道这个！\
**Shamane**: Sister, Mother told me about this. You physically can't take such a great amount of arcanum in you! The Manus should also know this!

**库玛尔**：……我很感谢他们还记得我，但我是自愿的。\
**Kumar**: I appreciate that they remembered this about me, but this is the path I chose.

库玛尔低头，看着脚下涌动的星云。\
Kumar looks down at the swirling nebula.

**库玛尔**：当我抬头仰望星空的时候，原本是我最自由的时候。\
**Kumar**: When I look into the sky, I feel myself the freest being in the world.

**库玛尔**：宇宙，它可以包容你的一切——无论你是神秘学家、人类，甚至是一粒小小的土……它都会包容你。\
**Kumar**: The universe, what a vast, life-embracing place it is! No matter if you're an arcanist, or a human, even a grain of sand ... it encompassed everything.

**库玛尔**：可我却因为最微不足道的事情，被逐出了我自己的事业，逐出了我的家庭。\
**Kumar**: But I was driven away from studying it, abandoned by my own family, for some insignificant, unimportant reasons.

**鬃毛沙砾**：……\
**Shamane**: ...

**库玛尔**：我早该明白的……我这样的挣扎，在这颗星球上毫无意义。\
**Kumar**: I should have understood this earlier ... that my struggle means nothing on this planet.

**库玛尔**：我累了，伽菈波那，我只想见见它。\
**Kumar**: I'm tired, Kaalaa Baunaa. I just want to see that celestial body with my own eyes.

**伽菈波那**：可是，库玛尔……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: But, Kumar ...

伽菈波那试图注视她的眼睛。\
Kaalaa Baunaa tries to stare into her eyes.

**伽菈波那**：星星不是这样看的，望远镜不应该放在地下室，不应垂下头颅……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: That's not how you look at a star. The telescope shouldn't be placed in a basement, and you shouldn't lower your head.

**伽菈波那**：库玛尔，你已经有多久，没见过夜空，没看见过那些其他的星星了——\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Kumar, how long has it been since the last time you looked up at the night sky, at the other stars?

**伽菈波那**：而且……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: What's more ...

伽菈波那的神情变得严肃。\
Kaalaa Baunaa looks grave.

**伽菈波那**：这颗天体如果真的落下，整个村子的人——包括那些孩子，将无一人幸免。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: If the star falls, people in the village, including those kids—none of them will survive.

**伽菈波那**：你操控的重塑……也已经伤害了太多的人，破坏了太多的家庭。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: The Manus you summoned here has brought disaster to this place, to the people and their families.

**伽菈波那**：——他们不应该为你的愿望陪葬。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: They are not the sacrifice of your wish.

**伽菈波那**：……不要再一意孤行地继续下去了，库玛尔。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Stop heading down the wrong path, Kumar.

憔悴冲破了体面的躯壳，映在库玛尔的眉宇间。\
Weariness reigns over Kumar.

而后，她扬起眉毛，摇了摇头，好像这些事情并不严重，而伽菈波那只是提出了一个无理的、无价值的研究提案。\
She raises her eyebrows and shakes her head slowly, as if nothing matters to her anymore.

**库玛尔**：……\
**Kumar**: ...

**库玛尔**：你知道吗？我不在乎那些。\
**Kumar**: You know what? I don't care about them.

**库玛尔**：——从来也没人在乎过我，不是吗？\
**Kumar**: Just like they've never cared about me, have they?

她轻轻摇了摇头。\
Kumar denies her, like she did when Kaalaa Baunaa pitched a terrible research proposal.

**库玛尔**：抱歉，这是我最后的愿望了。\
**Kumar**: Sorry, please indulge me with one last willful act.

库玛尔抬起手臂，幻境中的星星排列成了一条直线。\
As Kumar raises her arms, the stars in the Realm form a straight line.

**库玛尔**：我只想走我选择的路。\
**Kumar**: This is the path I chose.

**库玛尔**：你无法阻止我，伽菈波那。\
**Kumar**: And you can't stop me, Kaalaa Baunaa.

**库玛尔**：嗯？\
**Kumar**: Hmm?

清脆的碎裂声自宇宙深处响起，一声接着一声。\
Clear cracks come from the depths of the universe, one after another.

**库玛尔**：什么……\
**Kumar**: What?

**伽菈波那**：……看来是玛蒂尔达他们赶上了！\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: It's Matilda! They made it!

**玛蒂尔达**：快！快！学会了吗？没错……伽菈波那小姐就是这样教的……\
**Matilda**: Hurry! Quickly! Do you understand? Yes, that's what Ms. Kaalaa Baunaa taught me to do.

**坎吉拉**：唔，可是闭上眼睛的话，什么也看不到啊？\
**Kanjira**: Hmm. But I can't see anything when my eyes are closed.

**玛蒂尔达**：不要用你的眼睛……握好了这颗水晶，深呼吸——\
**Matilda**: Don't rely on the eyes. Hold this crystal and take a deep breath.

几个孩子贴着玛蒂尔达，他们在篝火边，坐成了一个不完美的圆。\
The kids sit next to Matilda, forming an imperfect circle by the fire.

外围，以阿贾尔为首的几个人类孩子好奇地探头探脑。\
Outside this little circle, the human kids are peering around curiously.

星穹之下，篝火旁的众人深吸了一口气，将手叠放在一枚小小的神像上。\
Under the starry sky, the ones sitting by the fire take a deep breath and put their hands on a small idol.

**坎吉拉**：去感受……她怎么说的来着？\
**Kanjira**: To feel, emm, what she said?

**路人男孩**：宇宙的变化……\
**Passer-by Boy**: The change of the universe.

星空寂静。\
The starry sky is completely quiet.

**玛蒂尔达**：……！\
**Matilda**: ...!

**玛蒂尔达**：流星雨提前开始了！！\
**Matilda**: The meteor shower is starting earlier!

**库玛尔**：……你做了什么？\
**Kumar**: What did you do?

**伽菈波那**：咳咳……只有咱们两个掌握的技巧，库玛尔。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: *coughs* That's the method only once known between you and me, Kumar.

**库玛尔**：观测技巧？\
**Kumar**: The observation method?

**库玛尔**：你把“宇宙之卵”的观测方法告诉了别人？\
**Kumar**: You told others about the Celestial Egg?

**库玛尔**：那又怎……\
**Kumar**: So wh- ...

她止住了话头。\
She stops herself.

是的，她唯一的天赋就是聪慧——\
She's always the clever one.

**库玛尔**：……我懂了，我懂了。你提交过这个研究方向……\
**Kumar**: I see, I see. You once pitched that research proposal to me.

她脸上的表情称得上欣慰。\
An almost gratified look appears on her face.

**库玛尔**：你确实是我最好的学生，伽菈波那。\
**Kumar**: You are indeed my best student, Kaalaa Baunaa.

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

**伽菈波那**：我之后终于明白你为何一直要求我守口如瓶——尽管我们称那个东西为“卵”……但它仍然是宇宙的投影，拥有宇宙的特性。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I finally understand why you asked me to keep it a secret. Even if we named it Egg, it's actually a projection of the universe, which has the same feature.

**伽菈波那**：宇宙是无限的……只要我有意识地，以自己为原点开始观测……我就变为了宇宙中心。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: The universe is infinite, as long as we observe it self-consciously, think each of ourselves as one of the centers of the universe.

**库玛尔**：……\
**Kumar**: ...

**伽菈波那**：“卵”会因为观测中心的增多而逐渐碎裂，坍缩……直到恢复寂灭，连同那颗星一起。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: The Egg will then collapse because of multiple centers, until it puts a quietus on everything, including that star.

**伽菈波那**：——只要拳头足够多，镜子就会完全破碎，不是吗？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: A shattered mirror will never be pieced together again, if there are enough forces to break it. Am I right?

**伽菈波那**：“于那时日，混沌中空无一物。存在者与非存在者皆无，无至上之域，无大气，无天穹。”\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: "Then there was neither existence nor non-existence; there was neither the realm of space nor the sky beyond."

**库玛尔**：……\
**Kumar**: ...

**库玛尔**：是谁？那群顽固的老家伙们？\
**Kumar**: Who could master these skills? Those old fogeys in the village?

**伽菈波那**：一个天才小姑娘……和一群抬头看过星空的孩子……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: A genius girl and a bunch of kids who looked up at the stars.

就像你当初带着我那样。\
"Just like you and me in the beginning."

伽菈波那嘴唇翕动，将这几个不合时宜的音节吞入了腹中。\
Kaalaa Baunna's lips quietly move, but none of those words come out.

**伽菈波那**：很抱歉，库玛尔……这次我，不，我们一定要阻止你。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I'm sorry, Kumar. I have to—no, we have to—stop you this time.

**伽菈波那**：我不能看着你毁了摩卢旁卡——\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I can't let you destroy Mor Pankh ...

她不是敌人——至少现在，这并非是一场对抗。\
They are not enemies. At least for now, this is not a confrontation.

**伽菈波那**：更不能看着你这样毁了自己。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ... or destroy yourself.

## Part 17 Neither Day Nor Night

**鬃毛沙砾**：——这里快塌了！我们快离开……\
**Shamane**: It's about to collapse! Got to go now.

**伽菈波那**：库玛尔！库玛尔——！\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Kumar! KUMAR!!

她奋力向前伸出手去，试图够到那抹破碎的身影。\
She extends her arm as far as possible, reaching for that figure.

**伽菈波那**：呃啊……！\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Ah!

巨大的土块落下，阻断了她们之间的路。\
A giant rock falls between them. Kumar is lost in her sight.

粗糙的地下室彻底坍塌，月光自早已不存在的天花板上散落下来。\
The shabby basement has completely collapsed. Moonlight floats down through the ceiling that no longer exists.

**伽菈波那**：咳，咳咳……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: *coughs*

**伽菈波那**：……鬃毛沙砾先生，你帮我挡了……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Mr. Shamane, you covered me.

男人拂开肩上的尘土。\
He pats the dust off his shoulder.

**鬃毛沙砾**：我没事。\
**Shamane**: I'm fine.

他将目光投向远处。\
He looks in the other direction.

**鬃毛沙砾**：……\
**Shamane**: ...

伽菈波那顺着他的目光望去。\
Kaalaa Baunaa follows his gaze and sees Kumar.

**库玛尔**：真漂亮啊……\
**Kumar**: Pretty ...

衣衫褴褛，头发带着点花白的女人像是不熟悉这个动作似的，缓缓地抬起了头。\
The ragged woman with gray hair looks up slowly at the night sky.

夜空之中，几颗流星带着辉煌的尾焰划破了深色的天穹。\
Several meteors are crossing the sky with glaring tails.

**库玛尔**：……\
**Kumar**: ...

**鬃毛沙砾**：幻境破灭，坠落的天体消失了……\
**Shamane**: Her Realm has gone, taking that falling star with it.

**鬃毛沙砾**：只有流星雨一如往日地落下……\
**Shamane**: Tonight, only the meteor shower will sparkle in the sky.

**伽菈波那**：……库玛尔……库玛尔！\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Kumar. Kumar!

同样一身狼狈的女人踉跄着跑向那个正抬头看向夜空的身影。\
Kaalaa Baunaa, who is now also ragged, staggers toward the one staring at the night sky.

不安爬上了她的背脊。\
She's haunted by an ominous feeling.

快一点，快一些，像以前一样，重新握住……\
Faster, even faster, get to her side like she used to ...

**伽菈波那**：……库玛尔。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Kumar.

伽菈波那终于握住了她的双手。\
Finally, Kaalaa Baunaa holds Kumar's hands.

**伽菈波那**：库玛尔……我还在，我们……先回去怎么样？\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: I'm still here, Kumar. How about we ... go back first?

**库玛尔**：回去？\
**Kumar**: Go back?

**伽菈波那**：对，回去，回到研究所，回到大学里面——\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Yes, go back to the institution, to the university ...

她说不下去了。\
She cannot continue.

**库玛尔**：眼前人似乎已经听不懂她所说的一切，只是拧着眉毛，疑惑地看着她。\
**Kumar**: It seems Kumar can no longer understand her words. She just frowns and stares at her in confusion.

**库玛尔**：……\
**Kumar**: ...

**库玛尔**：忽然，她的眉头舒展开来，笑着摇了摇头。\
**Kumar**: Suddenly, she relaxes her eyebrows and smiles while shaking her head.

**库玛尔**：我没有可以回去的地方。\
**Kumar**: There's no place I can go back to.

**伽菈波那**：有！有的……我会接你到我那里，你去我的研究所，我们还能从头开始……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Yes, there is! You can stay at my place. You can use my lab. We can start over.

**库玛尔**：……\
**Kumar**: ...

**库玛尔**：可以呀。\
**Kumar**: Sure.

**伽菈波那**：真的吗？你真的愿意……走！那咱们先离开这里……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Really? You will? Let's go then! Leave this place first.

伽菈波那迅速起身，像是怕对方反悔似的拽住她的胳膊转身就走。\
Kaalaa Baunaa gets up quickly and holds Kumar's arm in hers. She drags Kumar to leave, seemingly afraid that Kumar may change her mind.

**库玛尔**：不过我需要带些资料离开，你先放开我。\
**Kumar**: But there are some papers I need to take with me. Let go of my arm.

库玛尔在她身后轻轻说道。\
Says Kumar behind Kaalaa Baunaa. She sounds quite relaxed.

**伽菈波那**：……好。\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Okay.

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

她觉得自己有点不敢回头，只得抬头看向对面男人的面孔。\
Somehow, Kaalaa Baunaa dares not look back. She can only look up at Shamane's face.

**伽菈波那**：鬃毛沙砾先生……库玛尔说会和我们离开！她要去拿些东西……很快……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Mr. Sharma, Kumar says she'll come with us! She just needs to take some papers. It won't take long!

**鬃毛沙砾**：男人缓缓地摇了摇头。\
**Shamane**: He slowly shakes his head.

**伽菈波那**：……\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ...

鬃毛沙砾的眼神比任何一个时刻都平静。他望着库玛尔的方向，却又不像是在看着她。\
Shamane never feels this calm. He looks at his sister, but he feels he is looking at someone else.

他望向的，是一个等待解脱的疲惫灵魂。\
He is looking at a weary soul waiting for her final salvation.

她或许是这个世界上最后一位与自己血脉相连的人。\
She is his last kin.

但他决定尊重她的选择。\
And he is going to respect her decision.

**库玛尔**：“无死无生，无昼无夜。”\
**Kumar**: "Then there was neither death nor immortality; there was neither day nor night."

**库玛尔**：每个人都能回去……多好的地方啊。\
**Kumar**: Everyone has a place to go back to. What a nice world to live in.

女人轻车熟路地走向坍塌之处的一隅，从其中摸出一把泛着黑色的小巧东西。\
Kumar is familiar with the space, even if it's a ruin now. She reaches a corner and takes out a black gadget.

这是在第一次接触重塑时，她开口向他们索要的唯一物品。\
It is the only item she has ever asked from Manus Vindictae.

从那之后——直到现在，它终于再次被她握在掌心。\
And now, for the second and the last time, she places her hand on it.

**库玛尔**：希望下次……宇宙再次将我重构的时候，不要让我再来到这样的世界啦。\
**Kumar**: I hope ... when the universe constructs me for a second time, I will not come to this world again.

“砰——”\
Bang!

**阿贾尔**：哦哦……这里就是昌迪加尔！太酷了！\
**Ajar**: Wow! So this is what Chandigarh look like! It slay!

**路人女孩**：那是什么……糖果吗？\
**Passerby**: What's this? Candy?

**阿贾尔**：这边，快来这边……\
**Ajar**: This way. Come over here.

尽管门前崎岖的土路如今早已变为了平坦的街道，但从旧村搬至新城的住民仍旧沿袭着他们以往的习俗。\
The once rugged paths have been turned into smooth roads. In this new city, the villagers still carry on their old customs.

春日的夜晚，点点烛火照亮了移居者们居住的每条大街小巷。\
Candles have lit up every street for the new immigrants on this spring night.

**鬃毛沙砾**：哦哦。原来你只是个协助教员啊！怪不得申请的时候这么麻烦。\
**Shamane**: Ah. So you're only an assistant! No wonder they made you go through so many procedures earlier.

**坎吉拉**：什么？原来你是个半吊子呀！嘻嘻……\
**Kanjira**: Haha. What? So you is just rookie?

**玛蒂尔达**：可恶！不准你再说！哼，当心点……等你到基金会，我一定要给你好看！\
**Matilda**: Shut up! I won't allow another word of it! Humph, you'd better be careful; otherwise, you will regret your doings when you get to the Foundation!

**坎吉拉**：噗呲！\
**Kanjira**: Heh heh.

**玛蒂尔达**：你还冲我做鬼脸——你别跑！\
**Matilda**: Did you just make a face to me? Stop right there!

**基金会人员**：夏尔贾女士和……鬃毛沙砾先生。\
**Foundation Member**: Ms. Sherjah and Mr. Sharma.

**基金会人员**：非常感谢你们二人对基金会成员的支援。\
**Foundation Member**: Thank you so much for helping our staff.

**夏尔贾老师**：呃，没有……我只是帮了一点小忙——\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Emm, you flattered me. I just did what I could.

**基金会人员**：不，女士。您的行为我们已尽数知悉……\
**Foundation Member**: No, madam, we've ascertained your achievement.

**基金会人员**：在此之前，您志愿救助了神秘学家与人类孩童10余名，在此次行动中，您共救助神秘学家30余名……\
**Foundation Member**: Before this incident, you volunteered to help over 10 arcanists and human children, and this time you rescued more than 30 arcanists.

**基金会人员**：非常了不起的成绩，女士。\
**Foundation Member**: That's remarkable, madam.

身着基金会制服的女性似乎在面具之下对她微微一笑，随即递出了一张灰白色的信封。\
The woman in the Foundation uniform seems to be smiling at Sherjah and passes over a gray envelope.

**夏尔贾老师**：这是……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: What's this ...

**基金会人员**：圣洛夫基金会的入职介绍信。\
**Foundation Member**: A letter of introduction to the St. Pavlov Foundation.

**夏尔贾老师**：……！\
**Ms. Sherjah**: ...!

**基金会人员**：您也知道，基金会驻昌迪加尔分部目前仍在建设中，我们非常欢迎像您这样富有责任心的人类成员加入。\
**Foundation Member**: I'm sure you know our branch in Chandigarh is already under construction. Such a responsible and caring human member like you will be very welcome.

**基金会人员**：请您务必考虑一下这个机会。\
**Foundation Member**: Please do consider this opportunity.

基金会人员低下头，翻找手中的资料。\
The Foundation member rummages through the materials in her hand.

**基金会人员**：根据记录，还有一名神秘学家也在此次任务中给予了我方帮助……\
**Foundation Member**: According to the record, there's one more arcanist who also provided help for us in this mission.

**基金会人员**：请问，伽菈波那小姐……她现在在哪里？\
**Foundation Member**: So, where is Ms. Kaalaa Baunaa?

**夏尔贾老师**：噢，她在……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Oh, she's ...

夏尔贾回过头，发现连坎吉拉也不见了身影。\
Sherjah turns around. Kanjira is gone too.

**夏尔贾老师**：奇怪……\
**Ms. Sherjah**: That's weird.

**夏尔贾老师**：……啊！\
**Ms. Sherjah**: Oh!

夏尔贾想起了什么。\
She suddenly realizes something.

**夏尔贾老师**：我想现在……她可能不太方便。\
**Ms. Sherjah**: I think it's not a good time for her.

**基金会人员**：……？\
**Foundation Member**: ...?

**夏尔贾老师**：等流星雨结束，他们就会回来的。\
**Ms. Sherjah**: They will be back after the meteor shower.

**伽菈波那**：♪～\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: ♪

**坎吉拉**：啊！是流星雨！果然和新闻里说的一样大！\
**Kanjira**: Ah! Meteor shower! So many of they as the news mention!

**坎吉拉**：唔……我要许愿去学校之后，每天都能吃饱！\
**Kanjira**: Hmm. I wish I can have my stomach full every day when I go school!

**玛蒂尔达**：让我成为调查员吧，哪怕只有一次也好……！\
**Matilda**: Let me be an investigator, even for once!

**鬃毛沙砾**：好啦，别那么贪心，许一个就好了……\
**Shamane**: Alright, people, don't be greedy! One wish only!

**伽菈波那**：<再见，库玛尔。>\
**Kaalaa Baunaa**: Goodbye, Kumar.
